### [1] [A phenomenological multiscale framework for orientational interactions and viscoelasticity in migrating epithelial monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15975)
*Ivana Pajic-Lijakovic,Milan Milivojevic,Peter V. E. McClintock*

Main category: q-bio.CB

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个现象学力学生物学框架（phenomenological mechanobiological framework），通过区分可逆与不可逆的细胞碰撞（collision）机制，将细胞尺度的定向相互作用（orientational interactions）与组织尺度的力学行为联系起来，阐明了能量储存与耗散之间的平衡如何调控上皮单层（epithelial monolayer）的集体迁移、堵塞转变（jamming transition）及活细胞挤出（live cell extrusion）等过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 上皮单层的集体迁移源于力学相互作用与生化信号之间的耦合，但现有的理论框架缺乏对细胞碰撞（collision）过程中定向相互作用（orientational interactions）的定量描述，尤其是可逆与不可逆碰撞在组织力学中各自的角色尚不清晰。

Method: 本文提出了一个现象学力学生物学框架（phenomenological mechanobiological framework），区分了正面碰撞（head-on collisions）与侧面碰撞（glancing collisions）的可逆与不可逆类型；利用定向相互作用势（orientational interaction potentials）、有效第二维里系数（effective second virial coefficient）及无量纲化的储存与耗散定向能量（stored and dissipated orientational energy）来量化这些效应。

Result: 可逆碰撞储存定向力学能量并保持碰撞几何结构，不可逆碰撞则耗散能量并改变细胞取向。能量储存与耗散的平衡调控集体迁移、力学反馈以及依赖密度的过程（如细胞堵塞与活细胞挤出）。这些机制在细胞堆积密度（cell packing density）升高时贡献增大，在接近堵塞转变（jamming transition）时占主导。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了从碰撞诱导的定向动力学（collision-induced orientation dynamics）到上皮流变学（epithelial rheology）的构成本构解释，表明密度依赖的相互作用模式塑造了集体迁移与组织粘弹性（tissue viscoelasticity）。

Abstract: Collective migration of epithelial monolayers emerges from the interplay between mechanical interactions and biochemical signalling. Here, we present a phenomenological mechanobiological framework linking cell-scale orientational interactions to tissue-scale mechanics. We distinguish reversible and irreversible head-on and glancing collisions, showing that reversible interactions store orientational mechanical energy while preserving collision geometry, whereas irreversible interactions dissipate energy and alter cell orientation. The balance between energy storage and dissipation governs collective migration, mechanical feedback, and density-dependent processes including cell jamming and live cell extrusion. These interactions regulate cell elasticity, contractility, and adhesion, thereby modifying epithelial surface tension and the effective viscoelastic response of the monolayer. We quantify these effects using orientational interaction potentials, an effective second virial coefficient, and dimensionless measures of stored and dissipated orientational energy. The relative contribution of these mechanisms increases with cell packing density, becoming dominant near the jamming transition. This framework provides a constitutive interpretation connecting collision-induced orientation dynamics with emergent epithelial rheology and suggests how density-dependent interaction regimes shape collective migration and tissue viscoelasticity.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.CO'></div>

# astro-ph.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Searching for Folded Primordial Non-Gaussianity with Galaxy Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15337)
*Si-Xiang Yang,Oliver H. E. Philcox*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究星系巡天能否探测折叠型原初非高斯性（folded PNG），系统分析了截断调控和耗散调控两类折叠PNG模型，利用有效场论框架计算红移空间星系功率谱和双谱的贡献，并通过Fisher预测量化约束能力，发现星系双谱是主要探测手段，且可探测性取决于折叠增强区域的宽度与形态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大尺度结构通过原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity, PNG）为暴胀物理提供重要探针，但以往研究主要关注局域型（local）、等边型（equilateral）和正交型（orthogonal）PNG，而折叠型（folded）PNG在星系巡天中的可探测性尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统评估折叠PNG的探测前景。

Method: 考虑激发初态（excited initial states）、虚声速（imaginary speeds of sound）和耗散暴胀（dissipative inflation）三类折叠PNG模型，将其分为截断调控（cutoff-regulated）和耗散调控（dissipation-regulated）两类。利用有效场论大尺度结构（EFTofLSS）框架，开发数值管道计算红移空间星系功率谱多极矩（multipoles）和双谱单极矩（bispectrum monopole）中的PNG贡献，并使用Fisher预测量化约束能力。

Result: 折叠PNG的约束力主要来自星系双谱。截断调控模型中，扰动参数边缘化（nuisance parameter marginalization）仅造成轻微信息损失；有限傅里叶空间分箱（binning）在折叠区域窄于箱宽时会显著削弱约束。耗散调控模型中，指数级窄的折叠增强难以分辨，可观测信号来自模板更宽的支撑区域，导致分箱依赖弱但与等边模板重叠更大。

Conclusion: 折叠PNG是星系双谱分析中独特且有前景的探测目标，其可探测性取决于折叠增强的宽度和形态。本文开发的数值管道具有通用性，可用于研究更广泛类别的不可分离原初双谱（non-separable primordial bispectra）。

Abstract: Large-scale structure provides a powerful probe of inflationary physics through primordial non-Gaussianity (PNG): the galaxy power spectrum depends on local PNG through scale-dependent bias, while the galaxy bispectrum depends sensitively on both equilateral and orthogonal PNG. In this paper, we study whether galaxy surveys can also probe folded PNG, whose shape is enhanced near $k_1+k_2-k_3\rightarrow0$. We consider three inflationary models with folded PNG, including excited initial states, imaginary speeds of sound, and dissipative inflation. These models fall into two classes: cutoff-regulated cases in which the folded-enhanced region has a power-law width, and dissipation-regulated cases in which the enhanced region is exponentially narrow. We develop a numerical pipeline for computing the corresponding PNG contributions to the redshift-space galaxy power spectrum multipoles and bispectrum monopole within the EFTofLSS. Using Fisher forecasts, we show that most of the constraining power on folded PNG comes from the galaxy bispectrum. For the cutoff-regulated models, nuisance parameter marginalization causes only a mild loss of information at large folded enhancement, but finite Fourier-space binning degrades constraints once the folded region becomes narrower than the bin width. For the dissipation-regulated models, the exponentially narrow folded enhancement is hard to resolve and the observable signal instead comes from the broader support of the template, leading to weaker binning dependence but larger overlap with the equilateral template. Our results show that folded PNG is a distinctive and promising target for galaxy bispectrum analyses, and the detectability depends on the width and morphology of the folded enhancement. The numerical pipeline developed in this work is general and can be used to study a wide class of non-separable primordial bispectra.

</details>


### [3] [Tunnelling out of Starobinsky inflation: Raising the spectral tilt](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15354)
*Jose A. R. Cembranos,Jesús Luque,Javier Rubio*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 提出一种混合型Starobinsky暴胀实现方式，通过真空衰变（vacuum decay）以一级相变（first-order phase transition）提前结束暴胀，从而将标量谱指数（scalar spectral tilt $n_s$）提升至与ACT等最新宇宙微波背景（CMB）观测数据一致的高值区域，同时产生可探测的随机引力波遗迹（stochastic gravitational-wave relic）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Starobinsky暴胀在预测标量谱指数$n_s$时偏向较低值，而近期ACT（Atacama Cosmology Telescope）等联合观测数据倾向于更高的$n_s$区域，因此需要一种机制在保留Starobinsky暴胀特征性小张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）的同时提升$n_s$。

Method: 构建一个有效双场系统（effective two-field system），包含一个亚稳态（metastable）的假Starobinsky分支（false branch）和一个真实分支（true branch）。暴胀子在可观測阶段沿假支缓慢滚动（slow-roll），直到沿正交方向的一级相变将系统连接至真支，暴胀由此突然终止，从而跳过原Starobinsky轨迹的末段。

Result: 该机制使宇宙微波背景枢轴尺度（pivot scale）在假支上离开哈勃半径（Hubble radius）的位置比标准Starobinsky暴胀更远离势能极小值，从而提升标量谱指数$n_s$，同时保持低张量-标量比。真空相变还会产生随机引力波遗迹，其峰值频率由隧穿时标（tunnelling timescale）和后续再加热历史（reheating history）控制。

Conclusion: 该混合模型为将Starobinsky暴胀的$n_s$预测移至与ACT相关观测吻合的高值区域提供了一种简洁方案，并预言了可通过引力波探测加以检验的随机背景信号。

Abstract: We propose a hybrid realization of Starobinsky inflation in which the inflationary epoch ends through vacuum decay. The model consists of an effective two-field system with a metastable Starobinsky branch shifted with respect to the true one. During the observable stage, the inflaton slow-rolls along the false branch, until a first-order phase transition in an orthogonal direction connects it to the true branch and ends inflation abruptly. This old-inflation-like exit skips the last part of the would-be Starobinsky trajectory. As a result, the Cosmic Microwave Background pivot scale exits the Hubble radius further from the minimum of the false branch than in ordinary Starobinsky inflation, raising the scalar spectral tilt $n_s$ while preserving the characteristic small tensor-to-scalar ratio. This provides a simple way of moving Starobinsky inflation towards the high-$n_s$ region favoured by recent ACT-related combinations. The same vacuum transition leaves a stochastic gravitational-wave relic whose peak frequency is controlled by the tunnelling timescale and the subsequent reheating history.

</details>


### [4] [Constraining primordial non-Gaussianity and parity-violation through Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves with next-generation ground-based interferometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16162)
*Ilaria Caporali,H. V. Ragavendra,Angelo Ricciardone,Nicola Bartolo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了利用第三代引力波探测器（如Einstein Telescope和Cosmic Explorer），通过标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）探测原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）及其宇称对称性。作者构建了包含双谱（bispectrum）和三谱（trispectrum）贡献的能谱框架，发现三谱中的宇称奇分量会在随机引力波背景（SGWB）中诱导圆极化（circular polarization），从而直接探测原初宇称破缺。即便加入天体物理前景（astrophysical foreground），仍可有效约束相关宇宙学与天体物理参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用第三代引力波探测器探测原初非高斯性及相关宇称对称性的可能性。原初非高斯性中的宇称奇分量（三谱）可诱导随机引力波背景的圆极化，为探测原初宇称破缺提供直接途径。

Method: 构建了一个理论框架，将标量非高斯性（由双谱和三谱量化）对引力波能谱密度（energy density spectrum）的贡献纳入考虑；使用Einstein Telescope和Cosmic Explorer的模拟数据进行参数推断（parameter inference）；并引入天体物理贡献作为SIGWs的前景（foreground）进行分析。

Result: 未来第三代干涉仪可对宇称奇标量三谱、双谱以及宇称偶三谱施加有竞争力的约束。即便存在天体物理前景，仍能有效约束与SIGW相关的宇宙学参数及天体物理参数。

Conclusion: 标量诱导引力波有望成为探测原初非高斯性和宇称破缺的有效工具；第三代引力波探测器具备同时约束宇宙学参数与天体物理前景参数的能力。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the prospects for probing primordial non-Gaussianity and associated symmetry of parity through scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs), with third-generation gravitational-wave detectors. We develop a framework that accounts for contributions to the energy density spectrum of GWs arising from the scalar non-Gaussianity quantified by bispectrum and trispectrum, and perform parameter inference using simulated data from Einstein Telescope and Cosmic Explorer. The parity-odd component of the scalar trispectrum induces circular polarization in the stochastic gravitational-wave background (SGWB), providing a direct probe of parity-violation in the primordial Universe. We show that future interferometers can place competitive constraints on the parity-odd scalar trispectrum, along with the bispectrum and parity-even trispectrum. Moreover, we include the astrophysical contribution, which could act as a foreground for the SIGWs. We show that, despite the addition of such a foreground, we are still able to effectively constrain the cosmological parameters related to SIGWs and the astrophysical parameters as well.

</details>


### [5] [Cosmological Evidence for Dark Axion-Dark Baryon Interactions from Apparent Phantom Crossing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16191)
*Justin Khoury,Meng-Xiang Lin,Mark Trodden*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过对比暗物质-暗能量相互作用模型（暗轴子-暗重子耦合）与DESI DR2 BAO、CMB和Ia型超新星的联合观测数据，发现最优拟合相比ΛCDM模型改善Δχ²=-14.48，模型表现出非单调暗物质质量演化及幻影穿越（phantom crossing）行为，但在数据偏好区域其早期暗能量（Early Dark Energy）组分太小，不足以显著缓解哈勃常数（H₀）张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在前期工作提出的暗轴子（dark axion）与暗重子（dark baryon）耦合的强耦合暗扇区（strongly coupled dark sector）模型基础上，进一步利用最新宇宙学观测数据（CMB、DESI DR2 BAO、SNe Ia）对该模型进行严格检验，以评估其在解释暗能量-暗物质相互作用及幻影穿越现象方面的可行性。

Method: 将暗轴子-暗重子相互作用模型植入玻尔兹曼码（Boltzmann code）中，并分别与CMB数据、DESI DR2重子声学振荡（BAO）数据以及Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）数据进行联合比对。

Result: 对于CMB+DESI DR2+DES-Dovekie数据组合，最优拟合相比ΛCDM模型改善Δχ²=-14.48；模型表现出暗物质质量的非单调演化——在物质-辐射等值期（matter-radiation equality）到再复合时期（recombination）质量下降，在BAO/SNe敏感时期质量上升，从而在有效暗能量描述中出现幻影穿越；该动力学在物质-辐射等值期附近产生类似早期暗能量（Early Dark Energy）的能量注入，但在数据偏好区域该组分过小，不足以显著提高H₀以缓解当前的哈勃常数张力。

Conclusion: 暗轴子-暗重子相互作用模型在拟合最新宇宙学数据方面优于ΛCDM，其非单调暗物质质量演化可自然导致幻影穿越行为，但模型产生的早期暗能量效应不足以充分解决哈勃常数张力问题。

Abstract: Interactions between dark matter and dark energy can lead to an apparent phantom-crossing behavior that mimics the expansion history preferred by the latest cosmological observations from DESI baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB), and Type Ia supernovae (SNe Ia) data. In a previous paper [Khoury, Lin, and Trodden 2025 arXiv:2503.16415], we proposed a concrete particle physics realization of this idea, consisting of a strongly coupled dark sector in which a dark axion is coupled to dark baryons. In this paper, we investigate this idea further by comparing its predictions to the latest cosmological data. We implement the dark axion-dark baryon interaction model in a Boltzmann code and confront it with CMB, DESI DR2 BAO, and SNe Ia data. For the CMB+DESI DR2+DES-Dovekie combination, the best-fit model improves the fit relative to $Λ$CDM by $Δχ^2=-14.48$. The preferred solution exhibits a non-monotonic dark-matter mass evolution: the mass decreases between matter-radiation equality and recombination, while increasing over the BAO/SNe-sensitive epoch, leading to an apparent phantom crossing in an effective dark-energy description. Interestingly, the same dynamics produces an Early Dark Energy-like energy injection near matter-radiation equality, but in the data-preferred region this component is too small to raise $H_0$ enough to substantially reduce the current tension.

</details>

### [6] [Nanoscale stray fields from micromagnets for optimal spin qubit architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15333)
*Sandrine Lopes,Quentin Schaeverbeke,Matthieu M. Desjardins,Daniel Lacour,Michel Hehn,François Montaigne*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过NV色心磁测量技术在非饱和磁化状态下对Co、Co/Ta多层膜及CoFe薄膜进行表征，建立可靠的微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）框架，预测CoFe微磁体在双量子点结构中产生超过±100 mT的反对称场（antisymmetric field），并实现自旋-光子耦合强度|g_s/g_c| ≈ 0.5，展示了在电路量子电动力学（circuit QED）架构中实现高保真度操作的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 片上微磁体（on-chip micromagnet）产生的局域磁场不对称性可实现自旋量子比特（spin qubit）的电学控制及其与电路量子电动力学（circuit QED）架构的集成，但准确预测自旋量子比特性能需要超越饱和磁化近似（saturated-magnet approximation），考虑非均匀磁化（nonuniform magnetization）的微磁建模。

Method: 结合薄膜表征（thin-film characterization）与NV色心磁测量（NV-center magnetometry）技术，在非饱和磁化（unsaturated regime）条件下对Co、Co/Ta多层膜及CoFe薄膜进行纳米尺度杂散场测量，以此建立可靠的微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）框架。

Result: CoFe微磁体在双量子点（double quantum-dot）结构中产生超过±100 mT的反对称场（antisymmetric field），这归因于其高饱和磁化强度（saturation magnetization）和有利的磁晶各向异性（magnetocrystalline anisotropy）。对于耦合到微波谐振器的自旋量子比特，预测的自旋-光子耦合强度达|g_s/g_c| ≈ 0.5，其中g_c表示底层电荷量子比特（charge qubit）的电荷-光子耦合强度。

Conclusion: 所建立的微磁模拟框架能够准确预测微磁体杂散场，CoFe微磁体具有在电路QED（circuit QED）架构中实现高保真度自旋量子比特操作的潜力。

Abstract: On-chip micromagnets generate local magnetic-field asymmetries, enabling electrical control of spin qubits via electric dipole spin resonance and their integration into circuit quantum electrodynamics (QED) architectures. Accurate prediction of spin-qubit performance requires modeling micromagnet stray fields beyond the saturated-magnet approximation, accounting for nonuniform magnetization. Here, we combine thin-film characterization of Co, Co/Ta multilayers, and CoFe films with nanoscale stray-field measurements using NV-center magnetometry in the unsaturated regime to establish a reliable micromagnetic simulation framework. We show that CoFe micromagnets generate antisymmetric fields in double quantum-dot geometries exceeding +/- 100mT, owing to their high saturation magnetization and favorable magnetocrystalline anisotropy. For spin qubits coupled to microwave resonators, the predicted spin-photon coupling reaches $\left| g_s/g_c \right| \approx 0.5$, where $g_c$ denotes the charge-photon coupling strength of the underlying charge qubit, highlighting the potential for high-fidelity operations in circuit QED architectures.

</details>


### [7] [Dynamical Polarization from Hidden Spin and Orbital Textures in p-Wave Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15353)
*Yantao Li,Jacob Linder,Pavlo Sukhachov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，在光驱动的 p 波磁体中，微运动（micromotion）会揭示出周期平均（period-averaged）描述所无法捕捉的隐藏净自旋极化（net spin polarization）以及由能带间量子几何（interband quantum geometry）驱动的轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum），从而确立 p 波磁体作为共振交流自旋极化与整流直流轨道极化之源的独特地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期平均描述常常遗漏驱动量子物质（driven quantum matter）的关键特征；作者旨在揭示光驱动 p 波磁体中隐藏的自旋极化与轨道角动量，这些效应在平衡态（equilibrium）和周期平均描述中均不可见。

Method: 通过分析光学驱动 p 波磁体（p-wave magnet）中的微运动（micromotion），研究驱动频率下场致自旋极化与轨道角动量的产生与增强机制，并区分线性响应（linear response）与非线性整流（nonlinear rectification）下的不同对称性行为。

Result: 隐藏的净自旋极化在驱动频率下振荡，并在由非相对论交换劈裂（nonrelativistic exchange splitting）设定的带间能隙处发生共振增强；驱动还激活了由能带间量子几何（interband quantum geometry）调控的轨道角动量，其线性响应保持动量奇宇称（momentum-odd），而非线性整流则产生静态、动量偶宇称（momentum-even）的轨道极化。

Conclusion: p 波磁体可产生共振交流自旋极化（resonant ac spin polarization）与整流直流轨道极化（rectified dc orbital polarization），这些效应在周期平均处理中完全不可见，从而拓展了对驱动量子物质中非平衡自旋与轨道现象的理解。

Abstract: Period-averaged descriptions often miss essential features of driven quantum matter. We show that the micromotion of an optically driven $p$-wave magnet unveils a hidden net spin polarization, absent from both the equilibrium and period-averaged spin textures, which remain odd in momentum. This spin polarization oscillates at the drive frequency and is resonantly enhanced at the interband gap set by nonrelativistic exchange splitting. The drive further activates an orbital angular momentum governed by interband quantum geometry. While its linear response remains momentum-odd, nonlinear rectification yields a static, momentum-even orbital polarization for suitably oriented driving fields. These results establish $p$-wave magnets as a source of resonant ac spin and rectified dc orbital polarization: effects invisible to any period-averaged treatment.

</details>


### [8] [Hot-Carrier Distribution Spectroscopy by Transconductance in Two-Dimensional Field-Effect Transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15578)
*Katsunori Wakabayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明场效应晶体管（field-effect transistor, FET）的跨导 $g_m$ 并非载流子密度的简单代理，而是一种对载流子分布函数形状敏感的能谱探针，并在此基础上发展了一套基于直流/锁相跨导测量的全电子学稳态载流子分布函数光谱技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将FET的跨导 $g_m$ 仅解读为载流子密度的代理，忽略了其对分布函数形状的敏感性。本文旨在揭示 $g_m$ 的能谱学内涵，并利用其发展一种无需光学读出的载流子分布函数光谱方法。

Method: 建立了二维FET的能分辨输运框架；在栅压无关的谱核（spectral kernel）近似下，将 $g_m$ 分解为密度调制项 $g_m^{(n)}$ 和分布形状驱动项 $g_m^{(α)}$；$g_m^{(α)}$ 作为测量 $g_m$ 减去平滑密度调制背景后的残差，在特定栅压 $V_G^{\rm pk}$ 处呈现特征反常峰。

Result: 反常峰在平衡输运中不存在，且无法仅用载流子密度调制解释。通过校准谱核，可从标准直流/锁相 $g_m$ 扫描中提取热载流子能量 $E_0$、谱宽 $σ$ 和产生阈值 $n_c$。时间分辨扩展可进一步恢复载流子弛豫时间 $τ$。

Conclusion: 二维FET可作为一种全电学的分布函数光谱仪（distribution-function spectrometer），无需光学读出即可实现稳态载流子分布函数的光谱表征。

Abstract: The transconductance $g_m = dI_D/dV_G$ of a field-effect transistor (FET) is conventionally read as a proxy for carrier density. We show that it is instead a spectroscopic probe of the carrier distribution: because $g_m$ weights the spectral current $j(E)$ by the gate-voltage derivative $\partial f(E)/\partial V_G$ and integrates over energy, it is sensitive to the \emph{shape} of $f(E)$, not merely its integrated weight $n$. We develop an energy-resolved transport framework for two-dimensional (2D) FETs and, within a gate-independent spectral-kernel approximation, derive the decomposition $g_m = g_m^{(n)} + g_m^{(α)}$ into the conventional density-modulation term $g_m^{(n)}$ and a distribution-shape-driven term $g_m^{(α)}$. The latter, obtained as the residual after subtracting the smooth density-modulation background from the measured $g_m$, exhibits a characteristic anomalous peak at a gate voltage $V_G^{\rm pk}$. This peak has no counterpart in equilibrium transport and \emph{cannot be explained by carrier density modulation alone}. With the spectral kernel calibrated, the peak position and height -- extracted from standard DC/lock-in $g_m$ sweeps -- constrain the hot-carrier energy $E_0$, spectral width $σ$, and generation threshold $n_c$, realizing a steady-state, all-electrical spectroscopy of the carrier distribution. An optional time-resolved extension further recovers the carrier relaxation time $τ$ from the transient response following a pump excitation, establishing the 2D FET as a distribution-function spectrometer that requires no optical readout.

</details>


### [9] [Long range spatial correlations in the periodically driven transverse field Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15665)
*Lazar Paroski,Ivan Iorsh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究周期驱动的横向场伊辛模型（transverse field Ising model）中激发之间关联的长时间行为，发现最长的关联长度由基布尔-祖雷克机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism）类比的拓扑缺陷与弗洛凯共振（Floquet resonance）诱导的拓扑缺陷之间的干涉决定，且通过调节驱动周期可使关联长度任意增大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解周期驱动自旋链中激发之间关联的长时间行为，特别是关联长度的决定因素与可控性。

Method: 基于可积的（integrable）周期驱动横向场伊辛模型，分析长时间极限下自旋链中激发关联的关联长度，重点关注基布尔-祖雷克机制类比与弗洛凯共振诱导的拓扑缺陷之间的干涉效应。

Result: 最长关联长度由基布尔-祖雷克机制类比的拓扑缺陷与弗洛凯共振诱导的拓扑缺陷之间的干涉决定；尽管系统可积导致关联长度有限，但通过调节驱动周期可使该关联长度任意增大。

Conclusion: 在可积的周期驱动系统中，关联长度可通过驱动周期进行有效调控，为控制量子关联性质提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: We consider a periodically driven transverse field Ising model and study the long-time behavior of the correlations between the excitations in the spin chain. We show that the longest correlation length is defined by the interference between the topological defects induced by the analog of the Kibble-Zurek mechanism and those induced by the Floquet resonance. We show that although the correlations always have a finite correlation length since the system is integrable, the correlation length can be made arbitrarily large by tuning the drive period.

### [10] [Strong intervalley mixing between copropagating quantum Hall edge channels in a silicon MOSFET](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15675)
*Gento Yamahata,Takase Shimizu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验证明在硅基量子霍尔边缘态中，通过侧栅调控可实现谷间耦合接近1/2的等效分束器操作，为构建紧凑型硅量子霍尔干涉仪奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共传播量子霍尔边缘通道（copropagating quantum Hall edge channels）是实现紧凑型电子干涉仪和飞行量子态的 promising 平台。硅中自旋翻转散射被弱自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit interaction）强烈抑制，因此谷自由度（valley degree of freedom）为自旋分辨边缘通道提供了天然替代方案。研究旨在探索硅中谷边缘通道间的通道间跃迁（interchannel transitions）。

Method: 实验在双层栅极硅金属-氧化物-半导体场效应晶体管（double-layer-gated silicon metal-oxide-semiconductor field-effect transistor）中进行。体填充因子（bulk filling factor）设为 ν=2，使两个自旋极化的谷边缘通道在耗尽侧栅附近紧密靠近，测量其间通道间跃迁概率。

Result: 观察到强烈的谷间混合（intervalley mixing），跃迁概率接近1/2，表明两个谷边缘通道达到几乎完全的均衡化（equilibration）。相比之下，不同自旋取向的边缘通道间传输的跃迁概率可忽略不计，与硅中自旋翻转散射被抑制的预期一致。

Conclusion: 结果表明，Si/SiO₂界面的谷间耦合（intervalley coupling）可以为共传播谷边缘通道提供类似分束器（beam-splitter-like）的操作，建立起通往紧凑型硅量子霍尔干涉仪（silicon quantum Hall interferometers）的关键构建模块。

Abstract: Copropagating quantum Hall edge channels provide a promising platform for compact electron interferometry and flying quantum states. In silicon, the valley degree of freedom offers a natural alternative to spin-resolved edge channels because spin-flip scattering is strongly suppressed by the weak spin-orbit interaction. Here, we investigate interchannel transitions between copropagating valley edge channels in a double-layer-gated silicon metal-oxide-semiconductor field-effect transistor. With the bulk filling factor set to $ν=2$, two spin-polarized valley edge channels are brought into close proximity near a depleted side gate. We observe strong intervalley mixing, with a transition probability close to 1/2, indicating nearly complete equilibration between the two valley edge channels. In contrast, interchannel transport between edge channels with different spin orientations shows negligible transition probability, consistent with suppressed spin-flip scattering in silicon. These results demonstrate that intervalley coupling at a Si/SiO$_2$ interface can provide a beam-splitter-like operation for copropagating valley edge channels, establishing a key building block toward compact silicon quantum Hall interferometers.

### [11] [Drift-Induced Nonreciprocal Hyperbolic Polaritons in Graphene/$α$-MoO$_3$ Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15722)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在石墨烯/α-MoO₃/SiC异质结构中施加直流电流，利用电流诱导的波矢依赖多普勒频移（Doppler shift）打破互易性；同时利用石墨烯等离激元（plasmon）与α-MoO₃中双曲声子极化激元（hyperbolic phonon polariton）的杂化以及SiC衬底的调控，实现等频轮廓（isofrequency contour）的栅压可调转变。

Result: 在费米速度5%的漂移速度下，系统展现出显著的动量依赖非互易性，对比度（contrast）达到约0.3，而垂直于漂移方向的方向由于对称性约束不受影响。实空间计算证实动量空间的不对称性可转化为定向的近场强度调制。

Conclusion: 电流偏置的范德瓦尔斯异质结构可作为电可调、无磁中红外非互易纳米光子学的平台。

Abstract: Achieving optical isolation requires breaking symmetry between forward- and backward-propagating light, a long-standing challenge at the nanoscale in the absence of magnetic fields. Here we theoretically demonstrate electrically tunable nonreciprocal phonon-plasmon polaritons in a graphene/$α$-MoO$_3$/SiC heterostructure operating in the mid-infrared. A dc current in graphene induces a wavevector-dependent Doppler shift that breaks reciprocity and generates strong directional asymmetry in hybrid plasmon-phonon propagation. In the reciprocal regime, hybridization between graphene plasmons and hyperbolic phonon polaritons in $α$-MoO$_3$, further shaped by the SiC substrate, enables gate-controlled transitions of isofrequency contours, including canalization along orthogonal crystal axes. At drift velocities of 5% of the Fermi velocity, the system exhibits pronounced momentum-dependent nonreciprocity with contrast reaching $\sim$ 0.3, while directions orthogonal to the drift remain unaffected due to symmetry imposed constraints. Real-space calculations confirm that this momentum-space asymmetry translates into directional near-field intensity modulation. These results establish current-biased van der Waals heterostructures as a platform for electrically tunable, magnet-free nonreciprocal nanophotonics in the mid-infrared.

Method: 实验上构建了基于碳纳米管的安德烈夫分子，即两个耦合的量子点约瑟夫森结（quantum-dot Josephson junctions）；同时引入最小理论模型（minimal theoretical model）对实验结果进行支撑和解释。

Abstract: Fermion parity is a fundamental property of superconducting many-body states. Here, we show that the global fermion parity of a delocalized superconducting state can be detected locally by exploiting the nonlocal Josephson effect. We further show that changes in the molecular ground-state parity manifest as characteristic $π$-phase shifts in the nonlocal response. Supported by a minimal theoretical model, these results identify global fermion parity as an experimentally accessible degree of freedom in hybrid superconducting circuits that can be readily revealed through the nonlocal Josephson effect.

### [13] [Electrothermal control of spin-reorientation transition in Co/Fe_3GaTe_2 heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15844)

Abstract: Electrical control of magnetic anisotropy in van der Waals (vdWs) magnets is a key step toward reconfigurable two-dimensional spintronics, yet how a conventional metallic ferromagnet competes with a van der Waals magnet across a direct interface has remained largely unexplored. Here we demonstrate reversible thermal and electrothermal control of a spin-reorientation transition in Co/Fe_3GaTe_2 (FGaT) heterostructures. In a Co-free FGaT device, Kerr microscopy traces the switching to a power-tunable domain nucleation barrier and demonstrates power-thresholded, field-assisted magnetization reversal at a threshold near 15 mW. Abstract: Photoelectrical readout of the electronic spin state of the nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center in diamond is attracting significant interest due to the numerous advantages it possesses compared with conventional fluorescence readout. ### [15] [Disentangling topological and anomalous Hall contributions of skyrmions using Kerr microscopy and thermal transport measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15946)

TL;DR: 本文通过在 Ta/CoFeB/MgO 单层厚膜中测量拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect），证实了拓扑保护斯格明子（skyrmion）的存在，并利用磁光克尔显微镜（Magneto-optical Kerr microscopy）将拓扑霍尔效应从主导的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）中分离，最终在室温下测得拓扑霍尔电阻率为 249(18) pΩ·m。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑霍尔效应是探测拓扑保护磁结构（如斯格明子）的重要工具，但在 Ta/CoFeB/MgO 单层薄膜体系中，拓扑霍尔效应信号微弱且与占主导的反常霍尔效应重叠，直接检测面临挑战，因此需要有效的方法将二者分离。

Method: 采用电子输运测量获取霍尔效应信号，同时结合磁光克尔显微镜（MOKE）对表面磁化进行成像，从而将拓扑霍尔效应与其他霍尔效应贡献分离；进一步通过 MOKE 跟踪外磁场扫描过程中斯格明子的形成，并利用热输运和电输运测量计算拓扑量，分别验证拓扑能斯特效应（topological Nernst effect）和拓扑霍尔效应。

Result: 在室温下，Ta/CoFeB/MgO 层堆叠的拓扑霍尔电阻率为 249(18) pΩ·m；MOKE 测量证实了斯格明子在磁场扫描过程中的形成，并与拓扑霍尔效应测量结果一致。

Conclusion: 通过结合磁光成像和输运测量，成功实现了在单层薄膜体系中拓扑霍尔效应的分离与确认，证明了该材料系统在室温下确实存在拓扑保护的斯格明子结构。

Abstract: The topological Hall effect is a valuable tool to indicate the presence of topologically protected magnetic structures. In this work, we present topological Hall effect measurements originating from topologically protected skyrmions in Ta/CoFeB/MgO single-layer thick films with a one nanometer thick magnetic layer. The simultaneous occurrence of the small topological Hall effect and the dominating anomalous Hall effect in this material system makes direct detection challenging as compared to bulk or multilayer systems. In electronic transport measurements, both effects' contributions impact electron trajectories in the same way, overlapping in the measurement signal, and require disentanglement. Magneto-optical Kerr microscopy was used to image the surface magnetization, enabling the separation of the topological Hall effect from other Hall effect contributions. These measurements reveal a topological Hall resistivity of $249(18)\,$\si{\pico\ohm\meter} for Ta/CoFeB/MgO layer stacks at room temperature. Magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) measurements also allow tracking skyrmion formation during external magnetic field sweeps to confirm their occurrence when measuring the topological Hall effect. We verify this outcome by comparing the results with thermal and electrical transport measurements from which we calculate the overall topological quantity that gives rise to the topological Nernst and Hall effect, respectively.

</details>


### [16] [Phase-controlled quasi-bound states in the continuum and thermoelectric enhancement in Majorana-quantum-dot nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15990)
*Alejandro Garrido,David Zambrano,Hishan Farfán-Bachiloglu,Juan Pablo Ramos-Andrade,Vladimir Juričić,Pedro Orellana*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了马约拉纳零模（MZMs）与连续谱中的束缚态（BICs）如何共同调控十字形量子点（QD）系统的热电响应，发现通过超导相位控制（superconducting-phase control）可实现高达约0.75的电子热电优值（ZT_{el}），并揭示一个普适的低温度值ZT^{max}_{el} ≃ 0.755和洛伦兹数比ℒ/ℒ₀ = 21/5源自二次传输零点（quadratic transmission zero）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索马约拉纳零模（MZMs）与连续谱中的束缚态（BICs）之间的相互作用如何影响电子热电响应，并寻找通过相位调控等手段高效提升拓扑杂化纳米结构热电性能的途径。

Method: 采用格林函数形式论（Green-function formalism）、精确线性响应能量积分以及低温索末菲展开（Sommerfeld expansion）对系统的谱性质和热电性质进行分析。

Result: 对称性破缺将BICs转化为准BICs，使其参与电导和热导并产生有限热电响应。量子点能级失谐可将ZT_{el}提升约一个数量级；而超导相位控制可实现更强的增强，达到ZT_{el} ≃ 0.75，并显著违反Wiedemann-Franz定律。低温下ZT^{max}_{el} ≃ 0.755和ℒ/ℒ₀ = 21/5是二次反共振（quadratic antiresonance）的普适结果。

Conclusion: 超导相位控制可高效调控马约拉纳耦合干涉结构的热电响应，为工程化设计拓扑杂化纳米结构（topological hybrid nanostructures）的电子性质提供有效手段。

Abstract: We investigate how the interplay between Majorana zero modes (MZMs) and bound states in the continuum (BICs) governs the electronic thermoelectric response of a crossbar-shaped quantum dot (QD) coupled to two topological-superconductor nanowires. Using the Green-function formalism, exact linear-response energy integrals, and their low-temperature Sommerfeld expansion, we analyze the spectral and thermoelectric properties of the system. We show that symmetry breaking converts BICs into quasi-BICs, allowing them to contribute to electrical and thermal transport and thereby generate a finite thermoelectric response. While unequal nanowire lengths, reflected in different intra-Majorana coupling strengths, produce only a modest enhancement of $ZT_{el}$, detuning the QD level increases $ZT_{el}$ by approximately one order of magnitude. Superconducting-phase control produces a much stronger enhancement, reaching $ZT_{el} \simeq 0.75$ through a quadratic transmission zero and a pronounced violation of the Wiedemann-Franz law. The low-temperature values $ZT^{max}_{el} \simeq 0.755$ and $\mathscr{L} /\mathscr{L}_{0} = 21/5$ are universal consequences of this quadratic antiresonance. Our results establish phase-tunable thermoelectric signatures of the Majorana-coupled interference structure and identify superconducting-phase control as an efficient means of engineering the electronic response of topological hybrid nanostructures.

</details>


### [17] [Qubit encodings in the p-orbital-valley spectrum for enhanced coherence and tunable two-qubit interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15993)
*John H. Caporaletti,J. P. Kestner*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 提出一种基于量子点中p轨道与谷态耦合的新型量子比特（pOv qubit），利用各向异性调控实现单比特操控，并发现电荷噪声不敏感的工作点（sweet spot），估计去相位时间T₂*约10微秒、品质因子约10⁴；两比特门通过四极-四极库仑相互作用实现，频率可调至约1 GHz，为可扩展量子计算提供新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子比特方案在电荷噪声抑制与可扩展性方面仍面临挑战，尤其是硅基量子点中谷态（valley states）与轨道自由度未被充分利用。本文旨在探索将p轨道与谷态耦合用于构建新型量子比特，以实现更高的相干时间和可调谐的两比特门。

Method: 将量子比特编码在各向异性量子点激发谷的最低p轨道态与基态谷的激发p轨道态构成的二能级子空间中，利用合金无序诱导的谷-轨道耦合（valley-orbit coupling, VOC）产生避免交叉（avoided crossing），通过基带电控调节点各向异性实现单比特完全控制。采用唯象的两能级涨落子（two-level fluctuator, TLF）偶极噪声模型估计去相位时间。两比特门通过四极-四极库仑相互作用（quadrupole-quadrupole Coulomb interaction）实现，通过调节各向异性点的相对取向进行电调谐。

Result: 特定点取向下存在电荷噪声一阶不敏感的“甜点”（sweet spot）。TLF模型估计平均去相位时间T₂*约10 μs，品质因子Q约10⁴。两比特门频率可从零电调至约1 GHz。

Conclusion: pOv qubit结合了p轨道与谷态的优势，在电荷噪声抑制和门可调性方面表现出良好性能，为可扩展硅基量子计算提供了一种新颖且可行的实现路径。

Abstract: We propose encoding a qubit in a two-level subspace spanned by the lowest $p$-orbital state in the excited valley of an anisotropic quantum dot and the excited $p$-orbital in the ground valley, which we dub the $pOv$ qubit. There is an avoided crossing between these states due to valley-orbit coupling (VOC) induced by alloy disorder, enabling complete single-qubit control using baseband electrical control of the dot anisotropy. We find that `sweet spots' exist at specific dot orientations where the instantaneous eigenstates are first-order insensitive to charge noise. Using a phenomenological two-level fluctuator (TLF) dipole noise model, we estimate an average dephasing time of $T_2^*\approx 10\,μ\text{s}$ and a quality factor of $Q\sim 10^4$. Alternatively, encoding in the $p$-orbital states in the ground valley near the isotropic dot point, we show that one can induce a similar sweet spot via an out-of-plane magnetic field. Finally, we find that two-qubit gates for the $pOv$ qubit are mediated by the quadrupole-quadrupole Coulomb interaction and can be electrically tuned from zero to $\sim 1~\text{GHz}$ by adjusting the relative orientation of the anisotropic dots, providing a novel pathway towards scalable quantum computation.

### [18] [Negative quantum friction in nanoscale water flows: the Wigner picture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16011)
*Adriano Tiribocchi,Marco Lauricella,Efthimios Kaxiras,Sauro Succi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于Wigner方程的单粒子模型探索“量子”摩擦现象，数值模拟显示了负量子摩擦（negative quantum friction）的明确特征，即固体壁面电子向流动水分子传递净动量，从而将水摩擦降低多达40%，结果依赖于经典与量子涨落之间的耦合强度。该研究为通过连续动力学理论和基于粒子的模拟来桥接经典与量子描述提供了理论框架前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索“量子”摩擦现象，特别是负量子摩擦（negative quantum friction）的存在性及其物理机制，试图在经典流体动力学与量子描述之间建立理论桥梁。

Method: 采用基于Wigner方程（Wigner equation）的单粒子模型，以模拟固体壁面中电子在约束纳米尺度水流（nanoscale water flows）中的行为，并通过数值模拟分析经典与量子涨落之间的耦合作用。

Result: 数值模拟显示负量子摩擦的明确特征：电子向流动水分子传递净动量，从而显著降低水摩擦，降幅最高达40%，其程度取决于经典与量子涨落之间的耦合强度。

Conclusion: 该研究有望为通过连续动力学理论（continuum kinetic theories）和基于粒子的模拟（particle-based simulations）桥接经典描述与量子描述提供理论框架。

Abstract: We explore the phenomenon of "quantum" friction based on a single-particle model patterned after the Wigner equation describing electrons flow in a solid wall confining nanoscale water flows. The numerical simulations show a clear signature of negative quantum friction, namely a net momentum transfer from the electrons in the solid wall to the flowing water molecules. Such net momentum transfer results into a sizeable reduction of the water friction, up to forty percent, depending on the strength of the coupling between classical and quantum fluctuations. Our results offer the prospect of a theoretical framework bridging classical and quantum description by using continuum kinetic theories and particle-based simulations.

### [19] [Magnons reveal topology and dynamics of a skyrmion crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16023)
*Raphael Ayache,Nilotpal Chakraborty,Manabendra Kuiri,Quentin Benichou,Antonio Lacerda-Santos,Lilian Seyve,Himadri Chakraborti,Leo Pugliese,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Cosimo Gorini,Roderich Moessner,Benoit Doucot,Preden Roulleau*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过设计纳米石墨烯结，在磁子发射器与探测器之间嵌入斯格明子维格纳晶体（skyrmion Wigner crystal），利用磁子输运（magnon transport）作为实空间探针，揭示了该晶体在门电压调控下逐个添加斯格明子时引发的近周期性涨落窗口，从而实现了对拓扑自旋织构非平衡集体动力学的探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管单个斯格明子（skyrmion）是拓扑保护的对象，但其合作形成的晶体有序性很脆弱，易受热涨落或外部扰动破坏。探测此类晶体的内部动力学既具吸引力又充满挑战，因为其精密的自旋织构（spin texture）必须在测量过程中保持稳定。

Method: 研究人员设计了一个纳米尺度的石墨烯结（graphene junction），在其中嵌入一个斯格明子维格纳晶体，并将其置于磁子发射器（magnon emitter）与探测器（detector）之间。通过改变门电压（gate voltage），测量整个样品中磁子计数的涨落模式。

Result: 随着门电压变化，检测到整个样品中出现了近周期性的磁子计数尖锐涨落窗口。这种涨落被解释为斯格明子逐个添加到准一维阵列中的结果：每次涨落爆发对应一个额外斯格明子的进入，在此期间晶格刚度（lattice stiffness）降低。

Conclusion: 研究表明，入射的磁子能够诱导并探测晶体的非平衡集体动力学（non-equilibrium collective dynamics）。该结果建立了通过磁子输运对量子霍尔型（quantum Hall-type）绝缘基态中拓扑自旋织构进行实空间探针的方法，并为探索莫尔（moire）及多层石墨烯系统中关联的拓扑有序相（topologically ordered phases）打开了新的可能性。

Abstract: Although individual skyrmions are topologically protected objects, their cooperative crystalline order is fragile, easily disrupted by thermal fluctuations or other external perturbations. Probing the internal dynamics of such a crystal is both compelling and challenging, as its intricate and delicate spin texture must remain stable during measurement. Here, we engineer a nanoscale graphene junction hosting a skyrmion Wigner crystal, embedded between magnon emitters and detectors. The skyrmion crystal geometry leaves a striking imprint on magnon transport: as the gate voltage is varied, near-periodic windows of sharp fluctuations in magnon count are detected across the entire sample. We develop an interpretation that this results from skyrmions being added one by one to a quasi-one-dimensional array. Each burst of the fluctuations thus corresponds to the entry of an additional skyrmion, during which the lattice stiffness reduces. The impinging magnons induce and act as a probe of non-equilibrium collective dynamics of the crystal. These results establish a real-space probe of topological spin textures in quantum Hall-type insulating ground states via magnon transport and open opportunities to explore correlated, topologically ordered phases in moire and multilayer graphene systems.

### [20] [Excitonic structure in CsPbBr$_3$ nanocubes, nanorods and nanoplatelets: the effect of dimensionality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16142)
*Jose L. Movilla,Josep Planelles,Juan I. Climente*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过变分有效质量模型（variational effective mass model）统一描述了 CsPbBr₃ 纳米晶在不同维度（纳米棒 1D、纳米片 2D、纳米立方体 3D）下的激子（exciton, X）基态性质，揭示了量子限域、介电限域、电子-空穴关联及极化子效应对激子束缚能、超辐射（superradiance）和辐射复合速率的调控机制，并发现双激子（biexciton, XX）几何构型在所有维度下均为扭曲四面体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 比较不同维度 CsPbBr₃ 纳米晶（纳米棒、纳米片、纳米立方体）的激子基态性质，阐明量子限域（quantum confinement）、介电限域（dielectric confinement）和各向异性几何对激子行为的影响机制。

Method: 采用统一的变分有效质量模型（variational effective mass model），在同等理论基础上同时描述三种维度体系，模型中包含了量子限域、介电限域、电子-空穴关联以及基于 Haken 模型的极化子效应（polaronic effects）。

Result: 强限域方向压缩激子波函数并增强弱限域方向的库仑吸引，从而激发超辐射，使辐射复合速率从纳米立方体到纳米片再到纳米棒依次加快；各向异性局域场因子（anisotropic local field factor）是增强辐射速率的次要但不可忽略的机制。激子束缚能主要由强限域方向决定，但弱限域方向在长宽比较小时也有影响；介电限域对束缚能影响显著，但对粒子间距离影响较小。所有维度下双激子几何构型均为扭曲四面体（distorted tetrahedron），而非由库仑主导的 2D 或 1D 结构中的方形或线性分布。

Conclusion: 维度降低通过强限域压缩激子波函数增强库仑相互作用和超辐射，导致辐射复合速率显著提升；介电限域是调控激子束缚能的关键因素；双激子构型的普遍扭曲四面体结构表明库仑相互作用在各维度下均无法完全将双激子约束为简单的低维几何构型。

Abstract: We present a theoretical study comparing the excitonic ground state properties of CsPbBr$_3$ nanocrystals with different dimensionality: nanorods (1D), nanoplatelets (2D) and nanocubes (3D). All three systems are described on equal footing, by means of a general variational effective mass model, which captures the influence of quantum confinement, dielectric confinement, electron-hole correlations and polaronic effects (within a Haken model). The strongly confined directions squeeze the exciton (X) wavefunction and enhance Coulomb attractions along the weakly confined directions. This stimulates superradiance, thus making radiative recombination rates speed up from cubes to platelets and to rods, in line with recent experiments. The anisotropic local field factor is a secondary, yet non-negligible, mechanism further enhancing radiative rates. X binding energies are also determined primarily by the directions of strong confinenement, which is also consistent with experiments. Weakly confined directions become however influential for small aspect ratios. Dielectric confinement plays a major role in determining the binding energies, and less so in the interparticle-distances. For all dimensionalities, the biexciton (XX) geometry is that of a distorted tetrahedron, rather than squared or linear distributions that would result in Coulomb-governed 2D and 1D structures.

### [21] [Mitigating Detector Ageing Effects with Graph-Based Multi-Modal Track Reconstruction at Belle II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15361)
*Lea Reuter,Tristan Brandes,Giacomo De Pietro,Torben Ferber*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文评估了基于图神经网络（GNN）的统一径迹寻找算法在 Belle II 中心漂移室长期探测器老化条件下的性能。该算法将径迹寻找形式化为一个全局关系聚类问题，利用目标凝聚（object condensation）方法重建每事件中未知且可变数量的径迹。在包含束流背景、探测器噪声和实测老化效应的全模拟环境下，GNN 方法将绝对径迹效率损失限制在 14%（基线算法为 28%），并保持 96% 的径迹纯度（基线算法为 90%），展现出对不规则击中模式和扩展非活动区域的更强鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Belle II 中心漂移室中由硬件故障和探测器增益退化引起的大背景会导致空间非均匀且随时间变化的非效率区域（inefficiencies），产生非活动区域和缺失击中，对传统径迹寻找算法构成挑战，因此亟需开发新的算法以应对长期探测器老化问题。

Method: 将径迹寻找建模为基于目标凝聚（object condensation）的全局关系聚类问题，使用统一的图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）进行求解；同时将探测器退化视为击中模式中的领域偏移（domain shift），通过在退化条件下重新训练 GNN 来适应变化。

Result: 在包含束流背景、探测器噪声和实测老化效应的全模拟中，GNN 方法将均匀位移μ子的绝对径迹效率损失限制在 14%（基线算法为 28%），径迹纯度达到 96%（基线算法为 90%）。

Conclusion: 统一的基于 GNN 的径迹重建算法对不规则击中模式和扩展非活动区域具有更强的鲁棒性，能够在 Belle II 长期探测器老化条件下保持稳定的径迹重建性能。

Abstract: Large backgrounds that can lead to hardware failures and the degradation of detector gain impact the track finding in the Belle II central drift chamber. These conditions lead to spatially non-uniform and time-dependent inefficiencies, which results in inactive regions and missing hits which challenges conventional tracking algorithms and necessitate the development of new track finding algorithms. In this work, we evaluate the performance of our previously developed unified graph neural network (GNN) based track-finding algorithm under realistic long-term detector ageing conditions. Track finding is formulated as a global relational clustering problem using object condensation, which enables the reconstruction of an unknown and variable number of tracks per event. Using a realistic full detector simulation incorporating beam-induced backgrounds, detector noise, and measured detector ageing effects, we evaluate the tracking performance and compare it to the current Belle II baseline reconstruction. We show that detector degradation can be treated as a domain shift in the observed hit patterns, rather than requiring a fundamentally new reconstruction strategy. After retraining on degraded detector conditions, the GNN-based approach limits the absolute track efficiency loss for uniformly displaced muons to 14%, compared to 28% for the baseline tracking, while maintaining a track purity of 96%. Under the same conditions, the baseline reconstruction achieves only 90% track purity. These results demonstrate that the unified GNN-based reconstruction provides increased robustness to irregular hit patterns and extended inactive regions, enabling stable tracking performance under long-term detector ageing at Belle II.

### [22] [Growth of quartet correlations in neutron-rich Tellurium isotopes within quartet Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15700)
*Yixin Guo,Hiroyuki Sagawa,Masaaki Kimura*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文在四重态BCS（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer）框架下研究富中子Te同位素中的四重态关联。以^{100}Sn为惰性核芯，考虑两个价质子和价中子占据2d_{5/2}⊕1g_{7/2}模型空间，并利用与电荷无关的等矢量配对相互作用求解四重态BCS变分方程。研究发现，随着价中子数增加，价四重态数目及凝聚四重态分量均增大，质子对1g_{7/2}轨道的占据显著增强，表明额外价中子增强了四重态混合，并将固定质子权重从类对构型重新分配至四重态构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索富中子Te同位素中四重态关联（quartet correlations）的行为，特别是在四重态BCS框架下研究价中子数变化对核子配对及四重态凝聚的影响。

Method: 采用四重态BCS（quartet BCS）框架，以^{100}Sn为惰性核芯（inert core），将两个价质子（valence protons）和价中子（valence neutrons）置于2d_{5/2}⊕1g_{7/2}模型空间中，利用与电荷无关的等矢量配对相互作用（charge-independent isovector pairing interaction）求解四重态BCS变分方程。有效配对强度通过Te同位素链中经验中子配对隙（empirical neutron pairing gaps）进行约束。

Result: 当价中子数从N_{\rm val}=2增大至14时，价四重态数目（valence quartet number）和凝聚四重态分量（condensed quartet component）均呈现增长趋势。质子对1g_{7/2}轨道的占据显著增强，接近简并权重极限（degeneracy-weighted limit），且相较于传统的同类粒子BCS参考态（like-particle BCS reference）有显著提升。

Conclusion: 额外价中子增强了关联四重态BCS态中的四重态混合（quartet admixture），同时将固定的质子权重从类对构型（pair-like configurations）重新分配至四重态构型（quartet configurations）。

Abstract: Quartet correlations in neutron-rich Te isotopes are investigated within the quartet Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) framework. Taking \(^{100}\)Sn as an inert core, we consider two valence protons and valence neutrons occupying the \(2d_{5/2}\oplus1g_{7/2}\) model space, and solve the quartet BCS variational equations with a charge-independent isovector pairing interaction. The effective pairing strength is constrained from empirical neutron pairing gaps in the Te isotopic chain. We find that the valence quartet number increases as the valence neutron number is enlarged from \(N_{\rm val}=2\) to \(14\). The same increasing behavior is also found for the condensed quartet component. The proton occupation of the \(1g_{7/2}\) orbit is strongly enhanced relative to the conventional like-particle BCS reference and is driven close to the degeneracy-weighted limit. These results suggest that additional valence neutrons enhance the quartet admixture in the correlated quartet BCS state, while redistributing the fixed proton weight from pair-like configurations to quartet configurations.

</details>

Yang,J. Yang,T. Yang,A. Yankelevich,L. Yates,U. Yevarouskaya,K. Yonehara,T. Young,B. Yu,H. Yu,J. Yu,K. Yu,X. Yu,W. Yuan,R. Zaki,J. Zalesak,L. Zambelli,B. Zamorano,A. Zani,L. Zazueta,G. P. Zeller,J. Zennamo,J. Zettlemoyer,K. Zeug,C. Zhang,S. Zhang,Y. Zhang,L. Zhao,M. Zhao,K. Zhu,E. D. Zimmerman,S. Zucchelli,A. Zummo,V. Zutshi,R. Zwaska*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 ProtoDUNE-DP 的实验运行情况。该探测器是迄今最大的双相液氩时间投影室（Dual-Phase Liquid Argon Time Projection Chamber），有源体积为 6×6×6 m³，对应有源质量 300 吨（总液氩质量 720 吨），于 2019-2020 年在 CERN 中微子平台利用宇宙线μ子取数。电荷读出平面（Charge Readout Planes）出现重大技术问题影响长期运行，但关键子系统（如 -300 kV 高压、可替换读出电子学、光子探测系统）验证了预期性能。实验经验促成了垂直漂移液氩时间投影室（Vertical Drift LArTPC）的改进设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建最大规模的双相液氩时间投影室以验证其在大尺度中微子探测器中的可行性，同时识别技术瓶颈并评估关键子系统性能。

Method: 采用液氩作为靶物质，电场垂直方向（vertical drift field）使电离电子向上漂移至顶部阳极；电荷在液面上方气氩中被提取，通过汤森德雪崩（Townsend avalanche）放大并由大面积电子倍增器（Large Electron Multipliers, LEM）构成的电荷读出平面收集。

Result: 电荷读出平面因严重技术问题无法长期稳定运行；但 -300 kV 高压馈入、可替换读出电子学以及光子探测系统均达到设计性能要求。

Conclusion: ProtoDUNE-DP 的运行经验和暴露的问题直接推动了垂直漂移液氩时间投影室（Vertical Drift LArTPC）的设计改进。

Abstract: ProtoDUNE-DP was the largest ever built Liquid Argon Time Projection Chamber (LArTPC) operating in Dual-Phase (DP) mode, with a liquid target and charge read-out placed in the gas. It had an active volume of $6\times6\times6$\,m$^3$ corresponding to an active mass of 300\,t (total LAr mass of 720\,t), constructed at the CERN Neutrino Platform and took data from 2019 to 2020 with cosmic muons. In ProtoDUNE-DP the electric drift field is oriented in the vertical direction, causing the electrons to drift vertically towards the anode at the top. The ionization charge is then extracted into the gaseous argon above the liquid surface, amplified by Townsend avalanches, and collected by the charge readout planes. The detector experienced significant technical problems affecting the long-term operation of the Charge Readout Planes, formed by the Large Electron Multipliers, but other critical segments demonstrated required performance including the delivery of -300 kV to the TPC cathode, verification of replaceable charge read-out electronics, and operation of the photon detection system. ProtoDUNE-DP experience resulted in improved designs of the Vertical Drift LArTPC.

</details>

### [24] [Spontaneous Nanopatterning and Strain Relaxation in SiGe Layers Grown by Oxidative Solid Phase Epitaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15332)
*Sophie E. Bierer,Trevor R. Smith,Arezoo Mafi,Sunzhuoran Wang,Chengqian Liao,Vatsalkumar Patel,Andrew P. Knights,Ryan B. Lewis*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过氧化固相外延（oxidative solid phase epitaxy, SPE）在Si(111)上形成超薄SiGe应变缓冲层（metamorphic buffer layer），用于III-V族材料与硅的异质外延集成，并发现在SiGe/Si界面上由Shockley不全位错（Shockley partial dislocations）构成的六方网络导致Ge浓度纳米图案化，该图案间距可用于非破坏性表征局部应变状态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: III-V族材料在硅片上实现晶圆级单片集成对于光电子硬件（optoelectronic hardware）具有变革性意义，但异质外延（heteroepitaxy）面临大的晶格失配（lattice mismatch）和热失配（thermal mismatch）问题，需要降低穿透位错密度（threading dislocation densities）。因此需要开发超薄应变缓冲层来克服这些挑战。

Method: 对Si(111)基底进行Ge+离子注入，然后通过氧化固相外延（oxidative SPE）工艺形成超薄SiGe应变缓冲层（metamorphic buffer layer）。利用扫描电子显微镜（SEM）和透射电子显微镜（TEM）观察Ge浓度变化在样品表面形成的纳米图案。通过分析SEM图案间距作为非破坏性方法获取SiGe层的局部应变状态。

Result: 氧化SPE工艺导致Ge浓度在样品表面形成纳米级图案化（nanopatterning），该图案由SiGe/Si界面处的Shockley不全位错（Shockley partial dislocations）构成的六方网络（hexagonal network）所引起。SEM图案间距分析被证明是一种简便、非破坏性的方法，可用于获取SiGe层的局部应变状态。

Conclusion: 这项工作对于工程化超薄SiGe应变缓冲层（metamorphic buffer layer）具有重要意义，可用于在硅平台上实现III-V族光电子器件的异质外延（heteroepitaxy）。

Abstract: The wafer-scale monolithic integration of III-V materials on Si would lead to revolutionary optoelectronic hardware for data, computing and other applications. However, heteroepitaxy of III-Vs on Si requires overcoming the large lattice and thermal mismatches between the materials and reducing threading dislocations densities. In this work, we explore the oxidative solid phase epitaxy (SPE) of Ge+ implanted Si(111) to form ultra-thin strain-relieving SiGe metamorphic buffer layers for heteroepitaxy on Si. The SPE process is shown to result in a nanopatterning of the Ge concentration variation across the sample surface, visible by scanning and transmission electron microscopy (SEM and TEM). The concentration patterning is the result of a hexagonal network of Shockley partial dislocations at the SiGe/Si interface. Analyzing the pattern spacing observed by SEM is demonstrated as an easy, non-destructive method for obtaining the local strain state of SiGe layers. This work is important for engineering ultra-thin SiGe metamorphic buffer layers for III-V optoelectronics heteroepitaxy on the silicon platform.

</details>


### [25] [Phase-Field Simulation of Dendrite Evolution in All-Solid-State Sodium Batteries during Cycling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15387)
*Chengyin Wu,Wolfgang Windl,Jung-Hyun Kim,Yanzhou Ji*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过相场模型（phase-field model）和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，揭示了钠全固态电池（Na SSBs）中枝晶持续穿透的机制：由于晶界几何结构导致的枝晶剥离（stripping）与沉积（plating）不对称性，形成残留的孤立钠金属，该金属在后续循环中被动力学稳定并重新激活，从而加速和加剧枝晶穿透。研究还分析了外加电压、电解质微结构和负极化学组成对枝晶行为的影响，提出了稳定Na SSBs负极/电解质界面的设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全固态电池（SSBs）中循环过程中的枝晶生长是限制其安全性和高能量密度发挥的关键挑战，尤其是充放电循环中枝晶持续穿透的机制尚不清楚且难以通过实验表征，因此亟需理论层面的理解与可视化分析。

Method: 本研究采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算提供参数的相场模型（phase-field model），对钠全固态电池（Na SSBs）中采用纯钠或Na-Sb合金负极以及多晶Na$_3$SbS$_4$电解质的体系进行枝晶穿透行为的原因分析和可视化模拟。

Result: 研究发现枝晶剥离相对于沉积具有内在不对称性，源于晶界几何结构，导致孤立钠金属在循环间持续存在；这些残留钠金属在晶界交界处被动力学稳定，并在后续沉积过程中被重新激活，从而加速和增强枝晶穿透。此外还考察了外加电压、固态电解质微结构和负极化学组成的影响。

Conclusion: 孤立钠金属被确认为Na SSBs中枝晶持续传播的关键贡献因素，研究结果为稳定Na SSBs的负极/电解质界面提供了设计原则。

Abstract: Dendrite growth during cycling remains a critical challenge for all-solid-state batteries (SSBs), limiting the full realization of their inherent safety and high energy density. In particular, the mechanisms of continuous dendrite penetration during charge-discharge cycling remain poorly understood and are difficult to characterize experimentally. This study applies a phase-field model, informed by density functional theory calculations, to rationalize and visualize the dendrite penetration behaviors during cycling in sodium (Na) SSBs with pure Na or Na-Sb alloy anodes and polycrystalline Na$_3$SbS$_4$ electrolyte. We show that dendrite stripping is intrinsically asymmetric with respect to plating due to grain boundary geometry, leading to the formation of isolated Na metal that persists between cycles. This residual Na metal becomes kinetically stabilized at grain-boundary junctions and is readily reactivated during subsequent plating, thereby accelerating and amplifying dendrite penetration. We further investigate the effects of applied voltage, solid-electrolyte microstructure, and anode chemistry on this phenomenon. These findings establish isolated Na metal as a key contributor for continued dendrite propagation in Na SSBs and provide design principles for stabilizing anode/electrolyte interfaces in Na SSBs.

</details>


### [26] [Ab initio time-dependent GW approach for nonequilibrium exciton-phonon coupled dynamics across momentum space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15411)
*Zhenfa Zheng,Benran Zhang,Jiawei Ruan,Chih-En Hsu,Zien Zhu,Supavit Pokawanvit,Felipe H. da Jornada,Hung-Chung Hsueh,Ting Cao,Mauro Del Ben,Yang-Hao Chan,Steven G. Louie,Zhenglu Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的从头算含时绝热GW方法（ab initio time-dependent adiabatic GW methodology），能够在实空间实时模拟包含完整有限动量电子-空穴（e-h）和电子-声子（e-ph）耦合的激子-声子相干动力学，并在单层WSe₂中揭示了约0.5皮秒内的超快谷间激子动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料中光学激发动力学通常涉及非平衡状态下相互纠缠的电子-空穴（e-h）和电子-声子（e-ph）相互作用，但现有第一性原理方法无法在实时中系统处理整个晶体动量空间中的相干激子激发与激子-声子相互作用，这是一个重大挑战。

Method: 该方法基于含时绝热GW框架（time-dependent adiabatic GW framework），将激子激发通过相互作用单粒子密度矩阵的运动方程自然描述，而激子-声子耦合在线性响应框架（linear-response framework）下构建，从而可在原胞内高效完成模拟。

Result: 在单层WSe₂的泵浦-探测时间分辨和角分辨光发射谱（time-resolved and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）模拟中，揭示了声子介导的超快谷间激子动力学，时间尺度约为0.5皮秒，表现为光发射强度从K谷向Q谷的带内转移。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个全面且实用的非平衡格林函数框架（nonequilibrium Green's function framework），能够从第一性原理精确模拟涉及激子与声子耦合的非平衡与相干激发过程。

Abstract: The dynamics of optical excitations in materials generally involves intertwined electron-hole (e-h) and electron-phonon (e-ph) interactions out of equilibrium. However, a full theoretical description of such nonequilibrium dynamics requires a systematic treatment of the coherent excitonic excitations and exciton-phonon interactions across the entire crystal momentum space in real time, which remains a major challenge and out of reach for first-principles approaches. Here, we present a new ab initio time-dependent adiabatic GW methodology that incorporates full finite-momentum e-h and e-ph couplings, enabling real-time simulations of the coherently coupled exciton-phonon dynamics. The excitonic excitations are naturally described by the equation of motion of the interacting single-particle density matrix, whereas their couplings to phonons are formulated within a linear-response framework, hence the simulations can be efficiently carried out within a primitive unit cell. We demonstrate the capabilities of this new approach by investigating the direct-to-indirect exciton transitions in monolayer WSe2 in a pump-probe setup of time-resolved and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy. Our results reveal that the phonon-mediated ultrafast intervalley dynamics of excitons of this system is within ~0.5 ps, manifested as in-gap photoemission intensity transfer from the K-valley to the Q-valley. This work establishes a comprehensive and practical nonequilibrium Green's function framework for accurately simulating nonequilibrium and coherent excitations involving coupled excitons and phonons from first principles.

</details>


### [27] [exa-PD: A scalable high-performance workflow for multi-element phase diagram construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15476)
*Zhuo Ye,Feng Zhang,Maxim Moraru,Weiyi Xia,Ying Wai Li,Yongxin Yao,Cai-Zhuang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: Exa-PD 是一个高度并行化的工作流，利用 LAMMPS 中的分子动力学（MD）和蒙特卡洛（MC）采样技术，结合 Parsl 工作流引擎和 PyCalphad 热力学建模，实现多元素相图（phase diagrams）的高效构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多元素相图的构建通常计算成本高昂，传统方法难以高效地同时对多个相进行精细的温度-组分网格采样。因此需要一种高度可并行化的工作流来加速自由能计算与相图构建过程。

Method: 采用 LAMMPS 软件包中的分子动力学（MD，Molecular Dynamics）和蒙特卡洛（MC，Monte Carlo）作为标准采样技术（standard sampling techniques），在精细的温度-组分网格上同时对多个相进行采样；以 Parsl 作为全局工作流引擎（global workflow engine），协调大量 MD 和 MC 任务实现大规模并行化（massive parallelization）与强可扩展性（strong scalability）；将得到的液相和固相自由能输入至 PyCalphad 软件包进行 CALPHAD 建模，以构建多元素相图（multi-element phase diagrams, PDs）。

Result: 实现了对液相和固相自由能的计算，并将结果用于 CALPHAD 建模，最终构建出多元素相图。

Conclusion: Exa-PD 提供了一种高度并行化、强可扩展的 workflow，能够高效构建多元素相图，为材料热力学计算提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Exa-PD is a highly parallelizable workflow designed for the construction of multi-element phase diagrams (PDs). It uses standard sampling techniques, molecular dynamics (MD) and Monte Carlo (MC) as implemented in the LAMMPS package, to simultaneously sample multiple phases over a fine temperature-composition mesh for free-energy calculations. Parsl serves as the global workflow engine, coordinating large ensembles of MD and MC tasks to achieve massive parallelization with strong scalability. The resulting free energies of liquid and solid phases are then fed to CALPHAD modeling via the PyCalphad package to construct multi-element PDs.

</details>


### [28] [Exploring the Potential of BY3 (Y = P, As) Monolayers as High-Capacity and Rapid-Diffusion Anodes for Sodium-Ion Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15514)
*Jakkapat Seeyangnok,Joongjai Panpranot,Udomsilp Pinsook*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文基于第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT），系统评估了二维BX₃（X = As, P）单层材料作为钠离子电池（SIBs）负极的性能。研究表明BAs₃和BP₃均具有优异的力学/动力学稳定性、本征金属性、强Na吸附亲和力、超低Na离子迁移势垒（0.19 eV和0.26 eV）以及极高的理论比容量（1365 mAh g⁻¹和3875 mAh g⁻¹），是下一代高能量密度储能系统的理想候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钠离子电池（SIBs）的快速发展亟需兼具高比容量和快速离子传输动力学特性的稳健负极材料，现有二维材料难以满足上述综合性能要求，因此需要探索新型二维负极候选材料。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）进行系统计算评估；通过力学与动力学稳定性测试验证结构可行性；利用投影态密度（PDOS）分析电子性质；计算Na吸附能、迁移势垒、平均开路电压及理论比容量等关键性能指标。

Result: BAs₃和BP₃单层均表现出优异的力学与动力学稳定性及本征金属性；Na吸附优先占据H3中空位点，由离子-共价协同键合机制驱动；最优Na离子迁移势垒分别仅为0.19 eV（BAs₃）和0.26 eV（BP₃）；即使在最大理论钠化极限下（Na₁₂₀B₈X₂₄），PDOS分析仍证实体系保持稳健的金属导电性；平均开路电压分别为0.15 V（BAs₃）和0.18 V（BP₃），理论比容量分别高达1365 mAh g⁻¹和3875 mAh g⁻¹，显著优于现有二维SIB负极材料。

Conclusion: BX₃单层材料具备优异的综合电化学性能与结构鲁棒性，是下一代高能量密度储能系统中极具前景的负极候选材料。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of sodium-ion batteries (SIBs) demands robust anode materials capable of delivering high specific capacities while maintaining rapid ion transport kinetics. In this work, we employ first-principles density functional theory (DFT) to systematically evaluate the two-dimensional BX3 (X = As, P) monolayers as high-performance anode candidates for SIBs. Our calculations reveal that both the BAs3 and BP3 frameworks exhibit excellent mechanical and dynamical stability alongside an intrinsic metallic character. These materials demonstrate a strong thermodynamic affinity for Na adsorption, driven by a synergistic ionic and covalent bonding mechanism that highly favors the H3 hollow site. Furthermore, they facilitate exceptionally fast charge and discharge kinetics, characterized by ultralow optimal Na-ion migration barriers of 0.19 eV and 0.26 eV for BAs3 and BP3, respectively. Crucially, projected density of states (PDOS) analyses confirm that both systems preserve their robust metallic conductivity even at their maximum theoretical sodiation limits (Na120B8X24), ensuring continuous and efficient electron transport throughout the electrochemical cycle. We predict low, stable average open-circuit voltages of 0.15 V for BAs3 and 0.18 V for BP3, alongside ultrahigh theoretical specific capacities of 1365 mAh g-1 and 3875 mAh g-1, respectively, which significantly outperform contemporary 2D SIB anodes. These compelling theoretical findings establish the BX3 monolayers as outstanding, structurally resilient candidates for next-generation, high-energy-density energy storage systems.

</details>


### [29] [Symbolic Predicate-Guided Language Agents for Inverse Design of Perovskite Oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15535)
*Dong Hyeon Mok,Seoin Back,Victor Fung,Guoxiang Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于领域特定语言（DSL）引导的多智能体材料设计框架ORCHESTRA，通过将自然语言设计规则转化为符号谓词（symbolic predicates），提升大语言模型（LLM）在逆向材料设计（inverse materials design）中的推理与规则验证能力，并在双钙钛矿氧化物（double perovskite oxides）的逆向设计中展示了优于纯自然语言规则的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据驱动和人工智能策略虽推动了高性能材料的发现，但大语言模型（LLM）的逆向设计能力仍需增强，尤其是在推理可解释性和设计规则的自评估方面。

Method: 引入一种领域特定语言（DSL）引导策略，将自然语言设计规则翻译为预定义化学DSL中的符号谓词（symbolic predicates），使LLM智能体能够从累积的材料数据中获取统计证据，从而在设计循环中评估并优化自身推理。基于该策略开发了多智能体框架ORCHESTRA（Operational Rule-grounded CHEmical Search Through Reasoning Agents）。

Result: 符号谓词帮助LLM识别无证据支持的规则、验证新提出的规则，并在迭代设计循环中改进规则库。与仅依赖自然语言规则的策略相比，DSL引导框架在提升材料设计性能方面展现出潜力，尤其针对具有挑战性的目标性质。

Conclusion: 数学与统计依据（mathematical and statistical grounding）能够增强LLM智能体在材料科学中的推理能力；基于LLM的逆向设计可有效执行，无需大规模任务特定数据集或额外模型训练。

Abstract: Efficient discovery of high-performance materials has been pursued through a variety of data- and AI-driven strategies, among which inverse design, generating materials from desired target properties, has emerged as an important paradigm. Large language models (LLMs) offer a complementary route for inverse materials design because their reasoning and in-context learning capability can be used not only to propose candidates but also to demonstrate interpretable design principles. In this work, we introduce a domain specific language (DSL)-guided strategy to improve the reasoning and design capability of LLM agents by translating natural language design rules into symbolic predicates encoded in a predefined chemistry DSL. These predicates allow the LLM agent to obtain statistical evidence from the accumulated materials data, enabling the agent to evaluate and refine its own reasoning during the design loop. Based on this strategy, we developed a multi-agent materials design framework, called Operational Rule-grounded CHEmical Search Through Reasoning Agents (ORCHESTRA), and applied it to the inverse design of double perovskite oxides under multiple target-property objectives. The results show that symbolic predicates help the LLM identify unsupported rules, validate newly proposed rules and improve the rule store over iterative design cycles. Compared with a strategy relying only on natural language rules, the DSL-guided framework showed the potential to improve materials design performance, particularly for challenging target properties. These findings suggest that mathematical and statistical grounding can enhance the reasoning capability of LLM agents in materials science and that LLM-based inverse design can be performed effectively without large task-specific datasets or additional model training.

</details>


### [30] [Terahertz Time-Domain Spectroscopy as a Universal Defect Fingerprinting Tool for Organic Halide Perovskite Solar Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15538)
*Inhee Maeng,Young Mi Lee,Jinwoo Park,Seung Jae Oh,Min-Cherl Jung*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机-无机杂化钙钛矿（OHP）单结与叠层器件的效率距离Shockley-Queisser（S-Q）极限仍有显著差距，主要原因在于晶界（grain-boundary, GB）缺陷驱动非辐射复合、离子迁移与降解；现有探针缺乏在器件相关薄膜中识别并定量特定缺陷物种的非接触能力。

Conclusion: 基于上述发现，提出一个三步闭环框架用于太赫兹引导缺陷工程：（I）通过振子强度分析定量测量缺陷；（II）从系统构建的太赫兹光谱库中提取材料特异性指纹；（III）基于指纹引导的缺陷消除与实时反馈，形成连接光谱诊断、钝化策略与最终效率提升的质量控制闭环。

Abstract: Organic-inorganic hybrid perovskites (OHPs) deliver certified single-junction power conversion efficiencies (PCEs) exceeding 26% and perovskite-silicon tandem values surpassing 34%, yet a substantial gap with the Shockley-Queisser (S-Q) limit persists-primarily due to grain-boundary (GB) defects that drive non-radiative recombination, ion migration, and degradation. Rational passivation demands a non-contact tool capable of identifying and quantifying specific defect species in device-relevant thin films, a capability absent from conventional probes. This short review demonstrates that terahertz time-domain spectroscopy (THz-TDS, 0.3-3.0 THz) fulfills this role. Across four OHP compositions fabricated by sequential vacuum evaporation (SVE)-MAPbI3, MAPbBr3, FAPbI3, and CsPbI3-the THz spectral window captures both intrinsic phonon modes and GB-localized molecular defect vibrations, enabling species-specific, quantitative characterization at room temperature. Notably, the oscillator strength of the SVE-specific 1.58 THz absorption in MAPbI3 scales linearly with XPS-quantified CH3NH2 defect concentration, establishing THz-TDS as a direct, non-destructive defect meter. Building on these findings, we propose a three-pillar framework for THz-guided defect engineering: (I) quantitative defect measurement via oscillator-strength analysis, (II) material-specific fingerprint identification from a systematically constructed THz library, and (III) fingerprint-guided defect elimination with real-time feedback-together defining a closed-loop quality-control cycle that connects spectroscopic diagnosis to passivation strategy and, ultimately, to enhanced solar-cell efficiency.

### [31] [Symmetry-Enforced Dirac Fermions and Structural Metastability in Pentagonal Monolayers of Transition-Metal Ditellurides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15580)
*Manoj Gadtoula,Clayton Conner,Avinash Sah,Ronghao Luo,Guang Bian*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，研究了过渡金属二碲化物（transition-metal ditellurides）中六方相（hexagonal）与五方相（pentagonal）多晶型之间的结构转变与电子性质变化，发现六方-半金属到五方-半导体的转变需越过一个中间结构阈值，而并非始于对称性降低的初始阶段，并揭示Te–Te二聚体形成及非对称（nonsymmorphic）对称性对能隙打开和狄拉克态（Dirac states）的关键作用。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），研究六方和五方两种多晶型（polymorphs）的单层XTe₂（X = Pd, Pt, Ni），并构建从六方相到五方相的连续结构插值（continuous structural interpolation）以追踪电子结构演变。

Conclusion: 五方XTe₂单层构成了一类新型二维半导体（2D semiconductors），其中对称性约束（symmetry constraints）与局域成键（local bonding）共同塑造了非常规的半导体内电子结构。

Abstract: The recent synthesis of pentagonal PdTe$_2$ monolayer motivates broader research interests in transition-metal ditellurides whose electronic phases are governed by symmetry and structural reconstruction. The pentagonal phase of transition-metal ditellurides exhibits electronic properties that are dramatically different from those of its hexagonal counterpart due to its lower crystalline symmetry. Using first-principles calculations, we study monolayer $X$Te$_2$ ($X=\mathrm{Pd},\mathrm{Pt},\mathrm{Ni}$) in both hexagonal and pentagonal polymorphs. By constructing a continuous structural interpolation between the hexagonal and pentagonal phases, we show that the semimetal (hex)-to-semiconductor (penta) transition occurs only after an intermediate structural threshold rather than at the onset of symmetry reduction. The gap opening coincides with the formation of Te--Te dimers, which drive the bonding--antibonding splitting of the Te $p$ states and reorganize the band edges. In addition, the nonsymmorphic symmetry of the pentagonal phase enforces band degeneracies at the Brillouin-zone boundary, leading to symmetry-protected two-dimensional (2D) Dirac states. These results establish pentagonal $X$Te$_2$ monolayers as a new class of 2D semiconductors in which symmetry constraints and local bonding collectively shape the unconventional semiconducting electronic structure.

### [33] [Interface-Engineered Giant Multistate Resistance Switching in Altermagnetic CrSb Multiferroic Tunnel Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15728)
*Zhi Yan,Yuwen Hua,Yueting Li,Xujin Zhang,Jianhua Xiao,Xiaohong Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，展示了基于CrSb/α-In₂Se₃交替磁体多铁隧道结中由界面对称性、自旋通道匹配和铁电极化重构共同调控的巨大多态电阻开关效应，实现了最高8个非易失电阻态，TMR和TER分别达到3.77×10⁴%和4.18×10⁵%。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交替磁体（altermagnets）能够实现无杂散磁场（stray magnetic field）的自旋劈裂输运，但如何将依赖于动量（momentum）的自旋劈裂转化为强隧道结（tunnel junction）响应，仍需界面选择性的隧道通道（interface-selected tunneling channels）来实现。本文旨在探索这一转化机制并实现多态电阻开关。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function, NEGF）方法相结合的第一性原理计算，分析CrSb/α-In₂Se₃交替磁体多铁隧道结（altermagnetic multiferroic tunnel junction）的电子输运特性。

Result: 研究发现，电阻开关效应主要由界面机制决定：Cr/Sb终止层（termination）和h-BN或石墨烯插入层控制自旋通道匹配（spin-channel matching），铁电偏振（ferroelectric polarization）重塑静电势垒。对称与不对称终止层可反转平行/反平行Néel矢量（Néel-vector）构型与高/低阻态的对应关系。单层In₂Se₃结实现4个非易失电阻态，TMR和TER分别达1626%和2206%，费米能级移动后可提升至9576%和4144%。双层In₂Se₃引入层间偏振耦合，实现8个电阻态，最大TMR和TER分别为3.77×10⁴%和4.18×10⁵%。

Conclusion: 界面对称性（interface symmetry）、自旋通道匹配和铁电势垒重建（ferroelectric barrier reconstruction）可作为无杂散场多态自旋电子隧道器件（stray-field-free multistate spintronic tunnel device）的设计原则。

Abstract: Altermagnets enable spin-split transport without stray magnetic fields, yet converting their momentum-dependent spin splitting into a strong tunnel-junction response requires interface-selected tunneling channels. Here, using density functional theory combined with nonequilibrium Green's function calculations, we demonstrate giant multistate resistance switching in CrSb/$α$-In$_2$Se$_3$ altermagnetic multiferroic tunnel junctions. The response is governed not by the bulk spin splitting of CrSb alone, but by a symmetry-selected interfacial mechanism in which Cr/Sb terminations and \textit{h}-BN or graphene insertion layers determine spin-channel matching, while ferroelectric polarization reshapes the electrostatic barrier. Symmetric and asymmetric terminations reverse the correspondence between parallel/antiparallel Néel-vector configurations and high-/low-resistance states, showing that the actual alignment of interfacial Cr moments selects the dominant tunneling channels. Monolayer-In$_2$Se$_3$ junctions exhibit four nonvolatile resistance states, with tunneling magnetoresistance (TMR) and tunneling electroresistance (TER) reaching 1626\% and 2206\%, respectively, and increasing to 9576\% and 4144\% upon Fermi-level shifting. Finite-bias calculations further reveal robust spin filtering and tunable spin-polarized currents. Extending the barrier to bilayer In$_2$Se$_3$ introduces interlayer polarization coupling, enabling eight resistance states with maximum TMR and TER values of $3.77\times10^{4}\%$ and $4.18\times10^{5}\%$, respectively. These results establish interface symmetry, spin-channel matching, and ferroelectric barrier reconstruction as design principles for stray-field-free multistate spintronic tunnel devices.

Reflection high-energy electron diffraction as well as scanning electron and atomic force microscopy reveal that the first step results in a rough intermediate surface with open pits, whereas the final surface is smooth. ### [35] [Nonuniform pressure helps structural superlubricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15967)
*Melisa M. Gianetti,Viet Hung Ho,Bjørn Haugen,Graham Cross,Astrid S. de Wijn*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究发现非均匀压力分布实际上有助于结构超润滑（structural superlubricity），而非阻碍它。关键在于接触边缘的压力为零，这改善了钉扎脱钉（depinning）的标度行为，从而降低了摩擦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构超润滑虽能极大降低摩擦，但实际应用中要求完美均匀的原子级平整表面，而真实表面通常粗糙并导致非均匀压力分布。本文旨在探究非均匀压力分布对结构超润滑的影响。

Method: 通过刚性接触的解析计算（analytical calculations）作为基础，并利用简单模型的分子动力学模拟（molecular-dynamics simulations）纳入弹性效应（elasticity）的关键影响。

Result: 接触边缘压力为零（vanishing pressure at the edge of the contact）是关键因素，它改善了脱钉和标度行为（scaling depinning and scaling behaviour），从而降低摩擦。非均匀压力分布实际上促进了结构超润滑。

Conclusion: 非均匀压力分布对结构超润滑具有积极作用，而非传统认为的消极影响。这一发现有助于放松结构超润滑在实际应用中对完美平整表面的苛刻要求。

Abstract: Structural superlubricity, nearly vanishing friction between two structurally incommensurate crystalline surfaces, is a promising avenue for reducing friction in applications, but requires very specific and well-controlled conditions. One of those conditions is perfectly uniform atomically flat surfaces. Real-world surfaces are generally rough, leading to nonuniform pressure distributions. We investigate the effects of nonuniform pressure distributions on structural superlubricity, using analytical calculations for rigid contacts as a basis, and molecular-dynamics simulations for a simple model to include the crucial effects of elasticity. We show that a key ingredient is the vanishing pressure at the edge of the contact, and that this leads to improved scaling depinning and scaling behaviour, leading to lower friction. We thus show that nonuniform pressure distributions actually help structural superlubricity, rather than hinder it.

Method: 采用垂直分辨输运测量揭示厚SeI₂薄膜中由凝固过程中形成的成分和结构不均匀性引起的深度依赖电导率；通过空间光电流映射表征载流子收集均匀性；利用红外热成像验证实际成像能力。

Result: 刚凝固后的玻璃态SeI₂网络表现出缓慢的载流子传输和持续光电导（persistent photoconductivity）；经历长时间结构弛豫后，材料传输性能显著增强，实现了4.3毫秒响应时间的红外光电探测、8 kHz调制频率的稳定工作，以及1550纳米处10⁸ Jones和可见光波段10¹¹ Jones的散粒噪声限制探测率（shot-noise-limited detectivity）。

Conclusion: 结构弛豫（structural relaxation）可作为硒基半导体中载流子传输工程化的一种有效策略，SeI₂是一种有前景的可溶液处理的红外光电探测和热成像平台。

Abstract: The optoelectronic performance of amorphous and partially crystalline semiconductors is strongly governed by structural disorder, yet establishing direct correlations between structural evolution and carrier transport remains challenging. Here, we show that the solid state optoelectronic response of selenium iodine (SeI2) is dictated by its transformation from a metastable glassy phase into an ordered lamellar structure. Vertically resolved transport measurements reveal pronounced depth-dependent electrical conductivity within thick SeI2 films, arising from compositional and structural inhomogeneity developed during solidification. Immediately after solidification, the glassy SeI2 network exhibits sluggish carrier transport and persistent photoconductivity. Upon prolonged structural relaxation, however, the material undergoes significant transport enhancement, enabling millisecond-scale infrared photodetection with a response time of 4.3 ms, stable operation up to 8 kHz modulation frequency, and shot-noise-limited detectivities of 108 Jones at 1550 nm and 1011 Jones in the visible. Spatial photocurrent mapping demonstrates highly uniform carrier collection despite the self-assembled lamellar morphology, while infrared thermal imaging confirms practical imaging capability over a broad temperature range. These results establish structural relaxation as a powerful strategy for engineering carrier transport in selenium-based semiconductors and position SeI2 as a promising solution-processable platform for infrared photodetection and thermal imaging.

</details>

Abstract: The magnetic ground state of the altermagnet candidate RuO$_2$ remains controversial, with magnetic signatures observed mainly in epitaxial films. Charge-density and orbital-resolved analyses reveal interfacial electronic reconstruction, and substrate doping provides a route to tune the induced moments. In symmetric TiO$_2$/RuO$_2$/TiO$_2$ heterostructures, the two magnetic interfaces couple through the metallic RuO$_2$ spacer, producing a thickness-dependent alternation between weak-ferromagnetic and compensated altermagnetic states. Our results identify interface engineering as a practical route to stabilize and control fragile magnetism in RuO$_2$.

In this work, potential degradation hotspots associated with thermomechanical loading in Cu power metallization are investigated using a combined experimental--computational approach. Scanning three-dimensional X-ray diffraction measurements are coupled with thermomechanical crystal plasticity simulations to probe the evolution of grain-resolved plastic deformation during rapid cyclic loading. This integrated approach provides insight into the microstructural processes governing degradation hotspot formation, laying the groundwork for future microstructure-informed, physics-based reliability assessment of Cu metallization.

### [39] [Atomistic mechanism of corrosion-induced grain boundary migration in NiCr alloys in molten FLiNaK](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16167)
*Sadia Khan,Hamdy Arkoub,Miaomiao Jin*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用反应分子动力学（reactive molecular dynamics）模拟，研究了NiCr合金在熔融FLiNaK盐中四种代表性晶界（Σ3(111)、Σ11(113)、Σ5(012)和Σ5(013)）以及相应体表面的腐蚀行为。

Result: 表面晶体学（surface crystallography）控制初始溶解阶段，而晶界特征（grain boundary character）决定腐蚀的空间局域化和长期演化；识别出一种腐蚀驱动的晶界迁移机制，其中氟局域化（fluorine localization）、优先铬溶解（preferential chromium dissolution）和空位介导的迁移率（vacancy-mediated mobility）共同驱动界面远离脱合金区域移动；共格Σ3(111)晶界能抑制这些过程。

Conclusion: 低能特殊晶界（low-energy special boundaries）如Σ3(111)具有抑制腐蚀驱动晶界迁移的能力，表明其可作为耐腐蚀Ni-Cr合金晶界工程（grain boundary engineering）的目标。

Abstract: Corrosion of Ni-Cr structural alloys in molten fluoride salts is a persistent material degradation problem, yet the atomistic role of grain boundaries in this process remains poorly understood. Here we use reactive molecular dynamics to investigate corrosion of NiCr alloys in molten FLiNaK across four representative grain boundaries ($\Sigma3(111)$, $\Sigma11(113)$, $\Sigma5(012)$, and $\Sigma5(013)$) and corresponding bulk surfaces. Surface crystallography controls the initial dissolution stage, while grain boundary character governs the spatial localization and longer-time evolution of corrosion. We further identify a corrosion-driven grain boundary migration mechanism in which fluorine localization, preferential chromium dissolution, and vacancy-mediated mobility together drive interfacial motion away from the dealloyed region. The coherent $\Sigma3(111)$ boundary suppresses these processes, indicating low-energy special boundaries as targets for grain boundary engineering of corrosion-resistant Ni-Cr alloys.
