### [40] [A Dynamical Phase-Field Model for the Optical Properties of Ferroelectrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16180)
*Aiden Ross,Anya Frazer,Venkatraman Gopalan,Long-Qing Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种动力学相场模型（dynamical phase-field model），通过引入电子极化场（electronic polarization field）直接耦合铁电序参量与局域光学响应，实现了对复杂铁电微结构中空间分辨的、随温度和波长变化的光学性质的预测。应用于BaTiO3薄膜，该模型成功揭示了铁电畴结构对局域电光响应的显著增强作用（畴壁处超过4000 pm/V），并定量复现了实验测量的电光系数与温度依赖性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电材料因其自发极化与光学性质之间的强耦合，是可控光子器件（controllable photonic devices）的理想平台。然而，铁电畴结构（ferroelectric domain structure）与光学响应之间的紧密关联使得材料设计极具挑战性，现有理论方法无法同时捕捉两者之间的相互作用。

Method: 作者开发了一种动力学相场模型，通过引入一个电子极化场，将铁电序参量直接耦合到局域光学响应中。该方法可以在复杂铁电微结构中预测空间分辨的、随温度和波长变化的光学性质。

Result: 应用于BaTiO3薄膜，模拟显示铁电畴结构显著改变局域电光响应，畴壁附近电光系数超过4000 pm/V，远高于块体单晶值（r_51=1300 pm/V）。模型定量复现了BaTiO3 on silicon薄膜上测量的电光系数，并捕捉了多个铁电相变过程中的温度依赖性行为，揭示了相竞争（phase competition）与共存（coexistence）在决定电光响应中的作用。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种通用的方法来预测复杂铁电微结构中的光-物质相互作用（light-matter interactions），为光子学应用中铁电材料的计算设计（computational design）提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials are promising platforms for controllable photonic devices because of the strong coupling between their spontaneous polarization and optical properties. Yet, these materials remain challenging to design because of the close connection between the ferroelectric domain structure and optical response, which no existing theoretical approach can capture. Here, we develop a dynamical phase-field model that directly couples the ferroelectric order to the local optical response by introducing an electronic polarization field. This approach enables the prediction of the spatially resolved temperature- and wavelength-dependent optical properties in complex ferroelectric microstructures. Applying this method to BaTiO3 thin films, we investigate the evolution of the local refractive index and electro-optic response under varying electric fields and temperatures. We show that the ferroelectric domain structure strongly modifies the local electro-optic response, exceeding 4000 pm/V near domain walls, several times larger than the bulk single crystal value (r_51=1300 pm/V). Our simulations quantitatively reproduce the electro-optic coefficient measured in BaTiO3 on silicon films and capture the temperature-dependent behavior across multiple ferroelectric phase transitions, revealing the role of phase competition and coexistence in determining the electro-optic response. More broadly, this work establishes a general approach for predicting light-matter interactions in complex ferroelectric microstructures, enabling the computational design of ferroelectric materials for photonics.

### [41] [Orthonormal Sobolev estimates with fractal measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15826)
*Neal Bez,Keith M. Rogers,Shunya Toyoshima*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文证明了针对正交归一函数（orthonormal functions）的Lieb-Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev不等式的分形版本（fractal version），该结果既可作为正交函数系的迹定理（trace theorem），也可用于恢复壳势（shell potential）情形下负特征值个数的Rozenblum-Tashchiyan界以及负特征值之和的Rozenblum界。证明方法直接，避免了Schatten类（Schatten classes）与变分法（variational arguments），并先通过傅里叶分析（Fourier analysis）重新证明了Adams分形Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典的Lieb-Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev不等式推广到分形框架下的正交归一函数，以建立更一般的迹型不等式，并统一恢复壳势负谱问题的若干已有上界估计。

Method: 采用直接证明策略，先利用傅里叶分析重新证明Adams的分形Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev不等式（针对单函数），由此得到所需的端点估计（endpoint estimate）以及Frostman测度（Frostman measures）的相互作用能（interaction energy）上界；再以此为基础推导出正交归一函数系下的分形不等式。

Result: 得到了正交归一函数系的分形Lieb-Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev不等式，并由此恢复了壳势$-Δ-μ$的负特征值个数与负特征值之和的已知最优上界（Rozenblum-Tashchiyan界与Rozenblum界）。

Conclusion: 该分形不等式的证明无需Schatten类或变分法工具，提供了一条更直接的分析路径，同时统一了迹定理与负谱估计两个方向的已有结果。

Abstract: We prove a fractal version of Lieb's Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev inequality for orthonormal functions. On the one hand, this can be viewed as a trace theorem for orthonormal functions. On the other, it allows us to recover the Rozenblum-Tashchiyan bound for the number of negative eigenvalues of $-Δ-μ$, where $μ$ is a shell potential. We also recover Rozenblum's bound for the sum of negative eigenvalues via a Lieb-Thirring kinetic inequality. Our proof is direct, avoiding both Schatten classes and variational arguments. We first reprove Adams' fractal Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev inequality (for single functions) via Fourier analysis. This yields the required endpoint estimate as well as a bound for the interaction energy of Frostman measures.

### [42] [Reversible and irreversible dynamical topological transitions of magnetic Hopfions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15777)
*S. Y. Lu,H. M. Dong,D. X. Yu,K. Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 三维磁Hopfion在交变磁场（alternating magnetic field）作用下呈现出两种截然不同的动力学机制：弱场下发生不可逆拓扑重构转变为toron，强场下则实现吉赫兹频率可逆拓扑开关，开关路径由驱动频率选择（2 GHz呼吸模式或40 GHz旋转模式），揭示了场振幅与频率作为独立调控手段的角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁Hopfion作为一种三维拓扑孤子（topological soliton），其静力学稳定化已被广泛研究，但在交变磁场（alternating magnetic field）下的非线性动力学行为尚不清楚，亟需探索以实现其在三维自旋电子学（3D spintronics）中的应用潜力。

Method: 采用三维微磁学模拟（3D micromagnetic simulations）结合解析模分析（analytical mode analysis），研究受限磁Hopfion在交变磁场驱动下的动力学行为。

Result: 弱场下，Hopfion本征模的共振激发引发非线性不稳定性，导致不可逆拓扑重构为toron；强场下，系统在铁磁态与Hopfion态之间实现吉赫兹频率可逆拓扑开关，2 GHz驱动触发低频集体呼吸模式，40 GHz驱动则产生由强塞曼力矩（Zeeman torque）驱动的非共振旋转模式。

Conclusion: 磁场振幅和频率可作为独立控制手段；可逆Hopfion开关可源于低频集体运动的非线性延续，也可源于非共振高频场锁定（field locking）机制。

Abstract: Magnetic Hopfions are three-dimensional (3D) topological solitons characterized by a nonzero Hopf invariant and offer a promising platform for 3D spintronics. While their static stabilization has been widely studied, their nonlinear dynamics under alternating magnetic (AM) fields remain largely unexplored. We show, using 3D micromagnetic simulations and analytical mode analysis, that an AM field drives two qualitatively distinct dynamical regimes of a confined magnetic Hopfion. In the weak-field regime, resonant excitation of intrinsic Hopfion modes induces a nonlinear instability and an irreversible topological reconfiguration from a Hopfion to a toron. In contrast, in the strong-field regime, the system undergoes reversible field-locked topological switching at GHz frequencies, with the magnetization periodically alternating between a topologically trivial ferromagnetic configuration and a Hopfion state. The switching pathway is selected by the driving frequency: a 2 GHz field drives a breathing pathway associated with the low-frequency collective response, whereas a 40 GHz field produces a nonresonant rotational pathway governed by strong Zeeman-torque-driven precession and field locking. These results identify field amplitude and frequency as independent control knobs and reveal that reversible Hopfion switching can arise either from nonlinear continuation of low-frequency collective motion or from nonresonant high-frequency field locking.

### [43] [The Aeppli Parameter for the Heterotic Moduli](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15804)
*Pei-Lin Wu*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入Aeppli类，在不引入切丛上的辅助规范联络（auxiliary gauge connection）的情况下，构造了3-流形上Hull-Strominger系统的一族解，并利用隐函数定理（implicit function theorem）证明了该族解的存在性，且将该构造推广到了n-流形情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 改进先前工作中需要引入辅助规范联络的做法，从而使得解的维度与Bott-Chern参数（Bott-Chern parameter）精确匹配。

Method: 首先沿Aeppli类（Aeppli class）离壳（off-shell）形变共形平衡度量（conformally balanced metric），然后通过一个依赖于该Aeppli类的厄米(1,1)-形式（hermitian (1,1)-form）在壳（on-shell）调整该度量，以满足反常消去条件（anomaly cancellation condition），最后利用隐函数定理证明该族解的存在性。

Result: 成功构造了一族无需引入切丛上辅助规范联络的Hull-Strominger系统解，并表明该构造可推广至n-流形上的Hull-Strominger系统。

Conclusion: 所构造的解族在维度上与Bott-Chern参数匹配，改进了已有工作，且Aeppli参数化方法具有更一般的适用性。

Abstract: In this paper, we construct a family of solutions to the $3$-fold Hull-Strominger system using the Aeppli class, without introducing the auxiliary gauge connection on the tangent bundle. In particular, we deform the conformally balanced metric along an Aeppli class off-shell and then tune it by a hermitian $(1,1)$-form dependent on this Aeppli class on-shell to satisfy the anomaly cancellation condition. The existence of the family of solutions is then obtained by the implicit function theorem. This refines the previous work by not introducing auxiliary gauge connection, thereby matching the expected dimension with the Bott-Chern parameter. This construction of the Aeppli parameter also extends to the $n$-fold Hull-Strominger system.

### [44] [Multimessenger prospects of quasi-periodic eruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15360)
*Vojtěch Witzany,Alessia Franchini,Matteo Bonetti,Luca Broggi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文探讨了准周期性爆发（QPEs）与极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）及其引力波信号协同探测的可能性，指出当前已知的大部分QPEs对应的引力波频率超出LISA灵敏度带，且存在选择偏差问题，未来应寻找短周期“黄金”QPEs以实现协同观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究准周期性爆发（QPEs）与极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）产生的引力波信号能否被激光干涉空间天线（LISA）协同探测，以利用电磁对应体提供天区定位、实现标准汽笛测量哈勃常数，并约束EMRIs的形成机制。

Method: 结合已知QPEs的轨道周期与LISA灵敏度频段，分析当前QPEs对应的引力波信号频率覆盖情况，并评估QPE探测与LISA仪器各自的选择性偏差对协同探测的影响。

Result: 目前已知的大部分QPEs对应的EMRI轨道周期使得引力波信号频率落在LISA灵敏度带之外；此外，QPE探测与LISA仪器各自的选择偏差也可能阻碍协同探测。

Conclusion: 未来应扩展QPE星表并重点搜寻短周期“黄金”QPEs，这类源对应的EMRIs引力波频率将落入LISA频段，从而实现电磁与引力波协同观测。

Abstract: Quasi-Periodic Eruptions (QPEs) are recurring soft X-ray transients that may be generated by inspirals of stellar-mass objects spiraling into supermassive black holes, known as extreme mass ratio inspirals (EMRIs). Independently, EMRIs and the gravitational-wave signals they generate are one of the key targets for the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA). What is the potential of a coincident detection of EMRIs both as a QPE and by LISA? Electromagnetic counterparts to LISA events would provide sky localization, enable standard siren measurements of the Hubble constant and constrain formation mechanisms of the corresponding inspirals. Combined observations would link the accurate measurements of black hole masses and spins to their galactic nuclear environments and would thus enable lasting synergies with various observations across the electromagnetic spectrum. However, most of the currently known QPEs imply EMRI orbital periods that place the frequencies of the corresponding gravitational-wave signal out of the LISA sensitivity band. Additionally, the selection biases of QPE detections and the LISA instrument may preclude a coincident detection. Future searches should focus on expanding the QPE catalogs and ultimately hunt for ``golden'' short-period QPEs that correspond to EMRIs that fall within the LISA band.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.quant-gas'></div>

# cond-mat.quant-gas [[Back]](#toc)

### [45] [Isothermal compression of a Fermi gas to deep quantum degeneracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15616)
*Kirill Karpov,Jonas Auch,Eduard Heidt,Florian Kiesel,Alexandre De Martino,Christian Groß*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究利用低耗散光学调零阱（optical tune-out trap）在双物种混合物中实现物种选择性囚禁，通过等温压缩（isothermal compression）在玻色浴中冷却费米子量子气体，达到 $T/T_F = 0.024^{+0.007}$ 的深度量子简并，并发现热化时间在简并区与 $T/T_F$ 无关，为在复杂势阱中直接冷却提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法依赖谐波势阱中的蒸发或交感冷却达到最小熵后，所有状态转换只能通过绝热过程进行，熵单调增加。本文旨在突破这一实验范式，利用物种选择性囚禁技术实现非绝热、与环境耦合的熵降低方案。

Method: 采用低耗散光学调零阱（optical tune-out trap）实现双物种混合物的物种选择性囚禁，在玻色浴中对两组分费米子量子气体进行等温压缩（isothermal compression），并通过交叉维弛豫（cross-dimensional relaxation）和热化过程表征冷却效率。

Result: 成功将费米子气体冷却至 $T/T_F = 0.024^{+0.007}$ 的深度量子简并状态；在简并区热化时间与 $T/T_F$ 无关，表明轻费米子与重玻色子之间的冷却在简并区仍保持高效快速。

Conclusion: 该方法可直接应用于光晶格（optical lattice）、盒势阱（box trap）等复杂势阱中的冷却，无需依赖绝热状态转换即可进入强相互作用多体区域，为量子气体实验范式提供了突破性替代方案。

Abstract: The standard approach for generating deeply degenerate quantum gases is evaporative or sympathetic cooling in a harmonic trap, after which the gas has reached its minimum entropy. All subsequent state transformations rely on adiabatic changes of a closed system, and coupling to the environment or non-adiabatic processes monotonically increase the entropy. Here, we demonstrate that this experimental paradigm can be bypassed by utilizing species-selective trapping with a low-dissipation optical tune-out trap in a dual-species mixture. We successfully reduce the entropy of a two-component fermionic quantum gas via isothermal compression within a bosonic bath, reaching deep quantum degeneracy of $T/T_F = 0.024^{+0.007}$, with $T_F$ the Fermi temperature. By characterizing the cross-dimensional relaxation and thermalization, we demonstrate that cooling light fermions with heavy bosons remains efficient and fast, even deep in the degenerate regime, where the thermalization time is found to be independent of $T/T_F$. Our results pave the way for direct cooling within optical lattices, box traps, or other complex potentials, thereby eliminating the reliance on adiabatic state transformations to reach strongly interacting many-body regimes.

</details>


### [46] [Controlling charge and spin currents through nonreciprocal dissipative processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15767)
*Catalin-Mihai Halati,Jean-Sébastien Bernier*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个二维自旋费米子量子系统中，通过打破宇称（inversion）和时间反演（time-reversal）对称性的非互易耗散机制来产生和控制电荷流与自旋流。利用Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad主方程形式以及基于含时广义吉布斯系综的方法，作者识别出在弱耗散耦合区域中所需的最少非互易跳变算符集合，并发现通过两个非互易跳变算符即可同时产生电荷流和自旋流，调节非互易程度可主导从自旋到电荷的输运机制切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在打破宇称和时间反演对称性的二维自旋费米子量子系统中，如何利用非互易（nonreciprocal）耗散机制实现电荷流与自旋流的可控生成与调控，这是量子输运和自旋电子学中的核心问题之一。

Method: 采用Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad主方程（GKSL master equation）形式，并结合基于含时广义吉布斯系综（time-dependent generalized Gibbs ensemble）的方法，在弱耗散耦合区域（weak dissipative coupling regime）分析非互易跳变算符（nonreciprocal jump operators）对电流的驱动作用。

Result: 在存在有限隧穿（finite tunneling）、Rashba耦合（Rashba coupling）和磁场（magnetic field）的条件下，仅需两个非互易跳变算符分别将每种自旋分量非互易地耦合到不同的空间运动方向，即可同时产生电荷流和自旋流；通过调节非互易程度可实现输运机制从自旋主导转向电荷主导；该机制对退相噪声（dephasing noise）具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 非互易耗散机制能够有效且可控地产生电荷流与自旋流，并且该机制在额外耗散过程（如退相噪声）存在下依然保持稳定，为量子器件中的电流调控提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: We investigate the generation and control of both charge and spin currents via nonreciprocal dissipative mechanisms in a two-dimensional spinful fermionic atom quantum system with broken inversion and time-reversal symmetries. Within the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad master equation formalism and using an approach based on the time-dependent generalized Gibbs ensemble, we identify in the weak dissipative coupling regime the minimal set of nonreciprocal jump operators required to induce charge and spin currents and to control both their direction and magnitude. We find that in the presence of finite tunneling, Rashba coupling and magnetic field, the combine application of two jump operators nonreciprocally coupling each spin species to a different spatial direction of motion is sufficient to generate both types of current. Furthermore, by tuning the degree of nonreciprocity of the jump operators we modify the dominant transport mechanism from spin to charge. Finally, we checked that this nonreciprocal current generation mechanism is robust to the application of dephasing noise as even in the presence of this additional dissipative process the steady-state occupation distributions for the quasiparticle modes of the Hamiltonian remains non-trivial, an essential requirement to obtain non-zero currents.

### [47] [Field-induced first order transitions and phase coexistence in the Kitaev quantum spin liquid candidate BaCo2(AsO4)2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15346)
*Tanner J. Legvold,Bin Gao,Rong-Zhu Lin,Violet Williams,Tong Chen,Dehong Yu,Chien-Lung Huang,Gage Eichman,Renjie Lui,Benedetta Flebus,Pengcheng Dai,Douglas Natelson*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过中子散射（neutron scattering）对 Kitaev 量子自旋液体候选材料 BaCo₂(AsO₄)₂ (BCAO) 在磁场下的自旋激发进行表征，发现场诱导的双 zigzag 到上-上-下（UUD）相变伴随局域化 UUD 自旋激发簇的出现，且 UUD 到铁磁（FM）相变为一阶相变并伴随自旋 Seebeck 系数的尖峰响应。结果不支持 UUD-FM 临界场附近的量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）图像，而建模表明宽激发来源于束缚自旋翻转对，低能色散支则自然解释了自旋 Seebeck 响应的符号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 BaCo₂(AsO₄)₂ (BCAO) 在低温与磁场下丰富的相图，特别是验证在接近极化铁磁（ferromagnetic）相的狭窄场区间内是否存在场诱导量子自旋液相（field-induced quantum spin liquid phase）的提议。

Method: 采用中子散射（neutron scattering）技术表征 BCAO 在磁场下的自旋激发（spin excitation）结构演变，并结合输运（transport）测量（包括自旋 Seebeck 系数）以及理论建模进行综合分析。

Result: 发现双 zigzag 到 UUD 相变伴随局域化 UUD 自旋激发簇（cluster of localized UUD spin excitations）与传统自旋波（spin waves）共存；UUD 到 FM 转变为一阶相变（first-order transition），并出现自旋 Seebeck 系数的尖锐响应；建模表明宽激发源于束缚自旋翻转对（bound spin-flip pairs），而 FM 相界附近的低能色散支携带与 FM 序相同符号的磁化强度。

Conclusion: 实验结果不支持 UUD-FM 临界场附近存在量子自旋液相（quantum spin liquid phase）的解释；观测到的自旋 Seebeck 响应和有限残余热导率可由束缚自旋翻转对及低能色散激发自然解释，而非量子自旋液体的特征。

Abstract: BaCo2(AsO4)2 (BCAO) is an insulating Kitaev quantum spin liquid candidate with a rich low-temperature phase diagram. Below 5 K, it exhibits double-zigzag magnetic order. Upon application of an in-plane magnetic field, the magnetic structure first transforms into an up-up-down (UUD) state near 0.12 T and then enters a fully spin-polarized ferromagnetic (FM) state near 0.5 T. In the narrow field regime close to the polarized phase, a finite residual thermal conductivity has been reported, suggesting a possible field-induced quantum spin liquid phase. Using neutron scattering, we show that the field-induced double-zigzag-to-UUD transition near 0.15 T is accompanied by the emergence of a cluster of localized UUD spin excitations that coexist with conventional spin waves. Upon further increasing field, BCAO undergoes a first-order UUD-to-FM transition with coexistence of UUD and FM phases, accompanied by a sharp response in the spin Seebeck coefficient. These results do not support a quantum spin liquid scenario near the UUD-to-FM critical field. Instead, modeling indicates that the broad excitations arise from bound spin-flip pairs, while a low-lying dispersive branch near the FM phase boundary carries the same sign of magnetization as the FM order. These excitations naturally account for the observed sign of the spin Seebeck response and are likely relevant to the thermal conductivity near the critical field.

### [48] [Data-efficient reconstruction of critical quantum dynamics via blind fractional-envelope extrapolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15458)
*Hyunju Kim,Hyun-Yong Lee,Heung-Sik Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于分数阶微积分（fractional calculus）的包络外推方法（fSD），用于从短时量子动力学模拟数据中可靠地提取临界动力学行为。该方法通过盲选指数α、去除代数尾、残差用有限极点模型拟合，在临界XXZ链和DMFT谱上均优于传统有限极点方法，且不会在非临界系统中虚假地产生幂律行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统的实时动力学模拟常因纠缠增长（entanglement growth）而被限制在短时间尺度。传统的有限极点重建方法（如线性预测）在谱为离散激发集时效果良好，但在临界点（criticality）附近，低能谱呈现为幂律连续谱（power-law continuum），对应一个分支割线（branch cut），有限数目极点无法表示其长时间代数尾（algebraic tail）。因此，需要发展能在短时数据下有效外推临界动力学行为的方法。

Method: 本文提出一种受分数阶微积分启发的包络外推方法。其结构源于分数形式的Schwinger–Dyson方程（fractional Schwinger–Dyson equation, fSD），其中拉普拉斯符号s^α解析地承载分支割线，而残余自能（residual self-energy）保持亚纯（meromorphic）形式。在实际数据处理中，指数α在拟合窗口内盲选，信号经t^α去趋势（detrend），残差用稳定化的有限极点模型拟合，最后恢复代数包络（algebraic envelope）。

Result: 在临界XXZ链（critical XXZ chain）上，该方法（fSD）相比有限极点方法，对短时数据的外推精度通常提高数倍；指数α可在拟合窗口内盲选得到，在弱耦合下与闭式Luttinger值（Luttinger value）吻合。在Δ=1饱和相变点（saturation transition）处，盲搜得到z=2的稀磁振子指数（dilute-magnon exponent）α=1/2。在非临界动力学平均场谱（DMFT）上，低频频响应为正则（regular）情形，fSD不会选择稳定的分数包络，而是退化为标准极点结果，不会产生虚假的幂律行为。

Conclusion: 该分数包络外推方法（fSD）为仅能获得短时间模拟数据时的量子临界动力学（quantum critical dynamics）提供了一条高效、准确的路径。它在临界系统中显著优于传统方法，同时在非临界系统中不会误报幂律行为，具有良好的选择性。

Abstract: Simulating real-time dynamics of quantum systems is often limited to short times by entanglement growth. Finite-pole reconstructions such as linear prediction and related machineries extrapolate such data reliably when the spectrum is a finite set of excitations, but at criticality the low-energy spectrum is a power-law continuum $A(ω)\sim|ω|^{α-1}$ -- a branch cut whose real-time tail $G(t)\sim t^{-α}$ finitely many poles cannot represent. Here we develop a fractional-calculus-motivated envelope extrapolation for such data. Its structure is motivated by a fractional form of Schwinger--Dyson (fSD) equation, in which the Laplace symbol $s^α$ carries the branch cut analytically while the residual self-energy remains meromorphic. On real data we employ the corresponding operational alternative -- the exponent $α$ is selected blindly inside the fit window, the signal is detrended by $t^α$, the residual is fitted by a stabilized finite-pole model, and the algebraic envelope is restored. On the critical XXZ chain this blind fractional-envelope method (fSD for short) extrapolates short-time data typically several-fold more accurately than finite-pole methods, with the exponent $α$ identified blindly from the fit window alone and bracketing the closed-form Luttinger value at weak coupling. The same blind search finds the $z=2$ dilute-magnon exponent $α=1/2$ at the $Δ=1$ saturation transition, and the advantage persists in the gapped free-magnon phase with its sharp band edges. On noncritical dynamical mean-field spectra, whose low-frequency response is regular, fSD by contrast fails to select any stable fractional envelope and reduces to the standard pole result rather than manufacturing a spurious power law, making it an efficient and accurate route to quantum critical dynamics when only short simulation times are accessible.

</details>


### [49] [Topology and compact molecular orbitals in twisted bilayer WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15611)
*Chenyuan Li,Rwik Dutta,Fang Xie,James R. Chelikowsky,Jennifer Cano,Mit H. Naik,Qimiao Si*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理（first-principles）方法构建了扭曲双层WSe₂（tWSe₂）中顶部莫尔价带（moiré valence bands）的描述，发现其具有非平凡拓扑性质（Chern数 C=(+1,+1)），并通过部分Wannier化（partial Wannierization）构造了局域f轨道和拓扑c轨道，为理解该体系中的超导机制和拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）提供了从头算基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲双层WSe₂中观测到的超导现象引发了对其非常规配对机制（unconventional pairing mechanisms）的理论关注，核心问题在于能带拓扑（band topology）是否在关联物理（correlation physics）中扮演关键角色。目前缺乏第一性原理层面的定量描述。

Method: 利用密度泛函理论（DFT）计算分析相关转角范围内顶部价带的拓扑性质。通过部分Wannier化过程，并借助自旋C₃z对称性表示（spinful C₃z symmetry representations），从DFT波函数直接构造紧凑分子轨道（molecular orbitals），提取局域f轨道与互补拓扑c轨道的跃迁和杂化振幅。

Result: 在相关转角范围内，顶部价带具有非平凡拓扑，K谷顶部价带的Chern数为 C=(+1,+1)。通过部分Wannier化成功构造了局域f轨道和拓扑c轨道，并从中提取了从头算的跃迁和杂化参数。

Conclusion: 所获得的参数为有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）提供了第一性原理基准，为理解莫尔过渡金属硫族化物（moiré TMDs）中的超导现象奠定了理论基础，并将tWSe₂凸显为探索拓扑超导的重要平台。

Abstract: Recent observations of superconductivity in twisted bilayer WSe$_2$ (tWSe$_2$) have motivated theoretical proposals for unconventional pairing mechanisms. A central question is whether band topology plays an essential role in the system's correlation physics. In this letter, we develop a first-principles-based description of the top moiré valence bands in tWSe$_2$. Using density functional theory (DFT) calculations, we identify the bands in the relevant range of twist angles to be topologically non-trivial, with the top valence bands carrying Chern numbers $C=(+1,+1)$ for the $K$ valley. In order to treat the strong correlation physics, we construct compact molecular orbitals directly from the DFT wave functions through a partial Wannierization procedure and with the guidance of spinful $C_{3z}$ symmetry representations. This yields a localized $f$ orbital together with a complementary topological $c$ orbital, allowing us to extract hopping and hybridization amplitudes from first principles. The resulting parameters provide an ab initio benchmark for the effective Hamiltonian. Our work establishes a foundation for understanding superconductivity in moiré TMDs and highlights tWSe$_2$ as a promising platform for exploring topological superconductivity.

</details>


### [50] [Machine-learning test of the single-ion model for $dd$ excitations in cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15763)
*Maryia Zinouyeva,Leonardo Martinelli,Riccardo Arpaia,Nicholas B. Brookes,Daniele Di Castro,Kurt Kummer,Floriana Lombardi,Giacomo Merzoni,Francesco Rosa,Alessandro Tarasio,Enrico Tassi,Flora Yakhou-Harris,Ezio Puppin,Marco Moretti Sala,Giacomo Ghiringhelli*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用局域单离子模型框架，分别通过传统全局拟合（global fitting）和基于相同理论框架训练的卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network, CNN）两种方法，对YBa₂Cu₃O₆和La₂CuO₄的RIXS光谱中的dd激发进行分析与比较。

Result: 对于YBa₂Cu₃O₆，两种方法获得的激发态能量一致，能量由低到高依次为xy、3z²−r²、xz/yz顺序。对于La₂CuO₄，两种方法未能收敛到单一解。

Conclusion: 机器学习工具可用于分析以dd激发为主导的RIXS光谱；单离子模型在描述La₂CuO₄的dd激发时存在局限，高能激发可能需要考虑超出局域图像的额外贡献。

Abstract: We investigate $dd$ excitations in Resonant Inelastic X-ray Scattering spectra of YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_6$ and La$_2$CuO$_4$ using the local single-ion model. The data are analyzed by conventional global fitting and by a convolutional neural network trained within the same theoretical framework. For YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_6$, the excited state energies obtained with the two methods coincide, leading to the $xy$, $3z^2-r^2$, $xz/yz$ sequence for increasing energy. This result validates the use of machine learning tools for the analysis of RIXS spectra dominated by $dd$ excitations. By contrast, for La$_2$CuO$_4$, the two methods do not converge to a single solution, revealing the limitations of the single-ion model in describing $dd$ excitations in cuprates and pointing to the role of additional contributions beyond a purely local picture in shaping high-energy excitations.

### [51] [Thermal Order by Disorder in Resonating-Valence Bond States on the Checkerboard Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15813)
*Giorgi Gogaberishvili,Nika Kurdadze,Kirill Shtengel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在棋盘格点（checkerboard lattice）上推导出一个局域自旋-1/2哈密顿量（local spin-1/2 Hamiltonian），其基态为共振价键态（resonating valence bond state），并发现该基态中单态-单态关联呈指数衰减，而二聚体-二聚体关联在对应的量子二聚体模型（Quantum Dimer model）中呈幂律衰减；由此提出一种新的热致有序化（thermal Order by Disorder）机制，即热退相干抑制基态中不同关联贡献之间的破坏性量子干涉，从而形成具有准长程有序（quasi-long-range ordered）的混合态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索棋盘格点自旋系统中共振价键态（RVB state）的关联性质，并揭示量子与热涨落之间相互作用所导致的新型有序化机制。

Method: 从局域自旋-1/2哈密顿量出发，构建共振价键基态，并将其与对应的量子二聚体模型进行关联性质比较，进而分析热退相干对量子干涉的抑制效应。

Result: 单态-单态关联呈指数衰减，而二聚体-二聚体关联在量子二聚体模型中呈幂律衰减；热退相干通过抑制破坏性量子干涉，诱导出准长程有序的混合态。

Conclusion: 提出一种新的热致有序化机制，揭示了热涨落并非仅破坏量子有序，还能通过抑制量子干涉导致与基态定性不同的准长程有序相。

Abstract: We derive a local spin-1/2 Hamiltonian with a resonating valence bond ground state on the checkerboard lattice. The state is characterized by the exponential decay of singlet-singlet correlations, whereas dimer-dimer correlations decay with a power law in the corresponding Quantum Dimer model. This observation leads to a novel mechanism for thermal Order by Disorder whereby thermal decoherence suppresses destructive quantum interference between different contributions to the correlations in the ground state and results in a qualitatively different, quasi-long-range ordered mixed state.

</details>


### [52] [Altermagnetism without a long-range order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15954)
*V. E. Valiulin,A. V. Mikheyenkov,K. I. Kugel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过旋转不变格林函数方法研究Kugel-Khomskii自旋-赝自旋模型，证明在无长程磁序或轨道序的条件下，系统中仍可出现具有节点线的复合态，从而建立“交变磁顺磁体”（altermagnetic paramagnet）或“交变磁液体”（altermagnetic liquid）的新概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kugel-Khomskii自旋-赝自旋模型（spin-pseudospin model）最初用于描述具有轨道自由度的过渡金属化合物，近期被重新诠释于交变磁性（altermagnetism）的语境中。本文旨在理论上探究在无长程磁序或轨道序情况下交变磁行为的出现机制。

Method: 采用适用于SU(2)×SU(2)对称模型的旋转不变格林函数方法（rotation-invariant Green's function method），在方形晶格（square lattice）和线性链（linear chain）上分析自旋-自旋以及自旋-赝自旋关联函数、激发谱、热容和磁化率。

Result: 当超越临界子系间交换作用Kc(T)时，出现具有非零自旋-赝自旋关联的复合态，尽管每个格点上的平均自旋和赝自旋为零。激发谱分裂为声学支和光学支，并沿qx = qy方向出现节点线（nodal lines），此为交变磁对称性的直接特征。在相界处观察到热容峰和磁化率跳变。在一维情况下，相界呈非单调行为并表现出再入相变（reentrant transition）。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了“交变磁顺磁体”或“交变磁液体”的概念，即一种无长程序但仍具交变磁对称性的状态，对低维和强涨落系统具有重要参考价值。

Abstract: The Kugel-Khomskii spin-pseudospin model, originally developed for transition-metal compounds with orbital degrees of freedom, has recently been reinterpreted in the context of altermagnetism. In this work, we theoretically investigate the emergence of altermagnetic behavior in the absence of long-range magnetic or orbital order. Using the rotation-invariant Green's function method for the SU(2) x SU(2) symmetric model on a square lattice and on a linear chain, we analyze spin-spin and spin-pseudospin correlation functions, excitation spectra, heat capacity, and susceptibilities. We show that beyond a critical intersubsystem exchange Kc(T), a composite state arises with nonzero spin-pseudospin correlations, even though the average spin and pseudospin at each site are zero. The excitation spectrum splits into acoustic and optical branches, with nodal lines along qx = qy - a direct signature of altermagnetic symmetry. A peak in heat capacity and a jump in susceptibility are observed at the phase boundary. In 1D, the phase boundary is nonmonotonic and demonstrates reentrant transition. These results establish the concept of an "altermagnetic paramagnet" or "altermagnetic liquid" without long-range order, relevant for low-dimensional and strongly fluctuating systems.

### [53] [Deconfined quantum critical point in a dissipative spin-1/2 chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16039)
*Longye Lu,Shifeng Cui,Wenan Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过分析自旋-1/2 J-Q₃链与玻色子热库耦合的开放量子自旋系统，发现强耗散能稳定反铁磁相，且在亚欧姆和欧姆耗散下可发生连续的反铁磁-价键固体相变，其中欧姆情形出现自旋子退禁闭和涌现O(4)对称性，亚欧姆情形也可能存在自旋子退禁闭，超欧姆情形则预测从反铁磁相到准长程序相的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索开放量子自旋系统是否能够提供实现退禁闭量子临界性（deconfined quantum criticality）的新途径，这是之前尚未被充分研究的领域。

Method: 采用非阿贝尔玻色子化（non-Abelian bosonization）和重整化群（renormalization-group, RG）分析，并结合大规模量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）模拟，确定模型的相图和相变行为。

Result: 强耗散在亚欧姆、欧姆和超欧姆三种热库下均能稳定反铁磁（AFM）相；在亚欧姆和欧姆耗散区，增大多自旋相互作用可引发连续的反铁磁-价键固体（AFM-VBS）相变；欧姆临界点具有自旋子退禁闭（spinon deconfinement）和涌现O(4)对称性；亚欧姆情形中若自旋子在耗散VBS相中保持退禁闭，则相变也可能涉及自旋子退禁闭；超欧姆区则预测存在从AFM相到准长程序相的转变。

Conclusion: 开放量子自旋系统为退禁闭量子临界性提供了新的实现平台，欧姆和亚欧姆耗散均可支持连续AFM-VBS相变，且临界行为与自旋子退禁闭和涌现对称性密切相关。

Abstract: Open quantum spin systems offer a previously unexplored route to realizing deconfined quantum criticality. We consider a spin-1/2 $J$-$Q_3$ chain, consisting of an antiferromagnetic (AFM) Heisenberg exchange and a competing multi-spin interaction favoring a valence-bond solid (VBS) state, with each spin component coupled to a bosonic bath. Using non-Abelian bosonization and renormalization-group (RG) analysis, combined with large-scale quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) simulations, we determine the phase diagram and the associated phase transitions of the model. We show that strong dissipation stabilizes an AFM phase for sub-Ohmic, Ohmic, and super-Ohmic baths. Continuous AFM-VBS transitions at finite dissipation are found upon increasing the multi-spin interaction in both the sub-Ohmic and Ohmic regimes. Critical properties are obtained through perturbative RG analysis and QMC simulations. In the Ohmic case, the critical point features spinon deconfinement and emergent O(4) symmetry. In the sub-Ohmic regime, the transition may also involve spinon deconfinement, provided that spinons remain deconfined in the dissipative VBS phase. In addition, in the super-Ohmic regime, we propose a transition from AFM phase to a quasi-long-range ordered phase.

</details>


### [54] [Quantum Fisher information of magnetic quantum phase transition on Kondo lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16150)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异金属（strange metals）作为高度集体的量子多体系统，需要新的表征手段，量子信息方法具有很大潜力。作者旨在利用量子信息工具，特别是QFI，来刻画此类系统中多体纠缠的性质及其与量子相变的关系。

Method: 对近藤晶格模型计算横向量子Fisher信息，分析其在量子相变中的行为；辅以反铁磁海森堡模型（antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model）的解析分析阐明物理起源；提出利用极化与非极化非弹性中子散射实验进行验证的方案。

Conclusion: 不同多体系统算符不仅可用于见证不同扇区中的多体纠缠，还能阐明相图不同区域的整体物理。建议在重费米子相图的有序部分通过极化与非极化非弹性中子散射进行实验检验。

Abstract: Strange metals exemplify highly collective quantum many-body systems that call for new means of characterization, and there is considerable potential for quantum information approaches contributing to the cause. We investigate multipartite entanglement across the quantum phase transition of a Kondo lattice model using the quantum Fisher information (QFI). We show that the QFI associated with the spin components transverse to the order parameter characterizes the destruction of heavy quasiparticles in the Kondo-destroyed magnetic-ordered phase. The physical origin of this observation is elucidated through an analysis of the antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model. We propose to test the results in terms of both unpolarized and polarized inelastic neutron scattering measurements in the ordered part of the heavy fermion phase diagram. Our findings illustrate how different operators of a many-body system can be employed to not only witness multipartite entanglement in different sectors and but also elucidate the overall physics across different parts of the phase diagram.

### [55] [Circulation Statistics in Rayleigh-Bénard Convection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15489)
*Giovanni Saisse,Roshan J. Samuel,Luca Moriconi,Jörg Schumacher,Katepalli R. Sreenivasan*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究通过直接数值模拟（direct numerical simulation, DNS）探究瑞利-贝纳德对流（Rayleigh-Bénard convection）中速度环量（velocity circulation）的统计性质，发现其在热边界层（thermal boundary layer, TBL）内与温度场强相关、涡核纵横比统计显著改变，但在平行于壁面的平面上仍满足均匀各向同性湍流（HIT）中观测到的面积规则（Area Rule）；远离边界层后，统计行为回归HIT特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来均匀各向同性湍流（HIT）中速度环量的重要统计性质已被揭示，但尚不清楚这些性质是否在其他湍流类型中保持不变或被修正。由于小尺度结构在HIT环量涨落中占主导地位，本研究旨在检验其在瑞利-贝纳德对流（Rayleigh-Bénard convection）中的相关性。

Method: 对瑞利数为$10^9$、普朗特数（Prandtl number）为$O(1)$的瑞利-贝纳德对流进行直接数值模拟（DNS），分析热边界层（TBL）内外的速度环量统计性质，包括基本涡旋分布、涡核纵横比、概率分布函数及面积规则（Area Rule）的适用性。

Result: 在热边界层（TBL）内，基本涡旋分布与温度场强相关，涡核纵横比统计显著改变；平行于壁面的平面轮廓的环量概率分布函数呈现与HIT高度相似的特征，面积规则（Area Rule）除可能的过渡区域（距离几个TBL厚度）外依然成立。远离TBL的区域，统计行为总体上与HIT类似，小涡管间歇性空间分布由能量耗散场决定。

Conclusion: 瑞利-贝纳德对流中速度环量的统计性质在远离边界层时基本恢复HIT特征，而在热边界层（TBL）内受到温度场的显著调制，但面积规则（Area Rule）在大多数情况下仍然成立，表明该规则可能具有跨湍流类型的普适性。

Abstract: Important statistical properties of velocity circulation in homogeneous isotropic turbulence (HIT) have been unveiled in recent years, raising the question of whether they persist, or are modified, in other classes of turbulent flows. Motivated by the dominant role of small-scale structures in the circulation fluctuations of HIT, we investigate their relevance in direct numerical simulations of Rayleigh-Bénard convection at a Rayleigh number of $10^9$ and Prandtl number of $O(1)$. Within the thermal boundary layer (TBL), the distribution of elementary vortices is found to be strongly correlated with the temperature field, while the statistics of their core aspect ratios is significantly altered. Additionally, the probability distribution functions of circulation, computed for planar contours which are parallel to the walls, display salient features closely akin to those observed in HIT, with the {\it Area Rule} (a connection between circulation statistics and minimal surfaces) remaining particularly well satisfied -- except for a possible transitional region at a distance of a few TBL thicknesses. Away from the TBL, as expected, the overall statistical behavior of these structures likewise resembles that of HIT, where the intermittent spatial distribution of small vortex tubes is instead determined by the energy dissipation field.

</details>

### [56] [First-Order Topological FFLO Transition and Superconducting Diode Sign Reversal in Altermagnetic Nanowires](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15720)
*Bo Fu,Kaizhi Bai,Chang-An Li,Shun-Qing Shen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出在自旋-轨道耦合纳米线中，通过零净磁化（zero net magnetization）的 d 波交错磁体（d-wave altermagnet）实现拓扑 Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov (FFLO) 态，该转变是一级相变（first-order transition），并伴随超导二极管效应的尖锐符号反转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的FFLO态通常由有限磁化驱动、通过二级相变（second-order phase transition）产生；本文旨在探索一种无需净磁化、由交错磁体（altermagnet）诱导的拓扑FFLO态实现方案。

Method: 采用 Ginzburg-Landau 理论分析交错磁体近邻化自旋-轨道耦合纳米线中的配对机制，研究交错磁场如何产生能带分辨的竞争配对通道，并构建双谷自由能景观（double-valley free energy landscape）。

Result: 交错磁场导致自由能全局最小值发生不连续切换，从而引发一级拓扑FFLO相变，伴随库珀对振幅（Cooper pairing amplitude）和有限质心动量（finite center-of-mass momentum）的跳跃。该不连续拓扑重构显著增强二极管效率，并在相变处产生尖锐的符号反转。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种无需外加磁场、基于交错磁体的拓扑FFLO态实现路线，并识别出其直接输运指纹——超导二极管效应的符号反转。

Abstract: Fulde-Ferrell-Larkin-Ovchinnikov (FFLO) state conventionally emerges via a second-order phase transition driven by finite magnetization. Here we show that a spin-orbit-coupled nanowire proximitized to $d$-wave altermagnets -- with zero net magnetization -- can realize topological FFLO states through a first-order transition, marked by a sharp sign-reversing superconducting diode effect. The altermagnetic field generates band-resolved competing pairing channels, giving rise to a double-valley free energy landscape whose global minimum switches discontinuously. It consequently leads to a first-order topological FFLO transition with simultaneous jumps in the Cooper pairing amplitude and finite center-of-mass momentum. Remarkably, this discontinuous topological reconfiguration substantially enhances the diode efficiency and drives a characteristic sharp sign reversal across the transition. The mechanism of such exotic phenomena is captured by Ginzburg--Landau theory. Our results provide a field-free altermagnetic route to topological FFLO states and identify their direct transport fingerprint.

*Yayi Lin,Marc Neis,Marcello Pio Guardascione,Janine Lorenz,Thomas J. Smart,F. Stefan Tautz,Felix Lüpke,Frederik Bolle,Martin Dressel,Rami Barends,Pavel A. Bushev,Marc Scheffler*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模超导量子技术（如量子计算）中，晶圆级超导薄膜的均匀性对器件性能的一致性至关重要，因此需要一种能够在光刻前对整片晶圆进行快速、无损评估的方法。

Method: 采用太赫兹（THz）光谱技术，对通过等离子体增强磁控溅射（plasma-enhanced magnetron sputtering）生长的4英寸和6英寸硅晶圆上的一系列铌钛氮（NbTiN）薄膜进行表征：在室温下对整片晶圆进行映射测量，并在低温下对代表性片段进行表征。

Conclusion: 该太赫兹映射技术证明了在光刻前评估晶圆级超导薄膜的可行性，有助于为可重复的器件制备准备薄膜。

Abstract: For large-scale superconducting quantum technology, e.g. quantum computing, the homogeneity of wafer-scale superconducting thin films is vital for consistent performance of the fabricated devices. Terahertz (THz) spectroscopy as a contactless and non-destructive measurement technique is a powerful tool to characterize the superconducting films. In this work, a set of niobium titanium nitride (NbTiN) thin films on 4-inch and 6-inch silicon wafers, grown via plasma-enhanced magnetron sputtering, are investigated via THz spectroscopy: full wafers are mapped at room temperatures and exemplary segments are characterized at cryogenic temperatures. The deviations in observed sheet resistance depend on the used deposition device and the film thickness. While the deviations in superconducting sheet kinetic inductance match those of the normal-state sheet resistance, the critical temperature and energy gap exhibit little variation. This THz mapping technique demonstrates the feasibility of evaluating wafer-scale superconducting thin films before lithography, facilitating preparation of the thin films for reproducible device fabrication.

Abstract: We present a full numerical solution of the Migdal--Eliashberg equations for the jellium model of phonon-mediated superconductivity. We find very low critical temperatures below 1~K, in contrast to earlier claims that the jellium model for hydrogen solids might reach room-temperature superconductivity. Our results suggest that full momentum and frequency dependence of the gap function and normal self-energy should be taken into account for accurate $T_c$ estimates.

### [59] [Coherent driving of displacive Higgs fluctuations in superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16055)
*Jacopo Fiore,Irene Zanotti,Kota Katsumi,N. P. Armitage,Claudio Castellani,Goetz Seibold,Lara Benfatto*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文发现超导体中强太赫兹激光脉冲可通过位移激发（displacive excitation）机制（类似于不透明材料中相干声子的位移激发）非线性地驱动希格斯模（Higgs mode），并通过数值模拟、解析结果以及s波NbN实验验证了该机制在s波和d波超导体中的有效性，为利用强太赫兹场测量和控制超导集体自由度提供了新视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究强相位稳定太赫兹（terahertz, THz）激光脉冲如何通过多光子激发途径（multi-photon excitation pathways）以不同于线性响应中标准共振机制的方式相干驱动集体模（collective modes），特别是在超导体中非线性光学响应的增强机制。

Method: 结合数值模拟（numerical simulations）与解析结果（analytical results），并在s波超导体NbN中通过非线性第一谐波（nonlinear first harmonic）的相位温度依赖性进行实验验证。

Result: 位移激发机制（displacive mechanism）在s波和d波超导体中均可有效激发希格斯模；实验上通过s波NbN中非线性第一谐波相位的温度依赖性验证了该预测。

Conclusion: 结果表明，强太赫兹场有能力测量并最终控制超导光学响应对集体自由度（collective degrees of freedom）的参数依赖性，为非线性超导光学提供了新视角。

Abstract: Intense phase-stable terahertz (THz) laser pulses can drive collective modes coherently via multi-photon excitation pathways in a manner different than the standard resonant mechanism operative in linear response. Here we show that in superconductors the nonlinear optical response can be enhanced when excited quasiparticles activate a (non-resonant) static displacement of the superconducting order parameter, in full analogy with the displacive excitation of coherent phonons in opaque materials. By combining numerical simulations with analytical results we demonstrate that the displacive mechanism to excite the Higgs mode is operative in both $s$-wave and $d$-wave superconductors. We validate this prediction experimentally by the temperature dependence of the phase of the nonlinear first harmonic in superconducting $s$-wave NbN. We also discuss how the order-parameter relaxation at large times, which can be experimentally accessed via pump-probe protocols is connected to energy-dissipative processes. Our results offer a novel perspective on the ability of intense THz fields to measure, and eventually control, the parametric dependence of the optical response on collective degrees of freedom.

### [60] [Fragmented ETH: Prethermalization, Timescales, and Ensemble Inequivalence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15350)
*C. L. Sriram,Soumya Kanti Pal,Lea F. Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有强长程相互作用的有限量子系统趋近热平衡的动力学过程，发现近守恒量导致希尔伯特空间碎裂（Hilbert space fragmentation）和能带结构，从而引发缓慢的两阶段热化。通过微扰理论给出了预热平台（prethermal plateau）的高度与时间尺度，并提出了碎片化本征态热化假说（fragmented eigenstate thermalization hypothesis, fETH），揭示了能带分辨的热化机制及其对平衡态统计力学中系综不等价性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示强长程相互作用有限量子系统中热化过程的微观机制，特别是希尔伯特空间碎裂如何影响系统趋近热平衡的动力学与统计力学行为。

Method: 采用微扰理论（perturbative theory）推导预热平台的高度与时间尺度；通过能带内部的量子混沌（quantum chaos）分析定义带内微正则系综（microcanonical ensembles），并提出碎片化本征态热化假说（fETH）。

Result: 系统表现出缓慢的两阶段热化过程，存在长寿命预热平台；该行为并非普遍，取决于可观测量与初始态的选择。fETH 中的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）受对称性选择定则（symmetry-imposed selection rule）约束，限制了可比较的系统尺寸；微正则系综局限于单一能带，而正则系综涉及多能带混合，导致系综不等价性（ensemble inequivalence）。

Conclusion: 碎片化本征态热化假说（fETH）为强长程相互作用系统中的非遍历热化提供了统一框架，并解释了系综不等价性的起源，适用于一大类具有希尔伯特空间碎裂的哈密顿量。

Abstract: We investigate how finite quantum systems with strong long-range interactions approach thermal equilibrium. Nearly conserved quantities inherited from the fully connected limit fragment the Hilbert space and give rise to a many-body spectrum split into energy bands. As a result, equilibration becomes anomalously slow and proceeds through long-lived prethermal plateaus. This two-stage equilibration process is, however, not universal. We uncover the mechanism that determines which observables and initial states exhibit, or evade, prethermal plateaus. We also develop a perturbative theory that provides analytical expressions for both the height of the prethermal plateau and its timescale. Despite the lack of global ergodicity, quantum chaos develops within individual energy bands, enabling the definition of microcanonical ensembles within the bands. This supports a band-resolved formulation of thermalization, which we term fragmented eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (fETH). Unlike conventional ETH, finite-size scaling in fETH obeys a symmetry-imposed selection rule that restricts which system sizes can be compared. This band-resolved description has direct consequences for equilibrium statistical mechanics. While microcanonical ensembles remain confined to a single band, canonical ensembles mix different bands. This mismatch explains ensemble inequivalence without invoking equilibrium phase transitions. Our results apply to a broad class of Hamiltonians exhibiting Hilbert-space fragmentation.

</details>


### [61] [Scaling regimes of the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation from the functional renormalization group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15784)
*Liubov Gosteva,Nicolás Wschebor,Léonie Canet*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文重新审视一维随机Kuramoto-Sivashinsky（KS）方程的重整化群（RG）方法，指出基于尖锐截断（sharp cutoff）的微扰Wilson RG方法存在内在发散问题，转而采用光滑截断（smooth cutoff）的函数重整化群（FRG）框架。FRG流方程表明KS模型在大尺度流向Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）不动点；计算全两点关联函数后，发现了三个普适标度区：KPZ区（动力学指数z=3/2）、Edwards-Wilkinson区（z=2）和最近发现的无粘区（z=1）。此外，还研究了确定性KS方程在大尺度下的行为以及KPZ区在确定性情形的出现尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去的微扰Wilson RG方法应用于一维随机KS方程时，虽然得到了定性正确的图像，但存在内在发散问题——尖锐截断下的动量导数在某些情况下没有良定义。因此需要引入更严格的FRG框架来纠正这一缺陷并建立正确的流方程。

Method: 采用光滑截断（smooth cutoff）的函数重整化群（FRG）框架，替代原来有问题的尖锐截断（sharp cutoff）Wilson RG方法，建立KS模型的流方程，并计算完整的动量-频率空间两点关联函数。

Result: FRG流方程表明KS模型在大尺度流向KPZ不动点；两点关联函数展现了三个普适标度区：KPZ区（z=3/2）、Edwards-Wilkinson区（z=2）和无粘区（z=1，由有效粘度的消失导致，出现在大波数范围）。确定性KS方程在噪音趋于零的极限下，也确定了KPZ区能够出现的特征尺度。

Conclusion: 光滑截断的FRG框架能够有效解决之前尖锐截断Wilson RG方法在KS方程中的发散问题，提供了更可靠的RG分析；KS模型在大尺度上流向KPZ普适类，且其关联函数包含多个普适标度行为，包括新发现的无粘区。

Abstract: We revisit the renormalization group (RG) approach to the one-dimensional stochastic Kuramoto-Sivashinsky (KS) equation and show that previous approaches based on perturbative Wilsonian RG with a sharp cutoff are not valid, even though they yield a qualitatively correct picture. The reason is that taking momentum derivatives while using the sharp cutoff is not well-defined in some cases and leads to intrinsic divergencies. This is a well-known problem of Wilsonian RG, which can be simply cured by using a smooth cutoff, and employing the functional renormalization group (FRG) framework. We establish the flow equations for the KS model within the FRG, and demonstrate that it flows to the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) fixed point at large scales. We then calculate the full two-point correlation function over a wide range of momenta and frequencies. We show that it exhibits three universal scaling regimes that we characterize: the KPZ regime (with dynamical exponent $z=3/2$), the Edwards-Wilkinson regime (with $z=2$) and the recently discovered inviscid regime (with $z=1$). The latter develops over an extended range of large wavenumbers and originates from the vanishing of the effective viscosity. Lastly, we investigate the large-scale behavior of the deterministic KS equation by studying the limit of vanishing noise and we determine the scales where the KPZ regime can emerge in the deterministic case.

</details>


### [62] [Ultrametric organization of energy landscapes on random Erdős--Rényi graphs: topological origin of barrier hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15902)
*A. P. Zubarev*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究稀疏随机 Erdős–Rényi 图上能量景观的超度量（ultrametric）组织结构，通过构建动力学马氏距离（kinetic Mahalanobis metric）并证明其在大能量展宽极限下收敛于经典单链超度量，表明超度量性是具有崎岖能量景观的稀疏局部树状网络的普适性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究稀疏随机图上能量景观是否具有超度量组织（ultrametric organization），以及这种结构的出现条件与极限行为。

Method: 在 Erdős–Rényi 图上为每个顶点赋予均匀分布的随机自由能（展宽 $ΔF$），使用 Kramers 过渡速率（Kramers transition rates）建模马尔可夫过程（Markov process）；通过速率矩阵（rate matrix）的谱分解（spectral decomposition）构建吸引子间（basins of attraction）的动力学马氏距离（kinetic Mahalanobis metric）。

Result: 对 $V=5000$ 顶点、$E=5000$ 边的计算实验显示：非平凡超度量度（nontrivial ultrametricity）从 $ΔF=10$ kJ/mol 时的约 42% 单调递增至 $ΔF=1000$ kJ/mol 时的约 96%。证明极限定理：当 $ΔF→∞$ 时，该距离的对数渐近行为逐点收敛于经典单链超度量（single-linkage ultrametric），有限 $ΔF$ 下的次优路径修正随 $ΔF$ 增大呈指数压制。

Conclusion: 在大能量展宽极限下，稀疏局部树状网络上的崎岖能量景观普遍呈现超度量结构。

Abstract: We investigate the ultrametric organization of energy landscapes defined on sparse random Erdős--Rényi graphs. Each graph vertex is assigned a random free energy from a uniform distribution over an interval of width $ΔF$, and the kinetics are modeled by a Markov process with Kramers transition rates. Using spectral decomposition of the rate matrix, we construct a kinetic Mahalanobis metric between basins of attraction. Computational experiments for graphs with $V=5000$ vertices and $E=5000$ edges show that the degree of nontrivial ultrametricity increases monotonically from $\approx42\%$ for $ΔF=10$ kJ/mol to $\approx96\%$ for $ΔF=1000$ kJ/mol. We prove a limit theorem: as $ΔF\to\infty$, the logarithmic asymptotics of this metric converge pointwise to the classical single-linkage ultrametric. For finite $ΔF$, corrections from suboptimal paths are exponentially suppressed with increasing $ΔF$, so that the metric becomes asymptotically ultrametric. Our results suggest that ultrametricity is a universal property of sparse, locally tree-like networks with rugged energy landscapes in the limit of large energy spreads.

</details>


### [63] [Zigzag ordering, defects, and anomalous relaxation in antiferromagnetic Kuramoto lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15911)
*Priyanka D. Bhoyar,Prashant M. Gade*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究具有负最近邻耦合的Kuramoto振子（Kuramoto oscillators）的非平衡有序动力学。负耦合诱导锯齿状反铁磁序：一维中缺陷密度呈异常缓慢粗化（$D(t)\sim t^{-1/4}$），饱和时间标度$t_c(N)\sim N^2$，局域持续概率呈拉伸指数形式（$P(t)\sim\exp(-c t^{1/4})$）。这些指数与耦合强度无关，构成独特的普适类（universality class）。二维中几何阻挫（geometric frustration）抑制完全有序，产生长寿命亚稳态畴壁结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究确定性非线性动力学和几何阻挫本身是否足以产生慢弛豫（slow relaxation）和反常标度行为（anomalous scaling），而不需要淬火无序（quenched disorder）或随机噪声。

Method: 采用耦合Kuramoto振子模型，设置负最近邻耦合以引入几何阻挫；通过数值模拟获取一维和二维系统中的缺陷密度与局域持续概率的时序演化；利用连续近似和粗粒化偏微分方程进行理论解释，并借助线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）说明锯齿有序态的涌现机制。

Result: 一维中缺陷密度按$t^{-1/4}$衰减后饱和，饱和时间$t_c\sim N^2$；局域持续概率为拉伸指数$P(t)\sim\exp(-c t^{1/4})$。这些指数$\alpha=\delta=1/4$与$z=2$共同构成独特普适类，且耦合强度仅改变特征时间尺度。二维中阻挫抑制完全有序，形成长寿命亚稳态畴壁结构，缺陷密度在初始瞬态衰减后交叉饱和。

Conclusion: 确定性非线性动力学与几何阻挫即可产生慢弛豫和反常标度，无需随机性因素的引入；阻挫与连续相变量（continuous phase variables）能从根本上修改粗化动力学（coarsening dynamics），在确定性多体系统中生成异常缓慢的弛豫过程。

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium ordering dynamics of coupled Kuramoto oscillators with negative nearest-neighbor coupling, which induces a zigzag antiferromagnetic ordering. In one dimension, the defect density exhibits anomalously slow coarsening, decaying as $(D(t)\sim t^{-1/4})$ before saturating at a system-size-dependent time $(t_c(N)\sim N^z)$ with (z=2). The local persistence probability follows a stretched-exponential form, $(P(t)\sim \exp(-c t^α))$, with $(α=1/4)$. These exponents are observed are independent of the magnitude of the coupling, which merely rescales the characteristic time scale. The equality $(α=δ=1/4)$ together with (z=2) is consistent with a distinct universality class. These results demonstrate that deterministic nonlinear dynamics and geometric frustration alone are sufficient to generate slow relaxation and anomalous scaling, without quenched disorder or stochastic noise. A continuum approximation and the corresponding coarse-grained partial differential equation provide a theoretical explanation for the observed anomalous exponents, while linear stability analysis accounts for the emergence of the zigzag ordered state. In two dimensions, geometric frustration inhibits complete ordering and gives rise to long-lived metastable domain-wall structures. An initial transient defect decay is observed before crossover and saturation. These results demonstrate how frustration and continuous phase variables can fundamentally modify coarsening dynamics and generate anomalously slow relaxation in deterministic many-body systems.

</details>


### [64] [Nonequilibrium thermodynamics of feedback-control: a phase-space perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16186)
*José A. Almanza-Marrero*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了包含奇异情况的一般反馈控制系统的涨落关系（fluctuation relations），引入“不可用信息”（unavailable information）的概念，并通过有限分辨率的Szilard引擎（Szilard engine）说明，即使测量获取的信息发散，可提取功（extractable work）仍然有限，原因是同等发散量的信息变得不可用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的麦克斯韦妖（Maxwell demon）问题假设妖能够访问系统的整个相空间（phase space），但这一假设在许多实际应用中不成立，因此需要更一般的理论框架来处理有限信息或奇异情况。

Method: 推导了一般反馈控制系统的涨落关系，包括奇异情况（singular cases）；提出一种广义的“不可用信息”作为核心量，它代表已获取信息中无法用于提取有用功的部分；通过有限分辨率的Szilard引擎进行数值示例验证。

Result: 在有限分辨率Szilard引擎的高分辨率极限下，妖获取的信息可能发散，但可提取功仍然保持有限；同时，不可用信息也发散至同等程度，从而解释了功有限的原因。

Conclusion: 即使测量获取的信息量发散，由于同样发散量的信息变为不可用，系统可提取的功仍保持有限，这揭示了信息与热力学功之间更为精细的平衡关系。

Abstract: Maxwell demons can convert knowledge into thermodynamic advantage by using measurement-acquired information. However, standard formulations of this problem assume that the demon has access to the system's entire phase space, an assumption that fails in many practical applications. Here, I address this problem by deriving fluctuation relations for general feedback-controlled systems, including such singular cases. The central quantity is a generalized notion of unavailable information: a portion of the acquired information that cannot be used to extract useful work. Finally, a Szilard engine with finite resolution illustrates these results. In the high-resolution limit, the information acquired by the demon may diverge, yet the extractable work remains finite. This work shows that this occurs because an equally divergent amount of information becomes unavailable.

</details>

### [65] [The $α$-states of a string worldsheet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15336)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将弦振幅的世界面（worldsheet）描述重新诠释为婴儿宇宙场论（baby universe field theory），确定了拓扑弦论（topological string theory）——即赫维茨世界面（Hurwitz worldsheet）的α态（α-states）。研究发现，这些α态与哈特尔-霍金态（Hartle-Hawking state）的关系蕴含了对称群渐近表示论（asymptotic representation theory）的基础性结论。在全息对偶（holographic dual）中，结果表征了团簇分解关联子（cluster-decomposing correlators）系综的伪随机性质（pseudorandom nature）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在将弦振幅的世界面描述重新诠释为婴儿宇宙场论，并在此框架下确定拓扑弦论的α态，以揭示其与哈特尔-霍金态的关系所蕴含的对称群渐近表示论基础性结论。

Method: 采用世界面描述向婴儿宇宙场论的重新诠释（reinterpretation）作为理论框架，通过分析赫维茨世界面来确定拓扑弦论的α态。

Result: 确定了拓扑弦论（赫维茨世界面）的α态，并发现其与哈特尔-霍金态的关系蕴含着对称群渐近表示论的基础性结论。在全息对偶中，结果刻画了团簇分解关联子系综的伪随机性质。

Conclusion: α态与哈特尔-霍金态之间的关联为对称群渐近表示论提供了基础性见解；同时，该结果在全息对偶中揭示了团簇分解关联子系综的伪随机性特征。

Abstract: The worldsheet description of string amplitudes can be reinterpreted as a baby universe field theory. Under this reinterpretation, we determine the $α$-states of a topological string theory: the Hurwitz worldsheet. We find that their relation to the Hartle--Hawking state encodes foundational results in the asymptotic representation theory of the symmetric group. In the holographic dual, our results characterize the pseudorandom nature of an ensemble of cluster-decomposing correlators.

### [66] [On conformal symmetry in large-$N$ quiver mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15348)
*Andrea De Marco,Mustafa Mullahasanoglu,Joris Raeymaekers,Paolo Rossi,Gizem Sengör*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用局域化技术（localization techniques）导出并解释超共形箭矢指标（superconformal quiver index）的不动点公式，重点研究循环阿贝尔箭矢（cyclic abelian quivers）在大N极限下的行为，揭示了之前库仑支（Coulomb branch）上不可见的微观标度BPS指标（microscopic scaling BPS index）贡献，为AdS₂/CFT₁对偶的弦论实现提供了新步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AdS₂/CFT₁全息对偶中，极端超对称黑洞的微观描述仍然难以捉摸，尽管近极端黑洞物理的统计描述已取得进展。Denef的箭矢力学（quiver mechanics）描述的共形对称性（conformal symmetry）被超势修正（superpotential corrections）破坏，其意义尚不明确，因此需要澄清这一问题。

Method: 采用局域化技术（localization techniques）推导并解释超共形箭矢指标的不动点公式（fixed-point formula）。研究对象聚焦于循环阿贝尔箭矢（cyclic abelian quivers），并在箭矢规范群秩N趋于无穷大的大N极限下进行分析。

Result: 在特定大N极限下，不动点位于共形描述可靠的区域。所得到的超共形指标表达式精确捕捉了Beaujard, Mondal and Pioline推导的微观标度BPS指标（microscopic scaling BPS index）的一个贡献，该贡献此前在库仑支（Coulomb branch）上不可见。

Conclusion: 本研究的发现有望为AdS₂/CFT₁对偶提供一种弦论实现（stringy realization）的新途径。

Abstract: The microscopic description of extremal supersymmetric black holes in AdS$_2$/CFT$_1$ holography has remained elusive despite recent progress in the statistical description of near-extremal black hole physics. In this work we revisit Denef's quiver mechanics description of D-brane bound states in the Coulomb branch, which displays an emergent conformal symmetry in the AdS$_2$ scaling limit. This conformal symmetry is however broken by superpotential corrections near the locus where the Coulomb and Higgs branches meet, and its significance has so far remained unclear. In order to to clarify this issue, we derive and interpret a fixed-point formula for the superconformal quiver index using localization techniques. Focusing on cyclic abelian quivers, we show that, in a certain large-$N$ limit (with the rank $N$ of the quiver gauge group), the fixed points are located in the regime where the conformal description is reliable. In this limit, our expression for the superconformal index precisely captures a contribution to the microscopic scaling BPS index derived by Beaujard, Mondal and Pioline, which was hitherto not visible on the Coulomb branch. Our results are hoped to provide a step towards a stringy realization of AdS$_2$/CFT$_1$ duality.

### [67] [Non-abelian asymmetric orbifolds with vanishing one-loop vacuum energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15349)
*Bernardo Fraiman,Vittorio Larotonda,Michelangelo Tartaglia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对四维非超对称Type II环面轨形（toroidal orbifold）进行了部分分类，要求点群（point group）为非阿贝尔旋转群，且单圈弦微扰论中真空能为零。分类限制于点群仅作用于内部$T^6$中的$T^5$子空间。通过研究沿剩余$S^1$的退紧致化极限，发现17个解可等价地由Scherk--Schwarz紧致化方案从某种父代非对称轨形（asymmetric orbifold）获得。文中还计算了多种非阿贝尔晶体群$G$的配边群$\Omega_3^{Spin(BG)}$以排除反常。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦论中构建四维非超对称且真空能在一圈阶为零的模型是一个重要方向，但先前对具有非阿贝尔点群的轨形分类尚不完整。本文旨在填补这一空白，并探索此类模型与Scherk--Schwarz紧致化之间的联系。

Method: 采用弦微扰论（string perturbation theory）框架，对四维Type II环面轨形进行分类，点群为非阿贝尔旋转群且仅作用于$T^5$子空间；通过退紧致化极限分析将结果映射至Scherk--Schwarz紧致化；利用配边群$\Omega_3^{Spin(BG)}$计算检验反常消除条件。

Result: 在给定限制条件下完成了部分分类，共找到17个满足单圈真空能为零的解；这些解可统一视为从父代非对称轨形经Scherk--Schwarz紧致化导出；给出了多种非阿贝尔晶体群$G$的配边群$\Omega_3^{Spin(BG)}$计算结果。

Conclusion: 非超对称Type II轨形中确实存在一类真空能在弦单圈阶为零的模型，且其结构可通过退紧致化极限与Scherk--Schwarz紧致化建立等价关系。配边群计算为这些模型的无反常性提供了保障。

Abstract: We present a partial classification of four-dimensional, non-supersymmetric Type II toroidal orbifolds with non-abelian point groups of rotations, and vanishing vacuum energy at one loop in string perturbation theory. The classification is complete within a class of such orbifolds with the restriction that the point group only acts on a $T^5$ inside the full internal $T^6$. By studying their decompactification limits along the leftover $S^1$, we see that the 17 solutions we find can alternatively be obtained as Scherk--Schwarz compactifications of some parent asymmetric orbifold. Along the way, to ensure the absence of anomalies, we compute bordism groups $Ω_3^{Spin(BG)}$ for a variety of non-abelian crystallographic groups $G$.

</details>


### [68] [Massive Gravity @ 15](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15507)
*Claudia de Rham*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统回顾了无鬼魂（ghost-free）有质量引力（massive gravity）的理论发展，指出其作为大尺度广义相对论红外修正的理论地位，并讨论了其在Vainshtein机制、有效场论（effective field theory）一致性、黑洞纠缠熵（black-hole entanglement entropy）以及$T\bar{T}$形变（$T\bar{T}$ deformation）等前沿问题中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 核心方法在于构建一个高度受约束的非线性相互作用结构（nonlinear interaction structure），该结构恰好传播五个自由度，并将强耦合标度（strong-coupling scale）提升至最大值，从而将理论组织为有效场论（effective field theory）。非线性屏蔽通过Vainshtein机制（Vainshtein mechanism）自动内嵌，保证了局域引力测试的现象学一致性。近年来，该理论还被构建为在特定极限内具有显式良定性（well-posed）的表述。

Result: 从有效场论视角看，幺正性（unitarity）、解析性（analyticity）和因果性（causality）施加的强大约束将无鬼魂理论（ghost-free theory）凸显为有质量引力的一个独特的红外实现（infrared realisation）。该理论还被应用于黑洞纠缠熵（black-hole entanglement entropy）与“岛屿”（islands）时空区域的研究，并被发现可以在二维和特殊情况下的高维中作为一种精确可解的$T\bar{T}$形变（$T\bar{T}$ deformation）出现。

Conclusion: 有质量引力为探索广义相对论红外修正中现象学与紫外完备化（UV completion）之间的相互作用提供了一个有价值的理论实验室（theoretical laboratory）。

Abstract: Massive gravity is one of the most natural proposals for modifying gravity at large distance scales. First proposed to tackle the cosmological constant problem, it has the potential to simultaneously maintain theoretical consistency and agreement with current observational constraints. The development of Lorentz-invariant ghost-free massive gravity resolves long-standing obstacles associated with interacting massive spin--2 fields. Central to this development is a highly constrained nonlinear interaction structure that propagates exactly five degrees of freedom. The same interaction structure raises the strong-coupling scale to its maximal value, which organizes the theory as an effective field theory. Phenomenological consistency with local tests of gravity is ensured by nonlinear screening through the Vainshtein mechanism, which is automatically built in. Recent developments have shown how to formulate the theory in a manifestly well-posed way within some limits and beyond. From an effective field theory perspective, unitarity, analyticity, and causality impose powerful constraints that strongly single out the ghost-free theory as a distinguished infrared realisation of massive gravity. We further discuss these results in light of recent consistency analyses, which we put in context. Interestingly, massive gravity has recently been invoked in discussions of black-hole entanglement entropy and spacetime regions known as `islands'. The theory is also shown to emerge as an exactly solvable $T \bar T$ deformation in both two dimensions and for special cases in higher dimensions, opening up valuable insights into its UV behaviour. Massive Gravity thus serves as a valuable theoretical laboratory for exploring the interplay between phenomenology and UV completions in infrared modifications of General Relativity.

### [69] [Probing Lorentz-invariance-violation with quantum coherence of Unruh-DeWitt detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15551)
*Yihao Wu,Xiaobao Liu,Zehua Tian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本研究提出利用惯性Unruh-DeWitt探测器的量子相干性（quantum coherence）作为检验洛伦兹对称性破坏（Lorentz invariance violation, LIV）的低能探针，发现探测器的量子相干动力学对其快度（rapidity）存在强烈依赖，并在圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）启发的聚合物量子化标量场理论中展现出临界快度附近的急剧转变，从而为测试量子引力效应提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LIV的特征能量尺度M_\star通常远超现有实验能力，直接检验极为困难。因此，需要寻找一种低能探针来间接检测LIV效应，以弥合理论预测与实验可达能标之间的差距。

Method: 研究了一个惯性Unruh-DeWitt（UDW）探测器与具有Lorentz破坏色散关系ω_{|k|}=|k|f(|k|/M_\star)的无质量标量场之间的量子相干动力学。与Lorentz不变情形下量子相干性与快度无关不同，LIV情形下探测器量子相干的动力学表现出对快度的强烈依赖，并以此作为低能LIV信号。该方法进一步应用于圈量子引力启发的聚合物量子化（polymer-quantized）标量场理论。

Result: 在聚合物量子化标量场理论中，探测器的量子相干性对快度展现出显著的依赖性，并在临界快度β_c ≈ 1.3675附近发生急剧转变。该临界值处于现有设施（如相对论重离子对撞机）的可达范围内。此外，探测器的快度与能级间隔能够增强对LIV检验的响应灵敏度。

Conclusion: 量子相干性可作为检验LIV的灵敏且实用的低能探针，为测试量子引力（quantum gravity）导致的场论修正提供了一种互补性实验途径。

Abstract: Testing Lorentz invariance violation (LIV) is notoriously difficult, as its characteristic energy scale, $M_\star$, in modified dispersion relations typically lies beyond current experimental reach. To enable a low-energy probe, we investigate the quantum coherence of an inertial Unruh-DeWitt (UDW) detector interacting with a massless scalar field with a Lorentz-violating dispersion relation $ω_{|\textbf{k}|}=|\textbf{k}|f(|\textbf{k}|/M_\star)$. Unlike the Lorentz-invariant case where quantum coherence is rapidity-independent, we find for the Lorentz-violating quantum field case the dynamics of detector's quantum coherence exhibits a strong dependence on its rapidity -- offering a potential low-energy signature of LIV. Applying this to the polymer-quantized scalar field theory inspired by loop quantum gravity, we show that the detector's quantum coherence exhibits a pronounced dependence on rapidity and undergoes a sharp transition near a critical rapidity $β_c \approx 1.3675$, a value within reach of existing facilities like the Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider. We also show how the detector's rapidity and its energy-level spacing enhance the response to the test of LIV. Our results establish quantum coherence as a sensitive and practical probe of LIV, providing a complementary avenue for testing quantum gravity-induced modifications to field theory.

Abstract: We present the scattering modes of the oscillon, to the first three orders in the Fodor expansion, in terms of elementary functions. In the case of relativistic modes, these results are new. We use them to fully decompose the field and also to analytically invert the decomposition. In quantum field theory, this allows us to show that the corresponding creation and annihilation operators satisfy the usual oscillator algebra, extending to relativistic modes the demonstration that, at a fixed order in the Fodor expansion, a periodic oscillon state exists.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究了原始引力子与封闭理想反射光学谐振腔内量子化电磁场基模之间的相互作用，并分析了该系统中光子的Hanbury-Brown Twiss关联（Hanbury-Brown Twiss correlations）对引力子二阶相干度的响应。

Result: 即使忽略引力子与光子之间极弱的耦合强度，光子的Hanbury-Brown Twiss关联对引力子的二阶相干度仍不敏感。光子的二阶相干度不反映引力子的关联性质。

Conclusion: 即使原则上也无法通过腔模的强度关联来推断引力子的统计性质（包括其超泊松统计特性）。

Abstract: Unlike the gravitational waves classically generated by moving macroscopic masses, the diffuse backgrounds of gravitons originate most likely from zero-point fluctuations of the gravitational field amplified by the evolution of the space-time curvature. The resulting entangled states lead to specific second-order correlation effects that could be eventually detected. For a quantitative analysis of this empirical expectation we scrutinize the interactions between the cosmic gravitons and the fundamental mode of a quantized electromagnetic field confined inside a closed optical resonator with perfectly-reflecting walls. We show that the Hanbury-Brown Twiss correlations of the photons are insensitive to the degrees of second-order coherence of the gravitons even barring for the exceedingly small couplings of the problem. Since the degree of second-order coherence of the photons does not reflect the correlation properties of the gravitons, the statistical properties of the gravitons (and their super-Poissonian statistics) cannot be inferred, even in principle, from the intensity correlations of the cavity modes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文通过分析费曼积分的解析结构，推导出两类新的约束条件：一类标识了无法重复计算的不连续性，另一类标识了无论其他不连续性计算顺序如何都恒产生相同结果的不连续性；这些约束在维数正则化（dimensional regularization）的所有阶均成立。

Result: 两类新约束条件被提出并得到验证：不可重复的不连续性和顺序无关的不连续性。这些结果为朗道自举法（Landau bootstrap）提供了新的输入信息。

Conclusion: 这些新约束为利用费曼积分的奇点和不连续性信息构建其函数形式提供了更系统的理论工具，从而推动了费曼积分解析结构研究的进展。

Abstract: We describe recent advances in our understanding of the analytic structure of Feynman integrals. In particular, we describe two new classes of constraints on such integrals, that identify discontinuities that either cannot be repeated, or that always give rise to the same result (no matter which other discontinuities are computed first). These new constraints hold at all orders in dimensional regularization, and provide us with new input for the Landau bootstrap, where information about the singularities and discontinuities of individual Feynman integrals is used to construct their functional form.

Abstract: We discuss a class of symmetry structures in general spacetime dimension that arise when gauging symmetries in theories with a cubic 't Hooft anomaly. The anomaly mixes two Abelian discrete symmetries $A$ and $B$ with a characteristic class for an additional symmetry $C$, and we gauge $A\times B$. The novelty of this construction is that the resulting symmetry structure involves certain condensation defects of the dual symmetry $\widehat{A}\times\widehat{B}$. Conclusion: 组合全息量子秘密共享方案能够有效刻画体子区域逻辑信息在边界上的编码与保护性质，其性能由全息相变和子区域选择决定，且存在一族可实现的完美方案。

Abstract: We introduce combinatorial holographic quantum secret sharing (CHQSS) for a bulk subregion in AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ to study how logical information of the bulk subregion is encoded in the boundary and protected from erasures of boundary subregions. We introduce a distance, a reconstruction threshold, and a secret threshold to characterize CHQSS schemes. We present the phase transitions of multipartite entanglement wedges in a symmetric setup and observe multiple distinct phase transition points. The distance and thresholds depend on the holographic phase and the choice of bulk subregion. We derive the maximum distance. Moreover, we derive the relations between the distance and the thresholds. We construct a family of CHQSS schemes in the symmetric setting that includes perfect threshold CHQSS and perfect non-threshold CHQSS.

</details>


### [77] [Localized Vector Modes on Local Cosmic Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16120)
*Sergio Alameda-Calvo,Jose J. Blanco-Pillado,Jose Queiruga*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了阿贝尔-希格斯（Abelian-Higgs）模型中定域在宇宙弦上的矢量激发的动力学，发现这些激发是沿弦传播的有质量矢量自由度，具有长寿命特征，并通过非线性耦合与体辐射发生衰变；当标量自耦合足够大时，衰变由可解释为Feshbach共振的准正规模式主导，且场论模拟揭示了矢量模式与Goldstone扇区之间的参量不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究仅关注宇宙弦上的常规形状模（shape mode），而矢量激发作为一种局域化的有质量规范场涨落尚未被系统研究，其动力学特性、衰变机制以及是否在标量自耦合（$λ$）的全部取值范围内均存在等问题尚不明确。

Method: 通过解析手段确定矢量激发的频谱和空间分布；利用非线性耦合至体辐射（bulk radiation）分析其衰变行为；开展全$3+1$维场论模拟（field theory simulations）研究矢量激发弦的完整动力学；构建有效模型（effective model）捕捉参量不稳定性并识别其背后的非线性耦合。

Result: 矢量激发在所有$λ$取值下均保持有界；大$λ$时标量辐射通道运动学上不可及，衰变转由准正规模式（quasinormal modes）介导，此类模式可解释为弦的Feshbach共振；场论模拟发现矢量模式与Goldstone扇区之间存在参量不稳定性（parametric instability），且矢量模式可同时共振激发两个横向方向，这与形状模的行为不同。

Conclusion: 矢量激发是宇宙弦上一类长寿命的有质量自由度，其在局域弦动力学中扮演非平凡角色。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of vector excitations localized on cosmic strings in the Abelian-Higgs model. These confined gauge field fluctuations behave as massive vector degrees of freedom propagating along the string. We show that they remain bounded for all values of the scalar self coupling $λ$, including parameter regimes in which the previously studied conventional shape mode is no longer present. After determining their spectra and spatial profiles, we analyze their decay through nonlinear coupling to bulk radiation. Their amplitudes exhibit the characteristic power law relaxation associated with non-linear radiation. For sufficiently large $λ$ the scalar radiation channel becomes kinematically inaccessible and the decay is instead mediated by quasinormal modes which can be interpreted as Feshbach resonances of the string. We then study the full $3+1$ dimensional dynamics of the vector-excited string. Field theory simulations reveal a parametric instability between the vector mode and the Goldstone sector. In contrast to the shape mode, the vector mode resonantly excites both transverse directions simultaneously. In addition, we build an effective model that captures the instability and identifies the nonlinear couplings responsible for it. Our results show that vector excitations constitute a long-lived massive degree of freedom with a non-trivial role in the dynamics of local strings.

### [78] [Gravitational index of the D1-D5-P black string](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16134)
*Silvia Georgescu,Sameer Murthy,Andrew Svesko*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文找到了与 D1-D5-P 黑弦的超对称指标（supersymmetric index）对应的欧几里得引力路径积分（Euclidean Gravitational Path Integral, GPI）的鞍点（saddle-points）。这些鞍点是带有固定逆温度 β 的复、超对称、非极值 10 维 IIB 超引力解，其 Gibbons-Hawking 在壳作用量与具有相同单极荷的极值黑弦的超对称指标一致，且在对偶 D1-D5 SCFT₂ 的椭圆属（elliptic genus）的 Cardy 公式层面得到复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过欧几里得引力路径积分的鞍点方法，从超引力（supergravity）一侧直接计算与 D1-D5-P 黑弦相关的超对称指标（supersymmetric index），从而建立引力路径积分与对偶超共形场论（SCFT₂）中椭圆属（elliptic genus）之间的精确对应关系。

Method: 论文构造了 10 维 IIB 超引力理论中的复、超对称、非极值鞍点解，这些解带有固定的单极荷（monopole charges）$Q_1$、$Q_5$、$Q_n$ 和角动量 $J_L$，并具有固定的角速度 $Ω_R = -2πi/β$，从而在 GPI 中实现了 $(-1)^F$ 的插入。随后采用有限温度近地平线退耦极限（finite-temperature near-horizon decoupling limit），得到形如 $S^3$ 纤维化于 BTZ 时空之上的解。

Result: Gibbons-Hawking 在壳作用量（on-shell action）与温度无关，且与携带相同单极荷的极值黑弦的超对称指标一致。在近地平线极限下，尽管解具有有限的全纯（holomorphic）和反全纯（anti-holomorphic）模参数（modular parameters），但其在壳作用量复现了对偶 D1-D5 SCFT₂ 的全纯椭圆属（holomorphic elliptic genus）的 Cardy 公式（Cardy formula）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，欧几里得引力路径积分的鞍点可以准确捕捉 D1-D5-P 系统超对称指标的非微扰信息，且该指标通过 Cardy 公式与对偶二维超共形场论的椭圆属精确匹配，进一步支持了 AdS/CFT 对应（AdS/CFT correspondence）在超对称指标层面的有效性。

Abstract: We present saddle-points of the Euclidean Gravitational Path Integral (GPI) corresponding to the supersymmetric index of the D1-D5-P black string. These saddles are complex, supersymmetric, non-extremal solutions of 10-dimensional IIB supergravity theory with arbitrary inverse temperature $β$. The solutions carry fixed monopole charges $Q_1$, $Q_5$, $Q_n$, and angular momentum $J_L$ equal to the extremal supersymmetric black string. Crucially, the solutions have fixed angular velocity $Ω_{R} = - 2 πi /β$, which is the chemical potential dual to $J_R$. This implements the insertion of $(-1)^{F}$ in the GPI. The Gibbons-Hawking on-shell action is temperature-independent and agrees with the supersymmetric index of the extremal black string carrying the same monopole charges. Upon taking a finite-temperature near-horizon decoupling limit, we obtain solutions of the form $S^3$ fibered over BTZ. Although these near-horizon solutions have finite holomorphic and anti-holomorphic modular parameters, their on-shell action reproduces the Cardy formula of the holomorphic elliptic genus of the dual D1-D5 SCFT$_2$.

### [79] [Elastic stiffness of three-dimensional black holes and wormholes from Liouville line defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16155)
*Jeevan Chandra,Boris Post*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在 AdS$_3$ 引力中研究薄壳黑洞与虫洞的弹性变形，将其刚度核（stiffness kernels）的计算归结为共形焊接问题（conformal welding problem），并在半经典极限下计算了位移算符（displacement operator）和质量密度算符（mass-density operator）的谱，同时探讨了弹性变形对黑洞微观态统计和熵的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解薄壳黑洞与虫洞在 AdS$_3$ 引力中弹性变形的响应机制，以及这些变形如何通过全息对偶（holographic duality）与边界共形场论（CFT）中的线缺陷（line defects）相关联。

Method: 计算配分函数（partition function）对变形的二次响应，定义横向形状涨落和非均匀质量密度涨落的刚度核；将刚度核的计算转化为共形焊接问题，并在重壳极限（heavy-shell limit）下约化为普适的 Schwarzian 响应。

Result: 刚度核对应于 CFT 中缺陷局域算符（位移算符和质量密度算符）的两点函数；在半经典极限下，谱可以是离散的或连续的，取决于几何中是否存在垂直于壳的非紧致方向；利用线性响应理论（linear response theory）给出了洛伦兹（Lorentzian）解释，并计算了弛豫时间尺度。

Conclusion: 弹性变形会影响黑洞微观态统计和黑洞熵，表明全息框架下薄壳几何的弹性性质与微观自由度之间存在内在联系。

Abstract: We study elastic deformations of thin-shell black holes and wormholes in AdS$_3$ gravity. These geometries are sourced by line defects in the dual conformal field theory, and their shape and mass distribution define elastic moduli of the gravitational saddle. We compute the quadratic response of the partition function to these deformations, defining stiffness kernels for both transverse shape fluctuations and inhomogeneous mass-density fluctuations. The computation of the stiffness kernels can be realized as a hyperbolic response to a conformal welding problem which reduces to the universal Schwarzian response in the heavy-shell limit. The stiffness kernels are two-point functions of defect-local operators in CFT: the displacement operator, which measures the response to shape deformations, and a mass-density operator, which measures the response to local changes in the shell density. We compute the spectrum of these operators in the semiclassical limit, in various black hole and wormhole backgrounds. The spectrum can be discrete or continuous depending on the existence of a non-compact direction transverse to the shell in the geometry. We also provide a Lorentzian interpretation for the stiffness kernels using linear response theory and compute the relaxation time scales towards the corresponding transient deformations in the dual holographic CFT. Lastly, we compute the effect of these elastic deformations on black hole microstate statistics and black hole entropy.

### [80] [Dressed States Call for Logarithmic Asymptotic Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16179)
*Jorrit Bosma,Jeremy A. Mann,Charles Marteau,Blagoje Oblak,Marios Petropoulos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文受Wigner基本粒子分类（基于时空对称群的不可约酉表示）启发，探讨何种群结构能够产生带有红外规范玻色子云（clouds of infrared gauge bosons）的粒子量子态。研究表明，答案由标准渐近对称性（asymptotic symmetries，如引力情形中的BMS对称性）补充对数对称性（logarithmic symmetries）给出，后者来源于arXiv:2305.05436。由此推论，被 dressing 的粒子的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）可分解为“裸”单粒子态空间与软规范玻色子（soft gauge bosons）空间的张量积，且后者必须通过对数变换才能获得，该变换最终导致一个关键的Heisenberg中心扩张（central extension）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 借鉴Wigner将基本粒子分类为时空对称群不可约酉表示（irreducible unitary representations）的方法，探究何种对称群能够描述带有红外规范玻色子云的粒子量子态。

Method: 通过引入标准渐近对称性（如引力中的BMS对称性）以及arXiv:2305.05436中识别出的对数对称性（logarithmic symmetries），构建能够生成 dressed 粒子量子态的群结构。

Result: 被 dressing 的粒子的希尔伯特空间可以因子化为“裸”单粒子态空间与软规范玻色子空间的张量积（tensor product）；该分解必须通过对数变换实现，而该变换导致一个关键的Heisenberg中心扩张（Heisenberg central extension）。

Conclusion: 标准渐近对称性配合对数对称性足以从群表示论角度刻画带有红外规范玻色子云的粒子量子态，且对数变换是获得软玻色子希尔伯特空间不可或缺的条件。

Abstract: Inspired by Wigner's classification of elementary particles as irreducible unitary representations of a spacetime symmetry group, we ask what group can give rise in this way to the quantum states of a particle dressed with clouds of infrared gauge bosons. We show that the answer is given by standard asymptotic symmetries (such as BMS in the gravitational case), supplemented by the logarithmic symmetries identified in arXiv:2305.05436. A corollary is the factorization of the Hilbert space of a dressed particle as a tensor product of the space of `naked' one-particle states with a Hilbert space of soft gauge bosons. The latter cannot be obtained without logarithmic transformations, which are ultimately responsible for the presence of a crucial Heisenberg central extension.

</details>

### [81] [Enhanced Third-Harmonic Generation in Diamond Photonic Crystal Slabs via Doubly Resonant Quasi-Bound States in the Continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15526)
*Sangmin Ji,Satoshi Iwamoto,Hideki Gotoh*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出并数值论证了在金刚石光子晶体（PhC）平板中实现双共振三次谐波产生（THG）的方案：通过设计六角晶格三角孔平板，使基频（FH）模与三次谐波（TH）准连续区束缚态（quasi-BIC）模同时共振并满足频率三倍条件，采用三角形而非圆形气孔打破对称性以激活非线性耦合，基于耦合模理论推导闭式效率表达式并设计异质结腔体，三维仿真结果表明归一化THG效率可达2.7×10⁻⁷ W⁻²，在 fabrication 限制的品质因子（Q=200,000）下可提升至约0.034 W⁻²，且工作波长可通过晶格常数调控，覆盖通信波段到可见光及深紫外范围，为全金刚石平台上的高效单片片上频率转换提供了稳健路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现高效、单片集成的片上频率转换器件是量子光子学和非线性光子学的核心需求之一，而金刚石因其超宽透明窗口和优异光学性质成为理想平台；然而，如何在金刚石光子晶体中同时实现基频与三次谐波的双重共振并激活有效的非线性耦合，是尚未解决的关键挑战。

Method: 设计了一种六角晶格三角孔金刚石光子晶体平板，使K点带边基频（FH）模与Γ点准连续区束缚态（quasi-BIC）三次谐波（TH）模满足频率三倍条件；将气孔形状从圆形改为等边三角形，打破面内对称性以消除非线性耦合为零的限制；基于耦合模理论（coupled-mode theory）推导出THG效率的闭式表达式，并据此设计元胞和光子晶体（PhC）异质结腔体。

Result: 三维仿真结果显示，所设计腔体在中等品质因子下归一化THG效率为η=2.7×10⁻⁷ W⁻²；在 fabrication 限制的品质因子（Q=200,000）下，该效率预计可达约0.034 W⁻²。工作波长可通过晶格常数调节，覆盖从通信波段到可见光及深紫外（deep-UV）输出。

Conclusion: 该设计方案建立了在全金刚石平台上实现高效、单片片上频率转换的稳健路线，结合金刚石的超宽透明窗口，可适用于量子光子学和非线性光子学中的多种波长需求。

Abstract: We propose and numerically demonstrate doubly resonant third-harmonic generation (THG) in a diamond photonic crystal (PhC) slab, in which the fundamental harmonic (FH) and the third harmonic (TH) modes are simultaneously resonant within the same membrane. A hexagonal-lattice slab with triangular air holes is designed so that a K-point band-edge FH mode and a $Γ$-point quasi-bound-state-in-the-continuum (quasi-BIC) TH mode satisfy the frequency-tripling condition $3ω_1\approxω_3$. Modifying the hole shape from circular to equilateral triangular breaks the in-plane symmetry that otherwise forces the nonlinear coupling to vanish, thereby converting a TH mode with negligible overlap into one with finite while simultaneously reducing the required slab thickness. Guided by a closed-form expression for THG efficiency derived from coupled-mode theory, we design the unit cell and a PhC heterostructure cavity. Three-dimensional simulations of the designed cavity yield a normalized THG efficiency $η=2.7\times10^{-7}~\mathrm{W}^{-2}$ under moderate quality factors, which is projected to reach ~$0.034~\mathrm{W}^{-2}$ at the fabrication-limited quality factor (Q = 200,000). Because the operating wavelength is set by the lattice constant, this design, combined with the ultra-wide transparency window of diamond, can map a single geometry across various fabricable wavelengths, spanning from telecommunication bands to color-center-resonant visible and deep-UV outputs. These results establish a robust route toward efficient, monolithic on-chip frequency conversion in an all-diamond platform for quantum and nonlinear photonics.
