### [82] [Near-field Dressing of Thermal Emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15622)
*Victor Guillemot,Raphael Mol,Riccardo Messina,Valentina Krachmalnicoff,Philippe Ben-Abdallah,Wilfrid Poirier,Yannick De Wilde*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明近场电磁耦合会重塑远场热辐射，表现为距离依赖的“被修饰发射率”（dressed emissivity），并建立了热学版本的Purcell效应（Purcell effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近场辐射热传递（radiative heat transfer）在亚波长距离下可通过光子隧穿（photon tunnelling）增强能量交换，但近场相互作用是否也会改变物体自身发射的热辐射尚不明确。本文旨在回答这一开放问题。

Method: 采用双探针量热平台（dual-probe calorimetric platform），独立监测两个硼硅酸盐微球（borosilicate microspheres）在120微米到数百纳米间距下的辐射平衡，涵盖从远场到近场的过渡区域；通过纳瓦级分辨率的差分辐射测量法（differential radiometry）分析非对称热通量。

Result: 观测到非对称热通量（asymmetric heat fluxes）以及较热球体的非单调响应（non-monotonic response），表明热辐射不仅受发射体-热库相互作用支配，还受周围光子环境耦合影响。通过分析耦合系统与外部热库的总功率交换，直接提取了被修饰发射率，证明近场相互作用通过重新分布热涨落可用的电磁模式来重整化（renormalize）远场热辐射。

Conclusion: 这些观察提供了直接实验证据，表明热发射体受其电磁环境“修饰”（dressed），从而建立了热学版本的Purcell效应。

Abstract: Radiative heat transfer at subwavelength distances is generally understood as enhanced energy exchange mediated by photon tunnelling between neighboring bodies. While near-field interactions can dramatically increase mutual heat transfer, whether they also modify the thermal radiation emitted by the bodies themselves remains an open question. Here we experimentally show that near-field electromagnetic coupling reshapes far-field thermal emission through a distance-dependent dressed emissivity. Using a dual-probe calorimetric platform, we independently monitor the radiative balance of two borosilicate microspheres over separations ranging from 120 micrometers to a few hundred nanometers, spanning the transition from the far field to the near field. Nanowatt-resolved differential radiometry reveals asymmetric heat fluxes and a non-monotonic response of the hotter sphere, demonstrating that thermal radiation is governed not only by emitter-bath interactions but also by coupling to the surrounding photonic environment. By analyzing the total power exchanged between the coupled system and the external thermal bath, we directly extract a dressed emissivity and show that near-field interactions renormalize the far-field thermal emission of the pair through a redistribution of the electromagnetic modes available to thermal fluctuations. These observations provide direct experimental evidence that thermal emitters are dressed by their electromagnetic environment, establishing a thermal analogue of the Purcell effect.

</details>


### [83] [Sub-microsecond conformational dynamics in an optical nanocavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15925)
*Heehun Sung,Sam C Scholten,Pavlina Sasheva,Igor Marinkovic,Warwick P Bowen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种光纤集成硅光子传感器，通过亚波长光场约束和高光学均匀性，将蛋白质布朗运动抑制60倍，实现了在连续单次测量中以亚微秒速度（短至400ns）解析铁蛋白构象变化，并揭示了系综平均中隐藏的切换动力学、记忆效应和分子异质性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 蛋白质的微秒级构象变化（conformational changes）对许多功能至关重要，但此前缺乏无需标记即可在单次测量中快速观测单个蛋白质的方法：单次单分子测量速度不足，蛋白质的布朗运动（Brownian motion）也会掩盖信号。

Method: 采用光纤集成硅光子传感器（fibre-integrated silicon-photonic sensor），结合远亚波长光场约束（far-sub-wavelength optical field confinement）与高光学场均匀性（high optical field uniformity），将蛋白质布朗运动抑制约60倍。

Result: 在铁蛋白（ferritin）分子的单次测量中，观测到数万次与铁蛋白外壳构象涨落（conformational fluctuations）一致的跃迁，时间分辨率低至400 ns；长时间连续监测揭示了系综平均（ensemble averages）中隐藏的切换动力学（switching kinetics）、记忆效应（memory effects）和分子异质性（molecular heterogeneity）。

Conclusion: 该传感器为在单分子水平上连续、快速解析蛋白质动力学提供了新路径，有望加深对蛋白质功能的机制理解。

Abstract: Microsecond conformational changes underlie many protein functions, but ensemble averaging has been needed to observe them without labels. Single-shot measurements on individual proteins have had insufficient speed, while protein Brownian-motion has obscured signals. Here, we report a fibre-integrated silicon-photonic sensor that overcomes these barriers, resolving protein dynamics at sub-microsecond speeds in continuous single-shot measurements that can extend over minutes. This is achieved by combining far-sub-wavelength optical field confinement with high optical field uniformity that suppresses protein Brownian-motion by a factor of sixty. In single-shot measurements on ferritin molecules, we observe tens of thousands of transitions consistent with conformational fluctuations of the ferritin shell, resolving them over timescales as short as 400 ns. The ability to continuously monitor transitions over long times reveals switching kinetics, memory effects and molecular heterogeneity hidden in ensemble averages. This opens a new path to improved mechanistic understanding of protein function.

### [84] [Quantum Mechanics on Lie Groups: II. Path Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16029)
*Mathieu Beauvillain,Blagoje Oblak,Marios Petropoulos*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在李群 $G$ 上构建了路径积分（path integral）描述跃迁振幅（transition amplitudes），通过处理非交换动量空间（noncommutative momentum space）和群的紧致方向（compact directions），将紧致性问题归结为极大环面（maximal tori）上的绕数求和（sum over winding numbers），并应用于欧拉-阿诺德系统（Euler-Arnold systems）的半经典近似（semiclassical approximations）计算至双圈阶（two-loop order）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续 arXiv:2512.19840 中李群上量子动力学的研究，希望构建路径积分以描述 Hilbert 空间 $L^2(G)$ 中的跃迁振幅，并克服非交换动量空间和紧致方向带来的技术困难。

Method: 通过将紧致方向的处理转化为极大环面上的绕数求和，推广了圆环（circle）路径积分中常见的技巧，从而在非交换动量空间背景下构建出李群上的路径积分。

Result: 成功构建了李群上的路径积分，并应用该方法计算了欧拉-阿诺德系统的传播子（propagators）和配分函数（partition functions）的半经典近似，精度达到双圈阶。

Conclusion: 该路径积分框架有效处理了紧致李群上的量子动力学问题，绕数求和机制是紧致性带来的核心修正；半经典计算结果验证了方法的可行性。

Abstract: We continue our study of quantum dynamics on a Lie group $G$, initiated in arXiv:2512.19840, by building the path integral that governs transition amplitudes in the Hilbert space $L^2(G)$. This relies on the proper handling of both a noncommutative momentum space and the presence of compact directions in $G$. We show that compactness can be handled through a sum over winding numbers in maximal tori of $G$, generalizing the similar sum commonly encountered for path integrals on a circle. As applications, we compute semiclassical approximations of propagators and partition functions of Euler-Arnold systems, up to (and including) two-loop order.

### [85] [Quantum-classical crossover in fault-tolerant quantum dynamics simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16116)
*Jinzhao Sun,Bozhen Zhou,Jue Xu,Yuan Yao,Zhenyu Du,Zixu Zhang,Yuntian Gu,Junxiang Huang,Shuo Zhou,Ziruo Wang,Alexander Yosifov,Wenzheng Dong,Yiming Huang,Daniel Serrano,Xinzhao Wang,Tianfeng Feng,Shreyas Sadugol,Wenjun Yu,Zhou You,Dayue Qin,Xiao-Ming Zhang,Yantao Wu,Aditya Iyer,You Zhou,Tongyang Li,Ying Li,Xiongfeng Ma,Qi Zhao,Pei Zeng,Pan Zhang,Xiao Yuan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了量子多体动力学在容错量子计算与经典算法之间的具体交叉点（quantum-classical crossover）。作者提出一个可扩展的容错框架，结合相干可观测量估计与时空高效的非克利福德旋转实现，在物理错误率 $p=10^{-3}$ 条件下，对100位点一维混合场伊辛模型的模拟仅需约2小时和 $3.7 \times 10^5$ 个物理量子比特，而经典张量网络方法需约100年；二维模型中量子运行时间可缩短至分钟级。错误率降至 $10^{-4}$ 时，物理量子比特数和运行时间分别降低一个数量级以上。结果表明了实现实际量子优势的可扩展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管量子计算机有望解决经典上难以处理的问题，但确定容错量子计算在实用问题中何时超越最优经典算法仍是一个悬而未决的挑战。本文旨在建立量子多体动力学在现实硬件条件下超越经典算法的具体交叉点，为未来容错架构提供量化的工程目标。

Method: 提出一个可扩展的容错量子计算框架，核心包括：(1) 相干可观测量估计（coherent observable estimation）；(2) 时空高效的非克利福德旋转（non-Clifford rotations）实现，抑制仅部分容错方法中残留的逻辑错误。该框架与量子纠错和可观测量估计协议进行协同设计（co-design），通过改进的旋转态注入（rotation-state injection）抑制逻辑误差积累并降低采样开销。

Result: 针对混合场伊辛动力学（mixed-field Ising dynamics），在物理错误率 $p=10^{-3}$ 时：(1) 100位点一维系统需约2小时和 $3.7 \times 10^5$ 个物理量子比特，经典张量网络需约100年；(2) 二维系统量子运行时间可缩短至分钟级。物理错误率降至 $p=10^{-4}$ 时，物理量子比特数降至 $3.1 \times 10^4$，一维运行时间降至分钟级，二维降至秒级。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了量子多体动力学中容错量子计算超越经典算法的具体交叉点，表明在现实硬件条件下可实现实际量子优势（practical quantum advantage），并为未来容错量子架构提供了量化的工程目标。

Abstract: While quantum computers promise to solve classically intractable problems, identifying the point at which fault-tolerant quantum computation outperforms the best classical algorithms for practical applications remains an outstanding challenge. Here we establish a concrete quantum-classical crossover for quantum many-body dynamics under realistic hardware conditions. We introduce a scalable fault-tolerant framework that combines coherent observable estimation with a space-time-efficient implementation of non-Clifford rotations, suppressing the residual logical errors that limit existing partially fault-tolerant approaches. A benchmark against state-of-the-art tensor-network and variational Monte Carlo algorithms reveals a concrete crossover for mixed-field Ising dynamics at modest system sizes. For a physical error rate of $p=10^{-3}$, fault-tolerant simulation requires approximately 2 hours and $3.7 \times 10^5$ physical qubits for a 100-site 1D system, whereas tensor network approaches would require about 100 years. For 2D models, where rapid entanglement growth limits the classical evolution time, we project quantum runtimes within minutes. A physical error rate of $p=10^{-4}$ leads to at least an order of magnitude reduction in qubit count ($3.1 \times 10^4$ physical qubits) and runtime (minutes for 1D and seconds for 2D). The reduction in quantum runtime arises from our improved rotation-state injection and co-design of quantum error correction and observable-estimation protocols, which jointly suppress logical-error accumulation and reduce sampling overhead. Our results establish a scalable route towards practical quantum advantage and identify quantitative engineering targets for future fault-tolerant architectures.

### [86] [The Paradox of the Third Particle is classical](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15351)
*Ladina Hausmann,Renato Renner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明“第三粒子悖论”（The Paradox of the Third Particle）并非量子特有，在经典系统中同样存在，并建立了一个No-Go定理：当使用物理子系统（无论经典或量子）作为参考系时，若要求参考系变换保持信息不变，则无法从每个参考系的角度对世界进行有意义的子系统划分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通常认为第三粒子悖论源于量子叠加（quantum superposition），但作者试图探究该悖论及其推论（如子系统的相对性）是否已在经典层面出现，从而澄清该问题的根本来源。

Method: 通过分析经典系统中使用粒子作为参考系时的情形，论证第三粒子悖论及其相关效应在经典语境下已然存在，并由此推广建立一个一般性的No-Go定理。

Result: 发现第三粒子悖论及其导致的子系统相对性（relativity of subsystems）在经典系统中同样出现；并证明了一个No-Go定理：只要使用物理子系统作为参考系，且要求参考系变换保持信息，就无法从每个参考系视角有意义地将世界划分为独立子系统（如单个粒子）。

Conclusion: 第三粒子悖论并非量子力学特有现象，而是源于将物理子系统用作参考系这一更广泛的框架性限制；该No-Go定理对经典和量子系统均成立，揭示了子系统划分的根本局限性。

Abstract: The Paradox of the Third Particle arises when particles are described relative to one of them serving as a reference frame. Although it is typically attributed to quantum superpositions, we show that the paradox and its ramifications$\unicode{x2014}$such as the relativity of subsystems$\unicode{x2014}$already occur classically. In light of this insight, we establish a no-go theorem that holds whenever physical subsystems, whether classical or quantum, are used as reference frames: if one demands that frame transformations be information-preserving, then it is impossible to meaningfully partition the world into subsystems, like individual particles, from the perspective of each frame.

### [87] [Object-relative ultraviolet weighting of electromagnetic modes and one-loop ultraviolet finiteness in quantum electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16096)
*Christian Rembe*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文探索是否可以将局域电磁相互作用（localized electromagnetic interactions）建模为一种相对于相互作用对象的紫外模态权重（object-relative ultraviolet weighting），并展示在该框架下选定的一圈QED贡献变得紫外有限，同时保持受限的沃德一致性（Ward consistency）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机源于两个启发式考虑：一是弱场自反作用估计（weak-field self-backreaction estimate）表明足够局域的能量携带模式会产生有效权重；二是三维交叠论证（three-dimensional overlap argument）支持局域相互作用的这种描述。

Method: 该方案（ansatz）基于相对相互作用物体的协变模式变量（covariant mode variable）$u_\mu k^\mu$（即局域相互作用物体静止系中的模式频率）来构建权重，使红外（infrared）区域在特征角波数$k_c$以下保持不变，紫外（ultraviolet）贡献则被渐近抑制为$k_c^3/k^3$量级。

Result: 在选定的一圈QED贡献中，权重使得自能和顶点修正保持受限的一圈沃德一致性（one-loop Ward consistency）；四个测试案例（反常磁矩、贝特型低能兰姆移位估计、卡西米尔效应、紧凑紫外一圈测试）中，前三个分别产生了与电子康普顿尺度、原子束缚态尺度和板间距相关的有物理意义的特征尺度。

Conclusion: 结果表明不同可观测量可能探测到不同的有效局域化尺度（effective localization scales）。作用量层面的推导、谱一致性以及向一圈以上扩展仍为未解决的问题。

Abstract: This work explores whether localized electromagnetic interactions can be modeled in terms of an effective object-relative ultraviolet weighting of internal modes. The proposal is motivated heuristically by two considerations: a weak-field self-backreaction estimate for sufficiently localized energy-carrying modes and a three-dimensional overlap argument for localized interactions. In the resulting ansatz, the infrared sector remains unchanged up to a characteristic scale the at angular wavenumber $k_c$, while ultraviolet contributions are suppressed asymptotically by a factor of order $k_c^3/k^3$ with the angular wavenumber $k$. Because a crossover based solely on $k^μk_μ$ is not well suited to the intended mode-based interpretation, the weighting is formulated in terms of the object-relative covariant mode variable $u_μ k^μ$ with the four-velocity $u^μ$, i.e. the mode frequency measured in the rest frame of the localized interaction object. Within this restricted framework, selected one-loop QED contributions considered here become ultraviolet finite, and a restricted one-loop Ward-consistency check is preserved when the same scalar weighting is assigned consistently to the same internal photon mode in self-energy and vertex corrections. Four initial test cases are discussed: the anomalous magnetic moment, a Bethe-type low-energy Lamb-shift estimate, the Casimir effect, and a compact ultraviolet one-loop test. In the first three cases, the weighting leads to physically sensible characteristic scales associated with the electron Compton scale, an atomic bound-state scale, and plate distance, respectively. The results suggest that different observables may probe different effective localization scales. Action-level derivation, spectral consistency, and extension beyond one loop remain open problems.

</details>


### [88] [Non-Hermitian Quantum Adiabatic Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15343)
*Zi-Bo Jin,Yi Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出非厄米量子绝热算法不仅需要实能隙谱，还需要稳定的伪谱（pseudospectrum），并通过历史解耦构造实现了受控伪谱和实能隙谱，以CK最大独立集问题为基准展示了多项式时间的非厄米绝热计算及其鲁棒性，同时讨论了基于耦合波导和辅助损耗通道的光学实现方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统（non-Hermitian systems）为量子优化与计算提供新机遇，但现有非厄米量子绝热算法对伪谱稳定性（pseudospectral stability）这一关键条件缺乏系统研究，且直接的非厄米Feynman-Kitaev构造面临严重的伪谱不稳定性问题。

Method: 提出一种将非酉量子电路（non-unitary quantum circuits）映射到局域哈密顿量路径（local Hamiltonian paths）的新框架，通过历史解耦构造（history-decoupled construction）替代直接的非厄米Feynman-Kitaev构造，以同时实现受控伪谱和实能隙谱。

Result: 以CK基准问题族（CK benchmark family）中的最大独立集问题为例，实现了多项式演化时间（polynomial-evolution-time）的非厄米绝热计算，且该计算对扰动保持鲁棒。此外，提出了基于耦合波导与辅助损耗通道的光学实现方案。

Conclusion: 伪谱稳定性与实能隙谱（real, gapped spectrum）共同构成了非厄米量子绝热计算的关键原则，本文为实际实现提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian systems offer new opportunities for quantum optimization and computation. Here, we show that non-Hermitian quantum adiabatic algorithms require not only a real, gapped spectrum, but also a stable pseudospectrum. We propose a novel framework by mapping non-unitary quantum circuits to local Hamiltonian paths, thereby preserving their optimization advantages and shallow depth. While a direct non-Hermitian extension of the Feynman-Kitaev construction suffers severe pseudospectral instability, our history-decoupled construction yields both a controlled pseudospectrum and a real, gapped spectrum. Using the CK benchmark family of maximum independent set problems, we demonstrate polynomial-evolution-time non-Hermitian adiabatic computation that remains robust against perturbations. We further discuss a feasible optical implementation using coupled waveguides with an auxiliary lossy channel. Our work establishes pseudospectral stability, alongside real, gapped spectra, as key principles and a practical route for non-Hermitian quantum adiabatic computation.

### [89] [Fate of dynamical quantum phase transitions from sudden quench to slow quench limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15649)
*Xiang Zhang,Fuxiang Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了动态量子相变（DQPT）从突然淬火到缓慢淬火过程中的演化行为，发现缓慢淬火能够保留与平衡量子相变相关的本征DQPT，同时滤除偶然DQPT，从而揭示DQPT与平衡量子相变之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往对动态量子相变（dynamical quantum phase transition, DQPT）的研究主要集中于突然淬火（sudden quench）协议，缺乏对慢速淬火（slow quench）条件下DQPT行为的系统理解。

Method: 本文通过对比突然淬火与缓慢淬火两种协议，系统探索DQPT在从突然到缓慢淬火区间内的行为，并利用XY链（XY chain）、Aubry-André模型（Aubry-André model）以及三聚体Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型（trimer Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model）进行实例验证。

Result: 当淬火协议跨越平衡量子相变（equilibrium quantum phase transition）时，DQPT在缓慢淬火下保持鲁棒性；而当淬火前后哈密顿量位于同一平衡相时产生的偶然DQPT（accidental DQPT），在慢淬火极限下会被滤除。

Conclusion: 缓慢淬火能够揭示DQPT与平衡量子相变之间的内在联系，使得DQPT可以作为识别平衡量子临界点（equilibrium quantum critical points）的动态探针。

Abstract: Previous investigations of dynamical quantum phase transition (DQPT) have predominantly focused on sudden quench protocols. In this work, we systematically explore the fate of DQPT from the sudden to the slow quench regime. We establish that DQPT remains robust under slow quenching when the protocol crosses an equilibrium quantum phase transition. Conversely, we show that accidental DQPTs,which occur when the pre and post quench Hamiltonians reside in the same equilibrium phase, can be filtered out in the slow quench limit. This demonstrates that slow quenches can reveal the intrinsic connection between DQPT and equilibrium quantum phase transitions, thereby enabling DQPT to serve as a dynamical probe for identifying equilibrium quantum critical points. We illustrate these findings with examples from the XY chain, the Aubry-André model, and the trimer Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model.

### [90] [Reconstruction of the noise correlation spectral density from the cavity emission in a two-qubit system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15909)
*Nadine Lenke,Guido Burkard*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究腔耦合量子比特在纵向噪声（longitudinal noise）影响下的动力学行为，发现通过腔发射（cavity emission）可以表征噪声相关性（noise correlations），并提出了在噪声类型未知时提取噪声相关谱密度（noise correlation spectral density）的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computation）面临噪声挑战，其中关联噪声（correlated errors）对量子纠错（quantum error correction）构成严重威胁。本文旨在理解并表征两个腔耦合量子比特中噪声相关性的动力学行为。

Method: 假设量子比特受纵向噪声影响且无直接耦合，通过分析腔发射来研究噪声相关性的动力学。考虑白噪声（white noise）、准静态噪声（quasi-static noise）和奥恩斯坦-乌伦贝克噪声（Ornstein-Uhlenbeck noise）三种情形，并利用卷积定理（convolution theorem）在噪声类型未知时提取噪声相关谱密度。

Result: 在白噪声情形下，噪声相关效应以腔-量子比特耦合常数的五阶标度（fifth order）增长，显著弱于准静态噪声的三阶标度（third order）。通过多次噪声实现（noise realizations）的平均，可在已知频谱时从腔发射重构噪声相关谱密度；在噪声类型未知时，可借助卷积定理提取该谱密度。

Conclusion: 腔发射为表征量子比特间的噪声相关性提供了有效途径，且不同噪声类型下相关效应的标度行为存在显著差异，这对设计抗关联噪声的量子纠错方案具有指导意义。

Abstract: A significant challenge in the field of large-scale fault-tolerant quantum computation is the influence of noise. In addition to the influence of noise on individual qubits, the smaller additional effect of noise correlations is also of high significance because correlated errors pose a challenge for quantum error correction. We describe the dynamics of two cavity-coupled qubits that are subject to correlated noise, assuming that the qubits are affected by longitudinal noise and not coupled directly. We find that the cavity emission enables the characterization of the noise correlations and describe the cases of white noise, quasi-static noise, and Ornstein-Uhlenbeck noise. For a known frequency spectrum, the reconstruction of the noise correlation spectral density from the cavity emission is possible by averaging over many different noise realizations. We demonstrate that, in the case of white noise, the noise correlation effects scale with the fifth order of the cavity-qubit coupling constant and are thus strongly suppressed compared with the case of quasi-static noise, where they scale with the third order. Furthermore, we present a method for extracting the noise correlation spectral density from the cavity emission in the case where the underlying noise type remains unidentified. This can be achieved by applying the convolution theorem.

</details>


### [91] [Conditional Euclidean-Hamiltonian reductions for sign-problem toy models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15950)
*Tsogtgerel Gantumur*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种条件欧几里得-哈密顿量（conditional Euclidean-Hamiltonian, CEH）约化方法，将欧几里得蒙特卡洛（Euclidean Monte Carlo）与哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）形式相结合，通过将活跃扇区（active sector）保持为算符值（operator-valued）而非标量权重，以避免有限密度费米子系统中的复权重采样问题。在三个有限基准上的测试表明，该方法可在结构化有限模型中实现从标量符号重加权（scalar sign reweighting）到可监控活跃空间近似的转换，但尚未建立端到端的随机CEH处理或证实其可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限密度费米子系统中，费米子扇区求迹后常产生变号或复标量权重，使得依赖实非负路径积分权重的欧几里得蒙特卡洛方法失效；而哈密顿量形式虽避免复权重采样问题，却面临希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）的快速增长。为此，本文旨在融合两种描述的优点，设计一种可避免复权重问题的替代方案。

Method: CEH约化围绕一个蒙特卡洛可处理的参考问题（reference problem）和一个残差活跃扇区（residual active sector）来组织计算。活跃扇区不被求迹为行列式或标量权重，而是保持算符值形式，利用参考计算确定投影关联矩阵（projected correlation matrices）或转移矩阵（transfer matrices），从而定义一个有限有效哈密顿量（finite effective Hamiltonian），并在投影后引入剩余的有限密度依赖性。

Result: 在三个有限基准上进行了验证：双通道振子测试条件基压缩；正测度随机计算测试关联矩阵获取和广义特征值问题（GEVP）提取（含与PDMS风格估计器的比较）；四站点Hubbard环将有限预算行列式符号应力测试与非目标活跃空间中的有限密度延拓相结合。基准结果支持从标量符号重加权向可监控活跃空间近似的转换，但未提供Hubbard符号问题的端到端随机CEH处理，也未建立有利的扩展性。

Conclusion: CEH方法的实用性取决于两个条件：低秩可近似性（low-rank approximability）以及所需投影矩阵数据的高效提取。当前工作表明，该方法在结构化有限模型中具有潜力，但尚未达到完整的随机处理或可扩展性验证阶段。

Abstract: Euclidean Monte Carlo methods are effective when the path-integral weight is real and nonnegative, but finite-density fermion systems often produce sign-changing or complex scalar weights after the fermionic sector is traced out. Hamiltonian formulations avoid this complex-weight sampling problem but face rapid Hilbert-space growth. This paper studies a conditional Euclidean-Hamiltonian (CEH) reduction that combines these two descriptions.
  The calculation is organized around a Monte Carlo-tractable reference problem and a residual active sector. Instead of tracing the active sector into a determinant or scalar weight, CEH keeps it operator-valued and uses the reference calculation to determine projected correlation or transfer matrices. These matrices define a finite effective Hamiltonian, with the remaining finite-density dependence introduced after projection. At finite rank, the result is an effective model whose accuracy must be tested through basis enlargement, metric conditioning, stochastic matrix-element errors, and number-sector diagnostics.
  The construction is examined in three finite benchmarks. A two-channel oscillator tests conditional basis compression; a positive-measure stochastic calculation tests correlation-matrix harvesting and GEVP extraction, including a comparison with a PDMS-style estimator; and a four-site Hubbard ring combines a finite-budget determinant-sign stress test with finite-density continuation in non-target active spaces. The benchmarks support the proposed trade from scalar sign reweighting to a monitored active-space approximation in structured finite models, but they do not provide an end-to-end stochastic CEH treatment of the Hubbard sign problem or establish favorable scaling. Usefulness requires both low-rank approximability and efficient extraction of the required projected matrix data.

</details>


<div id='nlin.SI'></div>

# nlin.SI [[Back]](#toc)

### [92] [Singularity interactions for lattice equations: introducing the taishi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15670)
*Ralph Willox,Basil Grammaticos,Alfred Ramani,Thamizharasi Tamizhmani*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了几类可积晶格方程（integrable lattice equations）的奇异性（singularities），发现它们均存在三种奇异类型：一种有限延伸和两种无限延伸。其中一种名为“taishi”的带状奇异性（strip-like singularity）是新近发现的。研究表明，taishi 与其余两类奇异性的相互作用展现出丰富行为，且该行为可编码为简单的符号动力学（symbolic dynamics），即盒与球元胞自动机（Box & Ball cellular automaton）的动力学规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解可积晶格方程中奇异性的完整分类及其相互作用机制，尤其是新发现的 taishi 奇异性的普遍性与动力学特征。

Method: 选取若干可积晶格方程，分析其奇异性类型（有限与无限延伸），重点考察 taishi 与其他两类奇异的相互作用，并将所得行为映射为盒与球元胞自动机的符号动力学。

Result: 所有研究方程均存在三种奇异性：一种有限延伸和两种无限延伸；taishi 与其余奇异的相互作用展现丰富行为，且该行为在所有情形下均可由盒与球元胞自动机的简单符号动力学描述。

Conclusion: taishi 型奇异性在可积晶格方程中具有普遍性，其相互作用行为统一由盒与球元胞自动机的动力学编码，揭示了可积系统中奇异性动力学的深层结构。

Abstract: We study the singularities of some selected integrable lattice equations and show they all admit three types of singularities: one of finite and two of infinite extent. In particular, we show that all the equations we study possess a recently discovered, strip-like, singularity which is known under the moniker of ''taishi''. We study in detail the interaction of these taishi with the remaining two types of singularities and show that the rich behaviour first obtained in the case of the Korteweg-deVries equation is also present for other equations. Moreover, we find that in all cases this behaviour can be encoded in terms of simple symbolic dynamics which are just the dynamics governing a Box & Ball cellular automaton.

</details>

### [93] [Quasinormal Modes of Self-Dual Loop Quantum Gravity Corrected Kerr Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15324)
*Yu Wang,Meilin Liu,Haiguang Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用修正的Newman-Janis算法构建带有两个量子参数（聚合物参数P和最小面积参数a₀）的转动LQG黑洞度规；使用六阶WKB近似（sixth-order WKB approximation）和时域积分方法（time-domain integration）分析有效势、拟正则模频谱和振铃动力学。

Result: 聚合物参数P系统性降低振荡频率Re(ω)，而自旋参数a则增强振荡频率；时域信号明显依赖于多极数ℓ（multipole number）和泛音指数n（overtone index）。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解圈量子引力修正对黑洞微扰（black hole perturbations）和引力波振铃信号（gravitational-wave ringdown signals）的影响提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate scalar quasinormal modes and ringdown signals of a rotating loop quantum gravity black hole constructed via the revised Newman--Janis algorithm. The spacetime incorporates two quantum parameters, the polymeric parameter $P$ and the minimal area parameter $a_0$, and reduces to the Kerr spacetime in the classical limit. Using the sixth-order WKB approximation and time-domain integration, we analyze the effective potential, quasinormal mode spectrum, and ringdown dynamics. The polymeric parameter $P$ systematically reduces the oscillation frequency $\mathrm{Re}(ω)$, while the spin parameter $a$ enhances it. The time-domain signals exhibit clear dependence on the multipole number $\ell$ and overtone index $n$. Our results provide a theoretical framework for understanding the effects of loop quantum gravity corrections on black hole perturbations and gravitational-wave ringdown signals.

### [94] [Schwarzschild-like Black Holes Submerged in an Exponential Density Dark Matter Profile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15490)
*Kuantay Boshkayev,Yassine Sekhmani,Soroush Zare,Hassan Hassanabadi,Shahin Mamedov,Yergali Kurmanov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一类嵌入指数-椭球暗物质晕（exponential-spheroidal dark matter halo）中的Schwarzschild黑洞，通过解析求解爱因斯坦方程得到度规函数，并系统分析了该时空的曲率结构、能量条件、影子观测量、标量拟正规模（quasi-normal modes）以及灰体界限（grey-body bounds），发现暗物质晕会单调移动光子球和影子半径，并在低频段削弱有效势垒的透射率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在真实天体物理环境中，黑洞通常被暗物质晕所包围，但现有研究对这类嵌入暗物质晕的黑洞时空的精确解析解和完整物理性质（如拟正规模和灰体界限）仍缺乏系统分析。

Method: 基于唯象密度分布ρ(r)=ρ₀ e^{-r/r₀}建模暗物质晕，通过求解静态球对称爱因斯坦方程获得解析lapse函数；采用Padé-resummed WKB近似计算标量拟正规模，利用EHT观测数据（M87*和Sgr A*）约束影子半径。

Result: Ricci标量和Ricci平方在原点有限，但Kretschmann标量在黑洞质量存在时保留中心潮汐奇异性；弱、零和主导能量条件满足，强能量条件在有限径向区间内被违反；暗物质晕单调地增大光子球半径和影子半径；标准WKB近似在高阶泛音和强晕配置下不可靠，而Padé-resummed WKB近似给出稳定结果；灰体界限显示晕在低频段削弱透射率。

Conclusion: 该嵌入指数-椭球暗物质晕的Schwarzschild黑洞时空在无黑洞质量时退化为规则晕结构，在无晕时退化为标准Schwarzschild时空；EHT观测数据可对晕参数给出近似约束，为未来更精确的天文观测检验暗物质模型提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We study a class of Schwarzschild black holes embedded in an exponential-spheroidal dark matter halo, modelled by a phenomenological density profile $ρ(r)=ρ_0 e^{-r/r_0}$. By solving the Einstein equations for a static, spherically symmetric spacetime, we obtain an analytic solution for the lapse function that reduces to the Schwarzschild spacetime in the absence of the halo and to a regular halo configuration when the central black hole mass vanishes. Indeed, the two halo parameters, $ρ_0$ and $r_0$, describe the strength and radial extent of the dark matter distribution. We analyse the curvature structure, energy conditions, shadow observables, scalar quasi-normal modes and grey-body bounds of the resulting spacetime. The Ricci scalar and the Ricci square remain finite at the origin, whilst the Kretschmann scalar retains the usual central tidal singularity in the presence of a black hole mass. The weak, null, and dominant energy conditions are satisfied, whilst the strong energy condition is violated on a finite radial interval. We also show that the halo monotonically shifts the photon sphere and the shadow radius, which allows us to derive approximate constraints from the EHT observations of M87* and Sgr A*. For scalar perturbations, the Padé-resummed WKB approximation yields stable quasinormal frequencies, while the standard WKB approximation becomes unreliable for higher overtones and strong-halo configurations. Finally, the greybody bounds indicate that the halo weakens transmission through the effective barrier, particularly at low frequencies.

### [95] [Gauge-Unfixed Hamiltonian Casimir and Static Torsionful Sector in the Katanaev-Volovich Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15496)
*J. Manuel-Cabrera,J. M. Paulin-Fuentes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对一阶Katanaev-Volovich二维有挠引力模型进行了哈密顿分析，通过Dirac-Bergmann和Faddeev-Jackiw两种方法提取了正则结构与约束代数，最终恢复了Casimir不变量并分析了其对Killing温度和熵的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立一阶Katanaev-Volovich二维引力模型的正则哈密顿结构，明确其规范对称性生成元（gauge symmetry generators）与Casimir不变量（Casimir invariant）在约化相空间中的作用，并探讨挠率（torsion）对静态黑洞（static black hole）热力学参数的修正。

Method: 采用扩展的Dirac-Bergmann嵌入方法（extended Dirac-Bergmann embedding）分离辅助的第二类约束（second-class constraints），消去后恢复一阶作用量编码的正则结构；同时独立使用Faddeev-Jackiw约化方法（Faddeev-Jackiw reduction）验证约化括号的一致性。在此基础上，从约化后的第一类约束理想（first-class constraint ideal）直接恢复Katanaev/Poisson-西格玛模型（Poisson-Sigma Model）Casimir，并在不含任何规范固定条件下完成识别。

Result: 一阶作用量自然指定了正则共轭对：辅助Lorentz标量共轭于空间联络（spatial connection）和双标架（zweibein）。两种约化方法得到相同的约化括号。恢复的Casimir在归一化后成为有挠分支的哈密顿参数（Hamiltonian parameter）。在静态扇区中，Casimir归一化的径向场与Killing度量范数（Killing metric norm）不一致，对角代表满足关系 \(NB=e^{4βr}\)。挠率通过Killing时间（Killing time）的归一化修正了Killing温度（Killing temperature），而视界熵（horizon entropy）保持标准二维dilaton形式，Casimir归一化的第一定律成立。

Conclusion: 一阶Katanaev-Volovich模型的哈密顿分析确认了其正则结构与对称性生成元，Casimir不变量可作为约化相空间的全局标记（global label）；挠率对静态黑洞温度有非平凡修正，但熵与第一定律形式保持不变，表明该模型在热力学层面与标准dilaton引力存在一致性与区别。

Abstract: Hamiltonian analysis of the first-order Katanaev-Volovich model of two-dimensional gravity with torsion. The first-order action already singles out natural canonical pairs: the auxiliary Lorentz scalars are conjugate to the spatial connection and zweibein. An extended Dirac-Bergmann embedding isolates an auxiliary second-class sector whose elimination recovers the canonical structure encoded in the first-order action and leaves the first-class constraints generating the local gauge symmetries. An independent Faddeev-Jackiw reduction yields the same reduced brackets. The Katanaev/Poisson-Sigma Casimir is then recovered, up to normalization, directly from the reduced Dirac-Bergmann first-class constraint ideal, before imposing any gauge condition. This identifies the Casimir as a global label of the reduced canonical sectors; after the static normalization is chosen, it supplies the Hamiltonian parameter of the torsionful branch. The same normalization is applied to that branch in dilaton gauge, whose field equations are verified on shell. In this static sector the Casimir-normalized radial field does not coincide with the metric Killing norm: the diagonal representative satisfies \(NB=e^{4βr}\). Consequently, torsion modifies the Killing temperature through the normalization of the Killing time, while the horizon entropy retains its standard two-dimensional dilaton value and the Casimir-normalized first law holds.

</details>


### [96] [Viscous Accretion Disks around Regular Black Holes Embedded in a Quintessence Dark Energy Field: Beyond the Novikov--Thorne Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15679)
*Sandip Dutta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文构建了嵌在精质暗能量（quintessence dark energy）场中的旋转Hayward规则黑洞周围几何薄、光学厚吸积盘的完整相对论框架，通过在内稳定圆形轨道（ISCO）引入非零黏滞力矩，系统分析了黑洞自旋、Hayward长度尺度和暗能量密度对辐射效率及黏滞修正的影响，并提出了可观测的简并破除策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准吸积盘模型（如Novikov–Thorne–Page模型）假设内边界无应力，且通常仅考虑真空Kerr黑洞。本工作旨在将该模型推广至包含非线性电动力学修正（Hayward规则黑洞）与精质暗能量（quintessence dark energy, DE）场的更一般时空背景，并解析地引入非零内边界黏滞力矩（viscous torque），从而探索几何与暗能量对吸积盘辐射效率及观测特征的联合影响。

Method: 将静态球对称的Hayward非线性电磁场解与精质暗能量流体（状态方程参数ω<-1/3）解组合并旋转，构建旋转Hayward+quintessence黑洞时空。放弃Novikov–Thorne–Page模型的无应力内边界条件，利用相对论垂直本征频率（vertical epicyclic frequency）在ISCO处解析地引入非零黏滞力矩。通过解析计算辐射效率（bolometric efficiency）和黏滞修正比（viscosity amplification ratio），分析各参数的依赖关系。

Result: 证明了辐射效率η=[1-E(ISCO)]×100%严格独立于黏滞参数α，但对Hayward长度尺度l和暗能量密度ρ₀敏感。在基准参数（j=0.4, l=0.5M_BH, ρ₀=2×10⁻⁴）下，联合几何的辐射效率为8.71%，高于相同自旋下真空Kerr的7.51%。黏滞修正比δF/F_NTP在r→ISCO⁺处发散，且Hayward+DE背景下的黏滞放大比从真空Kerr的0.80–4.52%提升至0.87–6.76%（α=0.1）。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了可观测的简并破除（degeneracy-breaking）策略，即通过辐射效率和黏滞修正的联合测量，可区分黑洞自旋、Hayward长度尺度和暗能量密度的贡献。黏滞放大比随参数变化的单调行为可作为独立于整体谱归一化的观测判据，适用于NICER和NuSTAR等高精度X射线观测任务。

Abstract: We develop a comprehensive relativistic framework for geometrically thin, optically thick Shakura--Sunyaev $α$-viscous accretion disks around rotating Hayward regular black holes embedded in a quintessence dark energy (DE) field. The static, spherically symmetric building blocks of our spacetime are each exact solutions of the Einstein field equations, sourced respectively by the Hayward non-linear electromagnetic field and a quintessence fluid with equation-of-state parameter $ω<-1/3$; we combine and rotate them following standard practice for this class of models, and we are explicit throughout about the resulting metric's phenomenological status. Abandoning the stress-free inner boundary of the Novikov--Thorne--Page (NTP) model, we analytically incorporate a non-zero viscous torque $\Tcal_{\rm in}$ at the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) via the relativistic vertical epicyclic frequency $\Obot(r)$. We prove that the bolometric efficiency $η=[1-E(\rISCO)]\times100\,\%$ is strictly independent of the viscosity parameter $α$ but sensitive to both the Hayward length scale $l$ and the DE density $ρ_0$, establishing a rigorous two-observable degeneracy-breaking strategy. At benchmark parameters ($j=0.4$, $l=0.5M_{\BH}$, $ρ_0=2\times10^{-4}$), the combined geometry yields $η=8.71\,\%$, substantially above the vacuum Kerr value $7.51\,\%$ at the same spin. The viscosity correction $δ\Fcal/\Fcal_{\rm NTP}$ diverges at $r\to\rISCO^+$, amplified by the geometric odification of the boundary pressure: the viscosity amplification ratio rises from $0.80$--$4.52\,\%$ (vacuum Kerr) to $0.87$--$6.76\,\%$ (Hayward+DE) at $α=0.1$, providing a clean, monotonic observational discriminator accessible to \textit{NICER} and \textit{NuSTAR}, independent of the bulk spectral normalisation.

### [97] [Scalar quasinormal modes of Schwarzschild--anti-de Sitter black holes: spectral analysis and generalized boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15731)
*Davide Batic,Alan S. Cornell,Denys Dutykh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用切比雪夫谱方法（Chebyshev spectral method）研究四维 Schwarzschild–anti-de Sitter 黑洞上无质量标量场的拟正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs），并在标准 Dirichlet 边界条件之外引入广义边界条件变形，发现非 Dirichlet 条件下会出现具有正虚部的额外模式，表明存在边界条件诱导的不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在反德西特（anti-de Sitter, AdS）背景下黑洞微扰的边界条件对拟正则谱的影响，特别是当边界条件偏离标准 Dirichlet 条件时，系统可能出现的稳定性变化。

Method: 采用切比雪夫谱方法对径向问题进行数值求解，将外部区域紧致化后，将问题转化为关于无量纲频率的二次矩阵多项式（quadratic matrix pencil）；在 AdS 边界处施加广义系数边界条件来模拟边界条件的变形。

Result: 在标准 Dirichlet 边界条件下，成功复现了从小黑洞到中等及大黑洞的已知标量谱，包括长过音序列（overtone sequences）及小黑洞极限下趋近纯 AdS 正常模的行为。对于所有非 Dirichlet 边界条件，在代表性大小的黑洞中均观测到一个具有正虚部的额外模式，表明边界条件诱导的不稳定性；近 Dirichlet 区域精细扫描未发现有限临界角。

Conclusion: 非 Dirichlet 的广义边界条件会引入不稳定的拟正则模，且该不稳定性在 Dirichlet 边界附近没有有限的临界阈值，表明 AdS 边界条件的微小偏离足以破坏系统的稳定性。

Abstract: We study quasinormal modes (QNMs) of a minimally coupled massless scalar field on four-dimensional Schwarzschild--anti-de Sitter black holes using a Chebyshev spectral method. After compactifying the exterior domain, the radial problem is formulated as a quadratic matrix pencil in the dimensionless frequency. For the standard Dirichlet, or vanishing-field, boundary condition at the conformal AdS boundary, we reproduce the known scalar spectra across small, intermediate, and large black holes, including long overtone sequences and the expected approach to pure-AdS normal modes in the small black hole limit. We then deform the AdS boundary condition by imposing a generalized relation between the two independent asymptotic coefficients of the massless scalar. This deformation is treated as a generalized coefficient boundary condition for the massless scalar, and not as the usual alternative quantization for scalars in the Breitenlohner-Freedman window. The Dirichlet endpoint recovers the stable standard spectrum. For every non-Dirichlet value examined, and for representative small, intermediate, and large black holes, we find an additional mode with positive imaginary part, signaling a boundary-condition-induced instability. A near-Dirichlet refinement finds no finite critical angle down to the smallest deformation probed.

### [98] [Einstein crystals in Snyder and Snyder-de Sitter noncommutative backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15760)

Abstract: We investigate the behavior of Einstein crystals in noncommutative backgrounds described by the Snyder and Snyder-de Sitter models. We show that noncommutativity influences the key thermodynamic quantities, including internal energy and specific heat. These corrections can be directly related to modifications of the underlying uncertainty relations, of the generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) and generalized extended uncertainty principle (GEUP) types.

### [99] [The weight of light: colliding pulses of radiation in General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15761)
*Jorge Expósito Patiño,Vitor Cardoso,Hannes R. Rüter*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了极强电磁辐射脉冲的引力相互作用，发现无论是在单脉冲还是迎头碰撞情形下，都可以形成非常致密的状态，其致密性超过了“环假设（hoop conjecture）”所提出的最大值，并展示了从无视界状态到黑洞形成的多种终态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索极强电磁辐射脉冲在引力相互作用下的行为，特别是超越引力坍缩阈值后的物理现象，以检验环假设（hoop conjecture）在强场引力系统（strong-field gravitational systems）中的适用性。

Method: 通过数值模拟分别研究了单个电磁辐射脉冲和迎头碰撞情形，并调节参数使其达到甚至超过引力坍缩（gravitational collapse）的阈值。

Result: 发现了致密性超过环假设最大值的非常致密状态；单脉冲超越阈值时会产生一个快速黑洞（fast black hole）；迎头碰撞可通过调节参数形成两种无视界状态、两个小黑洞或一个大黑洞。

Conclusion: 无质量场（massless fields）的引力相互作用可以产生非平凡的终态或中间态，同时呈现出极高的光度和致密性。

Abstract: We study the gravitational interaction of very strong pulses of electromagnetic radiation, up to and beyond gravitational collapse. We demonstrate the existence of very compact states close to the threshold of collapse, both for a single pulse, and a head-on collision of such pulses, and we measure their compactness to be above the maximum value proposed by the hoop conjecture. For a single pulse above the threshold of collapse, a fast black hole is produced. Depending on the amount of tuning, head-on collisions can form two horizonless states, two small black holes or one big black hole. Our results show that the gravitational interaction of massless fields can lead to nontrivial final or intermediate states, while giving rise to extremely high luminosity and compactness.

</details>


### [100] [Optical and Thermodynamic Signatures of Lorentz Symmetry Breaking in Bumblebee AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15827)
*Behzad Eslam Panah,Abdullah Guvendi,Semra Gurtas Dogan,Omar Mustafa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在蜂鸟引力（bumblebee gravity）中研究了自发洛伦兹对称性破缺（spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking）对四维渐近AdS黑洞的标量波传播、零测地线（null geodesics）和热力学行为的影响，发现参数ℓ调控径向几何缩放、波传播特性及热力学稳定性，且作为热机（heat engine）时效率随ℓ增加并存在上限η≤1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在蜂鸟引力框架下，探讨自发洛伦兹破缺如何影响AdS黑洞的波动传播、几何光学极限及热力学性质，以建立洛伦兹破缺、波传播与黑洞热力学之间的统一理解。

Method: 通过径向Klein–Gordon方程转化为广义Helmholtz形式（generalized Helmholtz form），得到有效频率相关折射率（refractive index）；在非扩展和扩展相空间中进行热力学分析，并构建热机循环模型计算效率。

Result: 标量波传播在高频极限下与零测地线一致；ℓ控制径向尺度和几何光学极限；AdS边界反射波而视界（horizon）为单向吸收体；热力学满足第一定律和Smarr关系；ℓ影响热容、自由能和稳定性；作为热机时效率随ℓ增加，上限为η≤1。

Conclusion: 研究为蜂鸟引力中洛伦兹破缺、波传播、几何光学与AdS黑洞热力学提供了统一的理论框架，揭示了参数ℓ对多种物理性质的调控作用。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking on scalar wave propagation, null geodesics, and thermodynamic behavior of four-dimensional asymptotically AdS black holes in bumblebee gravity. The static, spherically symmetric solutions are characterized by a dimensionless parameter $\ell > -1$ arising from the vacuum expectation value of the bumblebee vector field, which globally rescales the radial geometry. Massless scalar fields are analyzed via the radial Klein--Gordon equation cast into a generalized Helmholtz form, yielding an effective frequency-dependent refractive index that identifies oscillatory and evanescent regions, classical turning points, and confinement induced by curvature and Lorentz violation. In the high-frequency limit, wave propagation coincides with null geodesics, with $\ell$ controlling radial scaling and governing the geometric-optics limit. The AdS boundary reflects waves, while the horizon acts as a one-way absorber. Thermodynamic analysis in non-extended and extended phase spaces confirms the first law and Smarr relation, with $\ell$ influencing heat capacity, free energy, and stability. \textcolor{black}{Modeling these black holes as heat engines, we construct explicit cycles and show that efficiency increases with $\ell$, leading to an upper bound imposed by $η\leq 1$. Our results provide a framework connecting Lorentz violation, wave propagation, geometric optics, and AdS black hole thermodynamics in bumblebee gravity.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用拉格朗日标量场形式化（Lagrangian scalar field formulation）和一阶哈密顿量重构方法（first-order Hamiltonian reconstruction method），将HN创生场的c-场动力学转化为等效的修正标量场理论，并与GCG的状态方程相对接。

Result: HN c-场动力学可由GCG状态方程通过等效修正标量场理论加以涵盖；在该统一描述下，推导出晚期宇宙加速（late-time acceleration）与线性扰动稳定性（stability of linear perturbations）条件。

Conclusion: 创生场宇宙学可嵌入一类更广泛的标量场模型中，这类模型包含对哈勃膨胀率（Hubble expansion rate）及相关物理可观测量的细微修正。

Abstract: The interplay of Hoyle-Narlikar (HN) creation field cosmology and scalar field models for the dark sector, including the generalized Chaplygin Gas (GCG), is investigated . Though originating from distinct theoretical frameworks, both the inclusion and the non-inclusion of the creation field degree of freedom (DoF) involve a scalar DoF, which addresses some of the limitations of the standard $Λ$CDM model. Using a Lagrangian scalar field formulation and the first-order Hamiltonian reconstruction method, the HN $c$-field dynamics is shown to be encompassed by the GCG equation of state through an equivalent modified scalar field theory. Late-time acceleration and stability of linear perturbations are derived within this unified description. Our results suggest that creation field cosmologies may be embedded in a broader class of scalar field models which encompasses subtle modifications to the Hubble expansion rate and related physical observables.

Method: 采用 $C-$度规在 $F(R)-$ModMax 理论下求解四维时空中的精确黑洞解；将该黑洞视为热力学系统，计算 Hawking 温度和熵；通过热容分析评估局部稳定性；并利用几何光学方法研究黑洞的角阴影与阴影半径。

We then examine how various parameters influence the behavior of accelerating ModMax black holes. Treating this black hole as a thermodynamic system, we calculate the Hawking temperature and entropy for the accelerating ModMax black holes within the framework of $F(R)$ gravity. Subsequently, we explore the impact of the parameters in $F(R)-$ModMax theory on the Hawking temperature and entropy. We also assess local stability by analyzing the heat capacity. Additionally, we investigate both the angular shadow and the shadow radius of an accelerating black hole in the context of $F(R)-$ModMax gravity.

### [103] [Massless scalar scattering by Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black holes:transparent-end channels and superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16068)
*Hai Huang,Xudong Sun,Juhua Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在旋转克尔-伯特-罗宾逊（Kerr–Bertotti–Robinson）黑洞几何上，采用透明边界条件，数值求解了中性标量场的实频散射问题。研究表明反射数据依赖于边界选取，超辐射受双重门控机制调控，并发现外磁场会收窄并关闭超辐射窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 Kerr–BR 黑洞背景下研究中性标量场的散射与超辐射，填补了该几何中实频散射问题数值解的空白，并揭示边界条件对反射数据的影响。

Method: 使用透明边界条件，将中性标量场的运动方程约化为四维共形波动方程（conformal wave equation），并通过共形因子缩放实现类卡特分离（Carter-like separation），结合数值方法求解实频散射问题。

Result: 反射数据依赖于边界选取而非定义唯一、与观测无关的截面；超辐射受双重门控机制控制，需要同时满足局部视界条件与外传播条件 $q_\infty^2>0$；在自旋参数 $a/M=0.9$ 时，共转偶极放大随外磁场增强而减小，外磁场在 $BM\simeq0.243$ 处关闭超辐射窗口；近传播阈值处放大系数随外波数线性归零。

Conclusion: Kerr–BR 黑洞的散射结果并非观测者无关，边界模型的选择是关键；外磁场可作为调控超辐射窗口的有效参数。

Abstract: We formulate and numerically solve the real-frequency scattering problem for a neutral, minimally coupled, massless scalar on the rotating Kerr--Bertotti--Robinson (Kerr--BR) black-hole geometry, using a specified transparent boundary condition at the coordinate end. Since the Maxwell stress tensor of the background is traceless, the minimally coupled wave equation reduces to the four-dimensional conformal wave equation, enabling exact Carter-like separation after scaling the scalar field by the conformal factor. Unlike the asymptotically flat case, the coordinate end $r\to\infty$ lies at a finite tortoise distance. We show that the resulting reflection data are conditional on this boundary prescription rather than defining a unique, observer-independent cross section. Within the transparent-end model,open-channel superradiance is governed by a double-gate mechanism requiring both the local horizon condition and the outer propagation condition $q_\infty^2>0$. At the benchmark spin $a/M=0.9$, the co-rotating dipole amplification decreases as the external magnetic field increases. Crucially, the field narrows and closes the open superradiant window at $BM\simeq0.243$. Near the propagation threshold, the amplification coefficient vanishes linearly with the outer wave number.

### [104] [Comparison of $f(R,T)$ Gravity with Multiple Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16158)
*Vincent R. Siggia,Eric D. Carlson*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过宇宙微波背景辐射、重子声学振荡、宇宙计时器和Ia型超新星等多类观测数据，对$f(R,T)=R+λT^ε$引力模型进行参数拟合，得到最佳拟合参数$ε=0.010^{+0.013}_{-0.021}$，该结果与标准宇宙学模型（$ε=0$）在误差范围内一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验$f(R,T)$修正引力理论（modified gravity theory）中不同$ε$取值下的模型与观测数据的符合程度，考察该理论是否能作为标准宇宙学模型（standard cosmological model）的有效替代或扩展。

Method: 利用宇宙微波背景辐射（cosmic microwave background, CMB）、重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）、宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometer）和Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae）等多源观测数据，在引入相关性和辐射效应后，通过数据拟合寻找不同$ε$值下的最佳拟合参数。

Result: 最佳拟合模型对应的参数值为$ε=0.010^{+0.013}_{-0.021}$，该结果在误差范围内与标准宇宙学模型的预期值$ε=0$一致。

Conclusion: 当前观测数据倾向于支持$ε$接近零的结果，表明$f(R,T)=R+λT^ε$引力模型在现有精度下并未显著偏离标准宇宙学模型。

Abstract: We examine $f(R,T)=R+λT^ε$ gravity models by finding the best fit parameters for various values of $ε$. This is accomplished by analyzing data from the cosmic microwave background, baryon acoustic oscillation observations, cosmic chronometer, and Type Ia supernovae introducing correlations and radiation effects to our previous work. We find the probability distribution for the best fit model around the value of $ε=0.010^{+0.013}_{-0.021}$, consistent with the standard cosmological model value of $ε= 0$.

### [105] [Thermo-elastic properties of hydrated epoxy-graphene nanocomposites from ensemble-based molecular dynamics simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15301)
*Maxime Vassaux,Werner A. Müller,James L. Suter,Alexandros Anastasiou,Martin Simmons,David Tilbrook,Peter V. Coveney*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过大规模系综分子动力学模拟，揭示了环氧树脂及其石墨烯纳米复合材料在5%重量比含水量以内的水合作用对玻璃化转变和弹性力学性能的影响，发现3%重量比含水量为关键阈值：低于此阈值时水合主要降低玻璃化转变温度，高于此阈值时力学性能开始恶化。研究还强调了足够大的系综规模对可靠预测异质体系力学性能的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环氧基材料具有吸湿性（hygroscopic），水分吸收会显著改变其短期和长期性能。石墨烯被认为是潜在的微观屏障，可减轻水合作用对基体的不利影响。本研究旨在系统探究水合作用对环氧树脂及其石墨烯纳米复合材料玻璃化转变和力学性能的影响，并揭示系综规模在分子动力学模拟中的关键作用。

Method: 采用大规模系综分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟方法，对纯环氧树脂（neat epoxy）和环氧-石墨烯（epoxy-graphene）体系在不同水合水平下进行温度驱动的玻璃化转变和力学响应分析，水含量范围最高达5%重量比。

Result: 发现3%重量比含水量为关键阈值：低于该阈值时水合主要降低玻璃化转变温度，力学性能不受影响；超过3%重量比后力学性能开始恶化，呈现出对水分吸收的非线性敏感性。此外，要获得收敛的力学性能预测分布，所需系综规模需显著大于当前领域标准。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了环氧基材料水合行为的新见解，强调了石墨烯在增强环境抗性方面的潜力，并推进了对聚合物纳米复合材料（polymer nanocomposites）结构-性能关系的理解，为在潮湿环境中设计更坚固的材料提供了指导。

Abstract: Epoxy-based materials are inherently hygroscopic, absorbing moisture from the environment, which can significantly alter their short and long-term performance. The presence of graphene is often considered as a potential candidate to act as a microscopic barrier, mitigating the adverse effects of hydration on the matrix. This study investigates the impact of hydration on the glass transition and elastic mechanical properties of epoxy resins and their graphene nanocomposites, focusing on water content up to 5 %wt. Using large-ensemble molecular dynamics simulations, we analyze the temperature-driven glass transition and mechanical response of both neat epoxy and epoxy-graphene systems under varying hydration levels. Our results reveal a distinct threshold at 3 %wt water content: below this, hydration primarily reduces the glass transition temperature, while mechanical properties remain unaffected. Beyond 3 %wt, however, the mechanical properties deteriorate, highlighting a non-linear sensitivity to water uptake. Furthermore, we emphasize the critical role of ensemble size in ensuring the reliability of molecular dynamics predictions for such heterogeneous systems. Our simulations demonstrate that ensembles substantially larger than current state-of-the-art standards are necessary to achieve converged distributions of the predicted mechanical properties, particularly in highly heterogeneous hydrated epoxy-graphene nanocomposites. These findings provide novel insights into the hydration behavior of epoxy-based materials and underscore the potential of graphene to enhance their environmental resistance. This work also advances the understanding of structure-property relationships in polymer nanocomposites, offering guidance for the design of more robust materials in humid environments.

### [106] [Kinetic Theory for the Shear Viscosity of Dense Binary Dipolar Fluid Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15691)
*Christopher Devik Fjeldstad,Roberto Troncoso,Astrid S. de Wijn*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文构建了强相互作用偶极硬球（dipolar hard spheres）致密二元流体混合物剪切粘度（shear viscosity）的动理学理论（kinetic theory）。该理论基于Enskog-Thorne理论，并受Pousaneh与de Wijn发展的纯流体理论启发，通过有效耦合参数、混合规则及碰撞积分（collision integral）启发式表达式导出二元混合物中的成对关联（pairwise correlations），在堆积分数（packing fraction）约0.35以内精确。与分子动力学（molecular-dynamics）模拟结果的对比表明，该剪切粘度表达式在堆积分数ξ≲0.3范围内，无需任何混合物导出拟合参数即可捕获二元偶极流体的密度与组分依赖行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密强相互作用二元流体混合物的输运性质（如剪切粘度）缺乏精确的理论描述，传统动理学理论在处理高密度下偶极相互作用时存在局限。

Method: 基于Enskog-Thorne理论框架，借鉴Pousaneh与de Wijn的纯致密流体理论，从纯流体有效耦合参数出发，结合混合规则（mixing rules）与碰撞积分的启发式表达式，推导出二元混合物中精确至堆积分数约0.35的成对关联表达式。

Result: 导出的剪切粘度表达式在堆积分数ξ≲0.3范围内，无需引入任何混合物衍生的拟合参数，即可准确描述二元偶极硬球流体的密度与组分依赖行为。

Conclusion: 该动理学理论为致密偶极二元混合物的剪切粘度提供了有效预测工具，填补了高密度强相互作用混合流体输运性质理论描述的空白。

Abstract: We construct a kinetic theory for the shear viscosity of dense binary fluid mixtures of strongly-interacting dipolar hard spheres. We derive an expression for the pairwise correlations in the binary mixtures that is accurate up to packing fractions around 0.35. The approach is based on Enskog-Thorne theory, and inspired by the theory for dense pure fluids developed by Pousaneh and de Wijn. It relies on effective coupling parameters obtained from the pure fluids combined with mixing rules and a heuristic expression for the collision integral. We compare our results to viscosities obtained numerically from molecular-dynamics simulations of dipolar hard-sphere fluids. Our expression for the shear viscosity of the binary mixtures captures the density and composition dependent behavior of the binary dipolar fluids up to packing fraction of $ξ\lesssim 0.3$ without any mixture-derived fit parameters.

### [107] [How Topology Shapes the Phase Behavior of Polyelectrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15703)
*David Beyer,Pierre J. Walker,Lena Tarrach,Zhen-Gang Wang,Christian Holm*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用随机相位近似（random phase approximation）发展了聚电解质凝聚的拓扑特异性理论，并将其应用于简单凝聚和复杂凝聚。结果表明，更紧凑的链拓扑（如星形和树枝状大分子）在比耶鲁姆长度（Bjerrum length）和盐浓度条件下表现出更强的液-液相分离倾向；不同拓扑的混合物中，仅凭拓扑差异即可驱动多相凝聚。研究建立了聚合物拓扑（polymer topology）作为一种独立于分子量、净电荷和单体化学性质的设计杠杆，用于调控带电大分子的相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有聚电解质凝聚理论主要关注线性链，缺乏对拓扑结构（如星形、树枝状大分子）影响相行为的系统性理解。本文旨在建立拓扑特异性的理论框架，揭示拓扑如何独立于其他分子特性调控凝聚行为。

Method: 采用随机相位近似（random phase approximation）作为核心理论工具，构建适用于不同拓扑结构（线性、星形、树枝状大分子）的聚电解质凝聚理论。通过引入有效χ参数（effective χ parameter）和简化全局相图（simplified global phase diagram）进行分析。

Result: 更紧凑的链拓扑（星形、树枝状大分子）在比耶鲁姆长度和盐浓度条件下表现出更强的液-液相分离倾向。仅凭聚合物拓扑差异即可驱动聚电解质的多相凝聚。拓扑驱动的相分离倾向在有限分子量时最大。

Conclusion: 聚合物拓扑可作为独立于分子量、净电荷和单体化学性质的设计杠杆，通过改变拓扑实现有效电荷密度的精细调控，从而精确调控带电大分子的相图。

Abstract: We develop a topology-specific theory of polyelectrolyte coacervation using the random phase approximation and apply it to both simple and complex coacervation. Our results for stars and dendrimers show that more compact chain topologies display a greater propensity for liquid-liquid phase separation, as a function of both Bjerrum length and salt concentration. For mixtures of different topologies, we demonstrate that differences in polymer topology alone are sufficient to drive multiphase coacervation of polyelectrolytes, which we rationalize in terms of an effective $χ$ parameter. Analysis of a simplified global phase diagram reveals that the propensity for such topology-driven phase separation is largest at a finite molecular weight. Overall, our results establish polymer topology as a powerful design lever for tuning the phase diagram of charged macromolecules independently of molecular weight, net charge, and monomer chemistry, since changes in topology enable fine-tuning of the effective charge density without altering these molecular characteristics.

</details>


### [108] [Bifurcation reordering programs snap-through symmetry in folded elastic ribbons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15706)
*Weicheng Huang,Qun Zhang,Bohan Zhang,Mingchao Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验、离散微分几何模拟和数值延拓等方法，揭示了在对称折叠弹性带中，通过重新排列对称破缺分岔（pitchfork bifurcation）与对称保持的鞍结分岔（saddle-node bifurcation）的出现顺序，可以编程控制屈曲突跳（snap-through）过程中的对称性保持与否，并构建了预测两种突跳路径切换的相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细长弹性结构的突跳（snap-through）通常被视为稳定构型间的突然转变，但转变路径可能根本不同：结构可能保持对称性突跳，或先失去对称性经过非对称状态再到达最终构型。在几何和加载本身对称的条件下，是什么机制在不同路径之间进行选择，目前仍不清楚。

Method: 研究使用带有两个对称局部折叠的弹性带，通过改变折叠位置来调控两种失稳模式的相对顺序；结合实验、离散微分几何（discrete differential geometry）模拟和数值延拓（numerical continuation）方法，绘制分岔顺序交换的相图；并建立约化双质量冯·米塞斯桁架（double-mass von Mises truss）模型来捕捉相同机制。

Result: 当对称破缺的叉形分岔（pitchfork bifurcation）先于鞍结分岔（saddle-node bifurcation）发生时，带先失去对称性然后突跳，遵循非对称路径；当鞍结分岔先发生时，带在对称分支上失去稳定性，产生对称保持的突跳转变。通过改变折叠位置可以交换这两种分岔的顺序。

Conclusion: 分岔重排（bifurcation reordering）作为一种几何机制，可用于编程控制细长弹性结构的突跳路径，为多稳态系统（multistable systems）、变形结构（morphing structures）和基于失稳的机械装置提供了设计原理。

Abstract: Snap-through in slender elastic structures is often viewed as a sudden transition between stable configurations, yet the pathway taken during this transition can differ fundamentally. A structure may snap while preserving symmetry, or first lose symmetry and pass through an asymmetric state before reaching its final configuration. What selects between these pathways remains less well understood, especially when the geometry and loading are themselves symmetric. Here, we show that snap-through symmetry can be programmed by reordering competing bifurcations in folded elastic ribbons. We study an elastic ribbon with two localized folds placed symmetrically about the midpoint and show that varying the fold position changes the relative order of two instabilities: a symmetry-breaking pitchfork bifurcation and a saddle-node bifurcation on the symmetry-preserving branch. When the pitchfork bifurcation occurs first, the ribbon loses symmetry before snapping and follows an asymmetric pathway. Conversely, when the saddle-node bifurcation occurs first, the ribbon loses stability while remaining on the symmetric branch, resulting in a symmetry-preserving transition. Combining experiments, discrete differential geometry simulations and numerical continuation, we map this exchange in bifurcation ordering and construct a phase diagram that predicts the switch between asymmetric and symmetric snap-through regimes. A reduced-order double-mass von Mises truss model captures the same mechanism as a generic competition between symmetry-breaking and symmetry-preserving instabilities. These results establish bifurcation reordering as a geometric mechanism for programming snap-through pathways in slender elastic structures, offering a design principle for multistable systems, morphing structures and instability-based mechanical devices.

</details>


### [109] [Statistical equivalence of reduced gravity and enhanced friction in granular packings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15712)
*Haiyang Lu,Zhikun Zeng,Houfei Yuan,Chengjie Xia,Hanyu Li,Chijin Zhou,Zihang Xu,Yujie Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过X射线断层扫描实验，发现降低有效重力与增加摩擦系数在统计力学上等价：两者均能降低颗粒堆积的随机松散堆积极限，并产生相同的体积分布、压实度和熵，其根源在于减少了参与承力桥结构的颗粒数，从而降低了对接触数的要求并提高了力学稳定态密度。但减重力条件下接触取向更为各向同性。这一发现将重力识别为控制力学稳定态统计可达性的物理参量，为爱德华兹（Edwards）统计力学框架提供了统一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有效重力降低对颗粒堆积（granular packing）统计力学行为的影响，并与摩擦效应进行比较，以揭示不同物理路径下力学稳定态（mechanically stable states）的统计等价性。

Method: 利用X射线断层扫描（X-ray tomography）技术，对比在减浮力有效重力（buoyancy-reduced effective gravity）条件下与正常重力条件下、颗粒摩擦系数系统变化时的颗粒堆积结构。

Result: 降低重力会降低随机松散堆积极限（random loose packing limit），其效果类似于增加摩擦；两种条件下的堆积表现出相同的体积分布（volume distributions）、压实度（compactivity）和熵（entropy）；两者均通过减少参与承力桥结构（load-bearing bridge structures）的颗粒数来松弛力学稳定性约束，从而降低对接触数的要求并提高力学稳定态密度；但减重力条件下接触取向（contact orientations）更为各向同性。

Conclusion: 重力可被视为控制爱德华兹框架（Edwards framework）中力学稳定态统计可达性（statistical accessibility）的物理控制参数；不同物理途径形成的颗粒堆积可在统计上通过爱德华兹体积系综（Edwards volume ensemble）得到统一描述。

Abstract: Using X-ray tomography, we compare granular packings prepared under buoyancy-reduced effective gravity with normal gravity packings of particles with systematically varied friction. We show that reducing gravity lowers the random loose packing limit in a manner analogous to increasing friction. Granular packings under reduced gravity and with enhanced friction exhibit identical volume distributions, compactivity, and entropy, indicating that both routes sample statistically equivalent Edwards volume ensembles of mechanically stable states. This equivalence originates from a common relaxation of the mechanical stability constraint: under both conditions, fewer particles are required to participate in the underlying load-bearing bridge structures, leading to a lower contact-number requirement and a higher density of mechanically stable states. Nevertheless, reduced gravity retains a distinct contact-scale signature through more isotropic contact orientations. These findings identify gravity as a physical control governing the statistical accessibility of mechanically stable states within the Edwards framework and provide a unified statistical description of granular packings formed through different physical routes.

</details>


### [110] [Property-dependent material times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15920)
*Aude Y. Amari,Lorenzo Costigliola,Jeppe C. Dyre*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过二元Lennard-Jones混合物的分子动力学模拟，研究了大幅温度上跳后的物理老化（physical aging）过程。研究发现，为每个可观测量（observable）分配独立的物质时间（material time）比使用统一的Tool-Narayanaswamy（TN）物质时间能更好地实现数据塌缩（data collapse），但改善程度因可观测量的不同而有显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，对于大幅温度上跳的物理老化过程，Tool-Narayanaswamy（TN）理论的统一物质时间（material time）概念在合理化老化响应方面效果不佳。本文旨在探索通过为每个可观测量分配独立的物质时间，能否改善TN形式体系的预测性能。

Method: 采用二元Lennard-Jones混合物作为模型体系，对从平衡态或缓慢弛豫态进行大幅温度上跳后的物理老化过程进行模拟分析。具体考察了从T=0.43和T=0.37上跳至T=0.48的情况。分析了势能时间自相关函数（potential-energy time-autocorrelation function）、自中间散射函数（self-intermediate scattering function）和时均方根位移（time-dependent mean-square displacement）三个可观测量，并系统检验了三角关系（triangular relation）——即物质时间存在的必要条件——的满足程度。

Result: 对于所有三个可观测量，当每个变量使用其独立的物质时间进行参数化时，均获得了最佳的数据塌缩效果。然而，改善程度在不同可观测量之间存在显著差异，其中以均方根位移的改善最为明显。

Conclusion: 为每个可观测分配独立的材料时间可以改善对大幅温度上跳后物理老化行为的描述，但这一改进并非均匀适用于所有物理量，表明不同观察量在老化过程中的弛豫动力学存在内在差异。

Abstract: We analyze simulations of physical aging following large temperature up-jumps from equilibrated, slowly relaxing states. Specifically, we consider up-jumps from temperatures T=0.43 and T=0.37 to T=0.48 in a binary Lennard-Jones mixture. The Tool-Narayanaswamy (TN) concept of a universal material time was recently shown to become less effective in rationalizing the aging response for such large jumps [Amari et al., Phys. Rev. E 113, 045411 (2026)]. Here, we investigate whether the performance of the TN formalism can be improved by assigning a separate material time to each observable. We examine the potential-energy time-autocorrelation function, the self-intermediate scattering function, and the time-dependent mean-square displacement. As part of this study, we perform a detailed analysis of the extent to which the triangular relation, a necessary condition for the existence of a material time, is satisfied. We find that, for all three properties, the best data collapse is obtained when each property is parameterized by its own material time. The degree of improvement varies considerably among the observables, however; it is most pronounced for the mean-square displacement.

</details>


### [111] [Fast temperature up steps as a test of the Tool-Narayanaswamy formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15988)
*Armand Rykner,Marceau Hénot,François Ladieu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过快速升温实验研究了玻璃形成液体TEAC的老化动力学，检验了Tool-Narayanaswamy (TN)形式主义的预测能力。结果表明，TN形式主义在小至中等温度步长（≤3.3 K）时预测与实验吻合良好，但较大步长下预测失败，暗示再平衡机制与平衡动力学脱钩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验Tool-Narayanaswamy (TN)形式主义对玻璃形成液体在非平衡老化过程中动力学行为的预测能力，特别是在不同振幅的温度突变条件下。

Method: 对玻璃形成液体triethyl-2-acetylcitrate (TEAC)施加0.3至13.6 K的快速升温步长，初始状态包括平衡态和通过预先降温实验制备的不同非平衡水平。利用小至中等振幅（≤3.3 K）步长下的降温老化实验确定TN参数，并借助玻璃转变温度以下的降温老化实验约束平衡弛豫时间的测定。

Result: 在距离平衡的虚温度差异高达10 K时，TN预测与实验吻合良好；但对于更大步长，预测逐渐无法捕捉老化动力学行为。这表明在大步长下再平衡机制与平衡动力学不再相关。

Conclusion: TN形式主义在小至中等振幅步长下有效，但存在适用范围上限。作者讨论了建立TN形式主义有效性普适判据的可能性，并与其他文献中的体系进行了比较。

Abstract: We investigated the aging dynamics of a glass-forming liquid triethyl-2-acetylcitrate (TEAC), following fast temperature up steps with amplitudes ranging from 0.3 to 13.6 K. The initial states were either at equilibrium or prepared at increasing levels of out-of-equilibrium through a prior down step experiment. Our goal was to test the predictive power of the Tool-Narayanaswamy (TN) formalism which assumes that the non-linear re-equilibration of a liquid can be linked to its linear response to a small perturbation. We determined the TN parameters for steps with small to moderate amplitude ($\leq$ 3.3 K) and crucially took advantage of down step aging experiments below the glass transition temperature to constrain the determination of the equilibrium relaxation time. We tested the TN predictions and found very good agreement for differences in fictive temperature characterizing the distance from equilibrium as high as 10 K. For larger steps, however, the prediction progressively fails to capture the aging dynamics. This likely indicates that the re-equilibration mechanism is no longer related to the equilibrium dynamics. Finally, we discuss the possibility of obtaining a general criterion for the limit of validity of the TN formalism, which we compare to other systems from the literature.

### [112] [Programmable transport of rotating particles in obstacle arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16091)
*Marcos Puerto,Alfredo Alexander-Katz,Juan L. Aragones,J. V. Alvarez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 旋转胶体（spinners）在障碍物阵列中表现出由惯性马格纳斯类升力（Magnus-like lift）与短程吸引力竞争所决定的频率设定稳态轨道和流。完全分辨的格子玻尔兹曼模拟揭示了水动力学耦合并识别了升力机制，而基于对称性的朗之万模型捕捉了由此产生的平衡。在周期晶格中，标量和矢量势的叠加产生两种稳健的轨道状态：角落态（corner states）和内态（inner states）。通过缓慢的频率调制可以在这些状态间切换，并产生定向、阶梯式的跨格输运。这建立了一种由单一驱动参数控制的最小水动力学机制，用于在结构化环境中对主动转子进行可编程引导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索旋转胶体在障碍物阵列中的轨道行为与输运机制，寻找一种由单一驱动参数控制、可通过水动力学效应实现可编程引导的最小物理机制。

Method: 采用完全分辨的格子玻尔兹曼模拟（lattice-Boltzmann simulation）揭示水动力学耦合并识别升力机制；同时构建基于对称性的朗之万模型（Langevin model）描述对称性平衡。

Result: 周期晶格中标量势和矢量势的叠加产生两种稳健的轨道状态：角落态（corner states，绕单个柱子轨道运动）和内态（inner states，跨越四个相邻障碍物的耦合轨道）。缓慢频率调制可实现状态切换并产生定向、阶梯式跨格输运。

Conclusion: 建立了一种由单一驱动参数控制的最小水动力学机制，能够在结构化环境中对主动转子进行可编程引导。

Abstract: Rotating colloids, or spinners, in obstacle arrays exhibit frequency-set stationary orbits and currents set by the competition between an inertial, Magnus-like lift and short-range attraction. Fully resolved lattice-Boltzmann simulations reveal the hydrodynamic coupling and identify the lift mechanism, while a symmetry-based Langevin model captures the resulting balance. In periodic lattices, the superposition of scalar and vector potentials produces two robust orbital regimes: corner states, in which spinners orbit individual posts, and inner states, in which orbits couple across four neighboring obstacles. Slow frequency modulation toggles these states and produces directed, stepwise transport across the grid. This establishes a minimal hydrodynamic mechanism, controlled by a single driving parameter, for programmable guidance of active rotors in structured environments.

### [113] [Absence of Spin-Glass Order on Migdal--Kadanoff Hierarchical Lattices near Three Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15676)
*Manaka Okuyama,Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文推导了对称二值耦合伊辛自旋玻璃（Ising spin glass）在具有偶数分支数的Migdal–Kadanoff（MK）层级晶格上不存在自旋玻璃序的严格充分条件。通过单个精确重整化群步骤以正概率产生零有效键，将问题简化为键渗流（bond percolation），当诱导的稀释超过渗流阈值时，所有温度下自旋玻璃序和刚性均消失。该条件严格证明了MK近似下平方晶格伊辛自旋玻璃不存在自旋玻璃相；进一步地，通过选择足够大的尺度因子和分支数，可以构造分形维数任意接近3但依然没有自旋玻璃序的MK层级晶格，这与小参数下约2.52的下临界维数（lower critical dimension）估计形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋玻璃的下临界维数（lower critical dimension）是统计力学中的核心问题，但严格结果稀缺。现有数值估计基于小尺度MK层级晶格给出下临界维数约为2.52，但缺乏严格的数学证明。

Method: 利用MK层级晶格上精确的重整化群（renormalization group）变换，证明单个RG步骤以正概率产生零有效键，从而将自旋玻璃问题映射为层级晶格上的键渗流（bond percolation）问题。

Result: 推导出不存在自旋玻璃序的严格充分条件：当诱导稀释超过渗流阈值时，自旋玻璃序和刚性在所有温度下（包括零温）均消失。该条件严格证明了MK近似下平方晶格无自旋玻璃相；通过选择足够大的尺度因子和分支数，可构造分形维数任意接近3但依然无自旋玻璃序的MK层级晶格。

Conclusion: 对于偶数分支数的MK层级晶格，自旋玻璃序的存在性可以通过渗流条件严格判定。这与小尺度参数下数值估计的下临界维数约2.52形成对比，表明MK近似中下临界维数可能依赖于尺度参数的具体选择。

Abstract: We derive a rigorous sufficient condition for the absence of spin-glass order in the Ising spin glass with symmetric binary couplings on Migdal--Kadanoff (MK) hierarchical lattices with even branching number. The key observation is that a single exact renormalization-group step creates zero effective bonds with positive probability, thereby reducing the problem to bond percolation on the corresponding hierarchical lattice. When the induced dilution exceeds the percolation threshold, both spin-glass order and stiffness are absent at all temperatures, including zero temperature. As a consequence, our criterion gives a rigorous proof that the Ising spin glass on the square lattice does not exhibit a spin-glass phase within the MK approximation. More unexpectedly, by choosing sufficiently large scale factors and branching numbers, we construct MK hierarchical lattices whose fractal dimensions are arbitrarily close to three from below but still exhibit no spin-glass order. This sharply contrasts with numerical estimates obtained for MK hierarchical lattices with relatively small scale factors and branching numbers, which placed the lower critical dimension near \(2.52\).

</details>


### [114] [A Flickering Resonance Degeneracy on Entropy-Ruled Charge Transport in the Extended Hopping Sites for Biological Systems: Role of Static-to-Dynamic Disorder Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15785)
*K. Navamani,M. Pavalamuthu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种闪烁共振耦合熵控电荷传输理论（flickering resonance-coupled entropy-ruled charge transport theory），用于计算生物分子在局域跳跃、离域能带输运及中间机制下的转移速率和扩散迁移率。该理论将动态无序（dynamic disorder）相关的简并性（degeneracy）纳入熵控电子转移速率与扩散-迁移率公式，发现超快动态及高简并条件下熵控迁移率转化为带迁移率（band mobility），而非热激活跳跃或扩散过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物分子中的电荷传输（charge transport, CT）在光生物学、生物能量学、氧化还原催化等过程中发挥关键作用，然而动态无序（dynamic disorder）对从小尺度到大尺度分子电导率的权重影响尚未明确，亟需一种能统一描述局域跳跃、离域能带及中间输运机制的理论框架。

Method: 提出闪烁共振耦合熵控电荷传输理论，通过纳入动态无序相关的简并性（以闪烁共振方式）来修正熵控电子转移速率与扩散迁移率（D/μ）的计算，使其同时适用于局域跳跃、离域能带输运及中间机制。

Result: 动力学驱动的电子位点匹配概率增强了简并性，该简并性由微分熵（differential entropy）量化。在超快动态和高简并条件下，熵控迁移率转化为带迁移率，而非热激活跳跃或扩散过程。

Conclusion: 所提理论为动态无序对生物分子电荷传输的影响提供了统一的定量描述，揭示了动态简并性在输运机制转变中的关键作用。

Abstract: Charge transport (CT) in biological systems is of great interest due to its role in various functional activities like photobiology, bioenergetics, redox catalytic and other metabolic activities, etc. It has been observed by various studies that the presence of a dynamic disorder in biomolecules facilitates charge dynamics in the intermediate transport regime, i.e., far from hopping and towards a bank-like mechanism. Hitherto, the dynamic disorder (in a time scale, coupling between electronic and nuclear dynamics) weightage on CT in molecules is not well-established for the measurement of molecular conductivity from small to long-range ordering. With this motivation, we propose the flickering resonance-coupled entropy-ruled charge transport theory for transfer-rate and diffusion-based mobility (D/μ) calculations. The proposed analytical formalism incorporates the impact of dynamic disorder-correlated degeneracy (in a flickering-resonance manner) on the entropy-ruled electron transfer rate and diffusion-mobility, which are valid for localized hopping, delocalized band transport, and regimes in between. By this approach, it has been observed that the dynamics-driven electronic site matching probability enhances the degeneracy, which is quantified by the differential entropy. The analysis clearly shows that for ultra-fast dynamical and degenerate cases, the entropy-ruled mobility is transformed as band mobility, rather than the thermally activated hopping or diffusion process.

</details>


### [115] [Quantum and classical entropic complexity of the thermal state: coherence, decoherence, and the ergodic-to-localized crossover in random-matrix and many-body models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15798)
*Imre Varga,Onur Aktan*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了热平均是否保留本征态复杂性（eigenstate complexity）的印记，通过对三种无序模型（Rosenzweig-Porter 系综、幂律带随机矩阵系综、随机场海森堡链）中熵复杂性（entropic complexity）C = S₁ - S₂ 的分析发现：热平均强烈抑制但未完全消除本征态复杂性信号；本征态复杂性在随机矩阵模型中产生明显的中间相峰值，而热态仅留下微弱（约10%）但可再现的“热影子”；两种特征分别由尺度不变的交叉指标追踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解热平均（thermal averaging）是否会破坏或保留本征态复杂性（eigenstate complexity）的印记，是连接量子多体系统的微观本征态结构与宏观热力学性质的核心问题。

Method: 定义熵复杂性 C = S₁ - S₂（香农熵减去二阶Rényi熵），将其区分为波函数层面量 C_eig 和热态（Gibbs state）的迹复杂性（trace complexity, C_tr）与对角复杂性（diagonal complexity, C_diag），并在三种无序模型（Rosenzweig-Porter 系综、幂律带随机矩阵系综、随机场海森堡链）中比较这些量在遍历-局域化交叉中的行为。

Result: 热平均强烈抑制但未完全消除本征态复杂性信号；C_eig 在RP和PLBRM模型中展现出显著的中相峰值，该峰值在热态对角复杂性中留下微弱（约10%）但可再现的“热影子”；本征态复杂性在海森堡链中则峰值位于多体局域化转变处。此外发现一个仅存在于热态的新特征——遍历相边缘，在PLBRM中随系统尺寸增大而退缩。两种特征分别由交叉温度的迹-对角对数比和相干相对熵（relative entropy of coherence）等尺度不变指标追踪。

Conclusion: 熵复杂性能够清晰区分热态物理与本征态物理：在波函数层面产生的尖锐特征，虽在不同随机矩阵模型中可再现，但在热观测量中仅留下微弱且结构上不同的印记。

Abstract: Does thermal averaging preserve signatures of eigenstate complexity? We study the entropic complexity C = S_1 - S_2 (Shannon minus second-order Renyi entropy) across the ergodic-to-localized crossover of three disordered models: the Rosenzweig-Porter (RP) ensemble, the power-law banded random matrix (PLBRM) ensemble, and the random-field Heisenberg chain. We compare a wavefunction-level quantity C_eig to the complexity of the thermal (Gibbs) state before and after pointer-basis dephasing, via the trace (C_tr) and diagonal (C_diag) complexities. The answer is mostly no: thermal averaging strongly suppresses, but does not eliminate, eigenstate-complexity signatures. C_eig develops a pronounced mid-phase maximum in RP and, at matching fractal dimension, in the structurally independent PLBRM model; a high-statistics scan resolves a weak (about 10%) but reproducible thermal shadow of this peak in the thermal diagonal complexity. This feature is confined to the two random-matrix models; in the Heisenberg chain the eigenstate complexity instead peaks at the many-body localization transition. A second, genuinely thermal feature, an edge just inside the ergodic phase, has no eigenstate counterpart and, in PLBRM, recedes with system size. Both features are tracked by scale-invariant crossover indicators: the log-ratio of the trace and diagonal crossover temperatures, which vanishes upon localization, and the relative entropy of coherence. Entropic complexity thus cleanly separates thermal-state and eigenstate physics: a sharp wavefunction-level feature, reproducible across unrelated random-matrix constructions, leaves only a faint, structurally distinct imprint on thermal observables.

</details>

### [116] [Tighter Dark Matter Constraints from the Projected Mass Method: A Neural Network Enhanced Method for Galaxy Groups and Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15339)
*Yinbo Huang,David Benisty*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于残差神经网络（residual neural network）修正经典投影质量估计器（Projected Mass Estimator, PME）的新框架，利用IllustrisTNG宇宙学模拟训练网络，显著降低银河系及邻近星系群总质量测量中的系统偏差和统计噪声，将质量估计的中位数偏差从约30%-46%修正至约2%，均方根误差（RMSE）从0.29-0.32 dex降至0.13 dex。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量银河系及邻近星系群的总质量极为困难，原因在于经典动力学估计器（dynamical estimators）严重依赖卫星轨道几何假设，而这些假设在实际中很少成立；同时，可用的运动学示踪天体（kinematic tracers）通常极少，导致传统方法存在显著系统偏差和大统计不确定性。

Method: 基于IllustrisTNG宇宙学模拟（cosmological simulation）中数千个模拟星系群的数据，训练残差神经网络来修正经典投影质量估计器（PME）；针对不同卫星样本规模（从5颗到50颗卫星）分别训练独立的网络，使修正过程自动计入小样本主导的统计噪声。

Result: 在模拟暗晕测试中，经典PME系统性地高估暗晕质量，中位数比例因子分别为1.30（使用二维距离）和1.46（使用三维距离），RMSE为0.29和0.32 dex；经神经网络修正后，中位数比例因子降至1.02，RMSE降至0.13 dex。应用于银河系，得到总质量为(M_MW = 1.144^{+0.399}_{-0.296}×10^{12} M_⊙)，其中基于最亮5-10颗卫星的估计值偏向稍低的范围（(0.8-0.95)×10^{12} M_⊙）。

Conclusion: 修正后的PME能够对星系群和星系团的维里质量（virial mass）及暗物质晕（dark matter halo）的预测给出更紧致的约束，显著提升了小样本条件下总质量测量的精度和可靠性。

Abstract: Measuring the total mass of the Milky Way and nearby galaxy groups is difficult because classical dynamical estimators rely on assumptions about satellite orbital geometry that are rarely satisfied in practice, and because only a handful of satellite galaxies are typically available as kinematic tracers. We present a new framework that corrects the well-known Projected Mass Estimator (PME) using a residual neural network trained on thousands of simulated galaxy groups from the IllustrisTNG cosmological simulation. Separate networks are trained for each satellite sample size, from as few as 5 satellites up to 50, so that the correction automatically accounts for the statistical noise that dominates when only a small number of tracers is available. In tests on simulated halos, the classical PME systematically overestimates halo masses by factors of $M_{\rm proj}/M_{\rm true} = 1.30^{+0.72}_{-0.62}$ (using the 2D distance) and $1.46^{+0.97}_{-0.72}$ (using the 3D distance), with RMSE of 0.29 and 0.32 dex respectively. The neural-network correction reduces this to $M_{\rm proj}/M_{\rm true} = 1.02^{+0.30}_{-0.26}$ with an RMSE of 0.13 dex. Applied to the Milky Way, the method yields a total mass of $M_{\rm MW} = 1.144^{+0.399}_{-0.296}\times10^{12}\,M_\odot$, with estimates based on the brightest 5-10 satellites favoring a somewhat lower range of $(0.8$-$0.95)\times10^{12}\,M_\odot$. The modified PME gives a tighter constraint on the virial masses and the dark matter rate prediction in galaxy groups and clusters.

### [117] [A Mesoscopic Ginzburg--Landau Model for Vibrational Strong Coupling Enhanced Rayleigh Scattering in Molecular Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15497)
*Wenxiang Ying,Abraham Nitzan*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于振动强耦合（VSC）分子液体中探测到的介观现象，构建了一个包含集体振动极化场 $P$ 和二次结构场 $m$ 的金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg–Landau）模型，成功解释了瑞利散射增强、浓度阈值及热塌缩等实验观测，并预言了长波长密度/介电关联增强、介观关联长度增大和结构动力学减缓等可检验效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sandeep 等人（2026）近期的实验表明，分子液体中的振动强耦合（vibrational strong coupling, VSC）能够产生超越单分子可观测量的介观现象，包括共振增强的瑞利散射、突变浓度阈值和热塌缩。现有理论无法充分解释这些介观行为，因此需要构建一个新的理论框架来理解腔调控下的集体效应。

Method: 构建了一个包含两个耦合场的介观金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg–Landau）模型：一个腔控集体振动极化场 $P$ 和一个次级结构场 $m$。$m$ 的长波长磁化率通过集体振动极化强度 $P^2$ 进行重整化（renormalized），这一机制被假设控制长波长密度/介电涨落。

Result: 在校准参数后，模型成功捕捉到观测的瑞利散射增强、集体标度关系（scaling relations）和阈值行为，并解释了为何当瑞利散射消失时极化激元/红外特征（polaritonic/IR signatures）仍可存在。模型进一步预言在瑞利散射增强的强耦合区域，会出现长波长密度/介电关联增强、介观关联长度增大以及结构动力学减缓。

Conclusion: 模型为振动强耦合（VSC）下的介观现象提供了统一的理论解释，并提出了可直接通过小角X射线/中子散射（small-angle X-ray/neutron scattering）和动态光散射（dynamic light-scattering）进行实验检验的预言。

Abstract: Recent experiments by Sandeep \textit{et al.} [Angew. Chem. Int. Ed. 65, e16917 (2026)] suggest that vibrational strong coupling (VSC) in molecular liquids can generate mesoscopic phenomena beyond single-molecule observables, including resonantly enhanced Rayleigh scattering, abrupt concentration thresholds, and thermal collapse. Motivated by these observations, we construct a mesoscopic Ginzburg--Landau model with two coupled fields: a cavity-controlled collective vibrational polarization $P$ and a secondary structural field $m$ whose long-wavelength susceptibility is renormalized by the collective vibrational polarization intensity $P^2$, assumed to govern long-wavelength density/dielectric fluctuations. With calibrated parameters, the model captures the observed Rayleigh enhancement, collective scaling relations, and threshold-like behavior, while explaining why polaritonic/IR signatures may persist when Rayleigh scattering disappears. The model further predicts enhanced long-wavelength density/dielectric correlations, enlarged mesoscopic correlation lengths, and slowed structural dynamics in the regime with strong Rayleigh enhancement, providing direct experimental tests through small-angle X-ray/neutron scattering and dynamic light-scattering probes.
